export class SwarmIntelligenceService {
  constructor(private readonly databaseService: DatabaseService) {}

  async analyzeFeedback(recitationData: any) {
    const { userId } = recitationData;
    const recitations = await this.databaseService.getRecitationFeedback(userId);
    if (recitations.length > 1) {
      return { swarmInsights: 'Progress improving based on historical trends' };
    }
    return { swarmInsights: 'More data needed for swarm insights' };
  }
}




12. websocket.service.ts (Batch-Style Real-Time Feedback)

Uses Socket.IO for real-time communication, enabling immediate emission of full-file results if desired.

// backend/src/recitation/websocket.service.ts
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { Server } from 'socket.io';

@Injectable()
export class WebsocketService {
  private server: Server;

  constructor() {
    this.server = new Server(3001, { cors: { origin: '*' } });
    this.server.on('connection', (socket) => {
      console.log('Client connected:', socket.id);
      socket.on('disconnect', () => console.log('Client disconnected:', socket.id));
      socket.on('joinRoom', (userId: string) => {
        socket.join(userId);
      });
    });
  }

  sendFeedback(socketId: string, feedback: any) {
    const socket = this.server.sockets.sockets.get(socketId);
    if (socket) {
      socket.emit('recitationFeedback', feedback);
    }
  }

  broadcastToUser(userId: string, feedback: any) {
    this.server.to(userId).emit('recitationFeedback', feedback);
  }
}


Batch Real-Time Flow:

Frontend calls /recitation/upload or /recitation/analyze with socketId and waits.

Once the batch pipeline completes, sendFeedback(socketId, result) or broadcastToUser(userId, result) pushes the full analysis back instantly.



13. recitation.gateway.ts (Streaming Gateway for True Real-Time AI Analysis)

Implements a Socket.IO Gateway that forwards incoming audio chunks to Google Cloud Speech’s streamingRecognize(), returns interim/final transcripts, and emits lightweight Tajweed/phoneme hints on the fly.

// backend/src/recitation/recitation.gateway.ts
import {
  WebSocketGateway,
  WebSocketServer,
  OnGatewayConnection,
  OnGatewayDisconnect,
  SubscribeMessage,
} from '@nestjs/websockets';
import { Server, Socket } from 'socket.io';
import { SpeechClient, StreamingRecognizeRequest } from '@google-cloud/speech';
import { TajweedFeedbackService } from './tajweed-feedback.service';
import { PhonemeFeedbackService } from './phoneme-feedback.service';
import { EmotionFeedbackService } from './emotion-feedback.service';
import { AIAgentService } from './ai-agent.service';

@WebSocketGateway(3002, { cors: { origin: '*' } })
export class RecitationGateway implements OnGatewayConnection, OnGatewayDisconnect {
  @WebSocketServer() server: Server;
  private speechClient = new SpeechClient();

  // Map of socket.id → streamingRecognize call (gRPC stream)
  private callStreams: Map<string, any> = new Map();

  constructor(
    private readonly tajweedService: TajweedFeedbackService,
    private readonly phonemeService: PhonemeFeedbackService,
    private readonly emotionService: EmotionFeedbackService,
    private readonly aiAgentService: AIAgentService,
  ) {}

  handleConnection(socket: Socket) {
    console.log(`Client connected (streaming): ${socket.id}`);

    // Create a streamingRecognize request for this socket
    const request: StreamingRecognizeRequest = {
      config: {
        encoding: 'WEBM_OPUS',          // Matches MediaRecorder settings
        sampleRateHertz: 48000,         // Default for webm/opus
        languageCode: 'ar-SA',
        enableWordTimeOffsets: true,
        interimResults: true,           // Receive partial transcripts
      },
      interimResults: true,
    };

    // Open gRPC streamingRecognize() call
    const call = this.speechClient
      .streamingRecognize(request)
      .on('error', (err) => {
        console.error('STT stream error:', err);
      })
      .on('data', async (data) => {
        // Emit interim/final transcript to the client immediately
        socket.emit('stt-transcript', data);

        // For each interim result, run lightweight Tajweed/Phoneme checks
        if (data.results && data.results[0].alternatives[0].transcript) {
          const interimText = data.results[0].alternatives[0].transcript;
          const isFinal = data.results[0].isFinal;

          // 1. Lightweight Phoneme hint (dummy, replace with real logic)
          const phonemeHint = await this.phonemeService.analyzePhonemes(interimText);
          socket.emit('phoneme-hint', { text: interimText, hint: phonemeHint, isFinal });

          // 2. Lightweight Tajweed hint (dummy)
          const tajweedHint = await this.tajweedService.analyzeTajweed(interimText);
          socket.emit('tajweed-hint', { text: interimText, hint: tajweedHint, isFinal });

          // 3. Periodic AI guidance (every few seconds or on final)
          if (isFinal) {
            const aiHint = await this.aiAgentService.provideGuidance({
              transcription: interimText,
            });
            socket.emit('ai-guidance', { text: interimText, guidance: aiHint });
          }

          // 4. Chunk-based emotion detection (every final chunk)
          if (isFinal) {
            const emotionHint = await this.emotionService.analyzeEmotion(interimText);
            socket.emit('emotion-hint', { text: interimText, emotion: emotionHint });
          }
        }
      });

    // Store call in map
    this.callStreams.set(socket.id, call);
  }

  @SubscribeMessage('audio-chunk')
  handleAudioChunk(socket: Socket, chunk: ArrayBuffer) {
    const call = this.callStreams.get(socket.id);
    if (!call) return;
    // Write raw chunk into gRPC stream
    call.write({ audioContent: chunk });
  }

  @SubscribeMessage('end-stream')
  handleEndStream(socket: Socket) {
    const call = this.callStreams.get(socket.id);
    if (call) {
      call.end();
      this.callStreams.delete(socket.id);
    }
    console.log(`Client ended stream: ${socket.id}`);
  }

  handleDisconnect(socket: Socket) {
    console.log(`Client disconnected (streaming): ${socket.id}`);
    const call = this.callStreams.get(socket.id);
    if (call) {
      call.end();
      this.callStreams.delete(socket.id);
    }
  }
}


Real-Time Streaming Flow

Client emits "audio-chunk" every ~250 ms with raw audio frames.

Gateway forwards each chunk to Google Cloud Speech’s streamingRecognize().

Google returns data events containing interim/final transcripts.

Gateway immediately emits:

"stt-transcript": partial/full transcript

"phoneme-hint" & "tajweed-hint": lightweight pronunciation hints

"ai-guidance": short GPT-4 suggestions (on final or per-sentence)

"emotion-hint": brief emotion summary (on final chunks)

Client displays these real-time hints as the user recites.



Frontend Components

The frontend is built with React and Vite, leveraging Redux Toolkit, TanStack Query, Material-UI, TailwindCSS, and Socket.IO for real-time features. Below are the key components for both batch and real-time analysis.



1. audioStreamer.ts (Audio Chunking Utility)

Sets up MediaRecorder in chunked mode (250 ms) to send to the streaming gateway.

// frontend-vite/src/utils/audioStreamer.ts
export function startStreaming(onChunk: (chunk: Blob) => void): Promise<MediaRecorder> {
  return navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true }).then((stream) => {
    const recorder = new MediaRecorder(stream, { mimeType: 'audio/webm;codecs=opus' });
    recorder.ondataavailable = (e) => {
      if (e.data.size > 0) onChunk(e.data);
    };
    recorder.start(250); // emit ~250 ms chunks
    return recorder;
  });
}




2. RecitationDashboard.tsx

Combined dashboard for recording, both batch upload and real-time streaming, and visualizing feedback.

// frontend-vite/src/components/RecitationDashboard.tsx
import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useMutation } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import axios from 'axios';
import { io, Socket } from 'socket.io-client';
import { startStreaming } from '../utils/audioStreamer';
import { Button, CircularProgress, Box, Typography, TextField } from '@mui/material';

const BATCH_SOCKET_URL = 'http://localhost:3001';   // Batch WebSocket
const STREAM_SOCKET_URL = 'http://localhost:3002';  // Streaming WebSocket

const batchSocket: Socket = io(BATCH_SOCKET_URL);
const streamSocket: Socket = io(STREAM_SOCKET_URL);

const RecitationDashboard: React.FC = () => {
  // Batch-mode feedback
  const [batchFeedback, setBatchFeedback] = useState({
    tajweed: '',
    phoneme: '',
    emotion: '',
    aiGuidance: '',
    swarm: '',
  });

  // Streaming-mode feedback
  const [streamFeedback, setStreamFeedback] = useState({
    transcript: '',
    interimPhoneme: '',
    interimTajweed: '',
    aiGuidance: '',
    emotion: '',
  });

  // Batch recording state
  const [isBatchRecording, setIsBatchRecording] = useState(false);
  const [batchAudioFile, setBatchAudioFile] = useState<File | null>(null);
  const [batchAudioURL, setBatchAudioURL] = useState<string>('');
  const [batchHistory, setBatchHistory] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const batchMediaRecorderRef = useRef<MediaRecorder | null>(null);
  const batchAudioChunksRef = useRef<Blob[]>([]);

  // Streaming recording state
  const [isStreaming, setIsStreaming] = useState(false);
  const [streamRecorder, setStreamRecorder] = useState<MediaRecorder | null>(null);

  // Simulated userId (replace with real auth)
  const [userId, setUserId] = useState<string>('user123');

  // Batch file upload + analysis mutation
  const { mutate: analyzeBatchRecitation, isLoading: isBatchLoading } = useMutation({
    mutationFn: (formData: FormData) =>
      axios.post('/api/recitation/upload', formData).then((res) => res.data),
    onSuccess: (data) => {
      setBatchFeedback({
        tajweed: data.tajweedFeedback,
        phoneme: data.phonemeFeedback,
        emotion: data.emotionFeedback,
        aiGuidance: data.aiGuidanceFeedback,
        swarm: data.swarmFeedback,
      });
      setBatchHistory((prev) => [
        ...prev,
        { file: batchAudioFile, feedback: data, url: batchAudioURL },
      ]);

      // Notify server to broadcast if desired
      batchSocket.emit('joinRoom', userId);
      batchSocket.emit('recitationFeedback', { socketId: batchSocket.id, ...data });
    },
  });

  // Listen for batch real-time feedback events
  useEffect(() => {
    batchSocket.on('recitationFeedback', (data: any) => {
      setBatchFeedback({
        tajweed: data.tajweedFeedback,
        phoneme: data.phonemeFeedback,
        emotion: data.emotionFeedback,
        aiGuidance: data.aiGuidanceFeedback,
        swarm: data.swarmFeedback,
      });
    });
    return () => {
      batchSocket.off('recitationFeedback');
    };
  }, []);

  // Listen for streaming feedback events
  useEffect(() => {
    streamSocket.on('stt-transcript', (data: any) => {
      const interim = data.results[0].alternatives[0].transcript;
      setStreamFeedback((prev) => ({ ...prev, transcript: interim }));
    });
    streamSocket.on('phoneme-hint', (hint: any) => {
      setStreamFeedback((prev) => ({ ...prev, interimPhoneme: hint.hint }));
    });
    streamSocket.on('tajweed-hint', (hint: any) => {
      setStreamFeedback((prev) => ({ ...prev, interimTajweed: hint.hint }));
    });
    streamSocket.on('ai-guidance', (guidance: any) => {
      setStreamFeedback((prev) => ({ ...prev, aiGuidance: guidance.guidance }));
    });
    streamSocket.on('emotion-hint', (emotion: any) => {
      setStreamFeedback((prev) => ({ ...prev, emotion: emotion.emotion }));
    });
    return () => {
      streamSocket.off('stt-transcript');
      streamSocket.off('phoneme-hint');
      streamSocket.off('tajweed-hint');
      streamSocket.off('ai-guidance');
      streamSocket.off('emotion-hint');
    };
  }, []);

  /*** Batch Recording Handlers ***/

  const startBatchRecording = async () => {
    const stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true });
    const recorder = new MediaRecorder(stream);
    batchMediaRecorderRef.current = recorder;
    recorder.ondataavailable = (event) => batchAudioChunksRef.current.push(event.data);
    recorder.onstop = () => {
      const audioBlob = new Blob(batchAudioChunksRef.current, { type: 'audio/wav' });
      const file = new File([audioBlob], `${userId}_${Date.now()}.wav`, {
        type: 'audio/wav',
      });
      setBatchAudioFile(file);
      setBatchAudioURL(URL.createObjectURL(audioBlob));
      batchAudioChunksRef.current = [];
    };
    recorder.start();
    setIsBatchRecording(true);
  };

  const stopBatchRecording = () => {
    batchMediaRecorderRef.current?.stop();
    setIsBatchRecording(false);
  };

  const analyzeBatch = () => {
    if (!batchAudioFile) return;
    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('file', batchAudioFile);
    analyzeBatchRecitation(formData);
  };

  /*** Streaming Recording Handlers ***/

  const startStreamingRecording = async () => {
    const recorder = await startStreaming(async (chunk: Blob) => {
      const arrayBuffer = await chunk.arrayBuffer();
      streamSocket.emit('audio-chunk', arrayBuffer);
    });
    setStreamRecorder(recorder);
    setIsStreaming(true);
    // Join a “room” by user ID so the gateway knows who to group
    streamSocket.emit('joinRoom', userId);
  };

  const stopStreamingRecording = () => {
    if (streamRecorder) {
      streamRecorder.stop();
      setIsStreaming(false);
      // Let the server know no more chunks will arrive
      streamSocket.emit('end-stream');
    }
  };

  return (
    <Box sx={{ p: 4 }}>
      <Typography variant="h4" gutterBottom>
        Recitation Dashboard
      </Typography>

      {/* User ID Input */}
      <Box sx={{ my: 1 }}>
        <TextField
          label="User ID"
          variant="outlined"
          value={userId}
          onChange={(e) => setUserId(e.target.value)}
        />
      </Box>

      {/* Batch Recording Section */}
      <Box sx={{ my: 3 }}>
        <Typography variant="h5">Batch Recording & Analysis</Typography>
        {!batchAudioURL && !isBatchRecording ? (
          <Button variant="contained" onClick={startBatchRecording}>
            Start Batch Recording
          </Button>
        ) : (
          <>
            {isBatchRecording ? (
              <Button variant="contained" color="error" onClick={stopBatchRecording}>
                Stop Recording
              </Button>
            ) : (
              <Box sx={{ mt: 1 }}>
                <audio controls src={batchAudioURL} />
                <Button
                  variant="contained"
                  sx={{ ml: 1 }}
                  onClick={analyzeBatch}
                  disabled={isBatchLoading}
                >
                  {isBatchLoading ? <CircularProgress size={24} /> : 'Analyze Batch Recitation'}
                </Button>
              </Box>
            )}
          </>
        )}
        {/* Batch Feedback Display */}
        <Box sx={{ mt: 2 }}>
          <Typography><strong>Tajweed (Batch):</strong> {batchFeedback.tajweed}</Typography>
          <Typography><strong>Phoneme (Batch):</strong> {batchFeedback.phoneme}</Typography>
          <Typography><strong>Emotion (Batch):</strong> {batchFeedback.emotion}</Typography>
          <Typography><strong>AI Guidance (Batch):</strong> {batchFeedback.aiGuidance}</Typography>
          <Typography><strong>Swarm Insights (Batch):</strong> {batchFeedback.swarm}</Typography>
        </Box>
      </Box>

      {/* Batch History Section */}
      <Box sx={{ my: 3 }}>
        <Typography variant="h6">Batch Recitation History</Typography>
        {batchHistory.map((rec, idx) => (
          <Button
            key={idx}
            sx={{ mr: 1, mt: 1 }}
            onClick={() => setBatchAudioURL(rec.url)}
          >
            Recitation {idx + 1}
          </Button>
        ))}
      </Box>

      <hr />

      {/* Streaming Recording Section */}
      <Box sx={{ my: 3 }}>
        <Typography variant="h5">Real-Time (Streaming) Recitation</Typography>
        {!isStreaming ? (
          <Button variant="contained" onClick={startStreamingRecording}>
            Start Real-Time Recitation
          </Button>
        ) : (
          <Button variant="contained" color="error" onClick={stopStreamingRecording}>
            Stop Real-Time Recitation
          </Button>
        )}
        {isStreaming && (
          <Typography sx={{ mt: 1 }}>
            Streaming: your mic is live… (check console for interim feedback)
          </Typography>
        )}
        {/* Streaming Feedback Display */}
        <Box sx={{ mt: 2 }}>
          <Typography>
            <strong>Interim Transcript:</strong> {streamFeedback.transcript}
          </Typography>
          <Typography>
            <strong>Phoneme Hint:</strong> {streamFeedback.interimPhoneme}
          </Typography>
          <Typography>
            <strong>Tajweed Hint:</strong> {streamFeedback.interimTajweed}
          </Typography>
          <Typography>
            <strong>AI Guidance:</strong> {streamFeedback.aiGuidance}
          </Typography>
          <Typography>
            <strong>Emotion:</strong> {streamFeedback.emotion}
          </Typography>
        </Box>
      </Box>
    </Box>
  );
};

export default RecitationDashboard;


How This Works

Batch Recording & Analysis

User records a full recitation, then clicks Analyze Batch Recitation.

The file uploads to /api/recitation/upload, triggering the batch pipeline (transcription, Tajweed/phoneme/emotion/AI guidance/swarm).

Once complete, the backend pushes results via Socket.IO on http://localhost:3001, updating Batch Feedback.

Real-Time (Streaming) Recitation

User clicks Start Real-Time Recitation. The app calls startStreaming(), which captures ~250 ms audio chunks and emits each via Socket.IO to http://localhost:3002.

The RecitationGateway forwards each chunk into Google Cloud Speech’s streamingRecognize(). As interim/final transcripts arrive, the gateway emits:
 • "stt-transcript" (partial/final transcript)
 • "phoneme-hint" & "tajweed-hint" (lightweight hints on pronunciation)
 • "ai-guidance" (short GPT-4 suggestions on final chunks)
 • "emotion-hint" (brief emotion summary on final chunks)

The client listens and updates Streaming Feedback live.

When the user clicks Stop Real-Time Recitation, the client emits "end-stream", prompting the gateway to close the gRPC stream and finalize any pending processing.



Integration with Existing Structure

Main Components

Backend (/backend)

Built with NestJS, extended with:

 • RecitationController, RecitationService, etc. for batch processing.

 • RecitationGateway for streaming.

Uses TypeORM (MySQL) for user data, Mongoose (MongoDB) for recitation documents.

Integrates with Google Cloud Speech (batch & streaming), OpenAI (GPT-4), Hume AI (emotion), and placeholder phoneme/Tajweed APIs.

Employs Socket.IO on port 3001 (batch feedback) and port 3002 (streaming).

Frontend (/frontend-vite)

Built with React and Vite, enhanced with:

 • RecitationDashboard.tsx supporting batch & streaming.

 • audioStreamer.ts utility for chunked capture.

 • Two Socket.IO clients:

 – io('http://localhost:3001') for batch events;

 – io('http://localhost:3002') for streaming.

Uses Redux Toolkit or local state for history; TanStack Query for batch HTTP calls.

UI styled with Material-UI and TailwindCSS for responsiveness.

Summary

Phase 4 delivers a comprehensive recitation analysis system with dual modes:

Batch-Style Analysis: Users record a full recitation, then upload it. The backend runs transcription, Tajweed/phoneme/emotion/AI guidance/swarm, stores results, and—if a socketId is provided—pushes feedback via Socket.IO.

True Real-Time Analysis: As users recite, ~250 ms audio chunks stream to Google Cloud Speech’s streamingRecognize(). Interim transcripts and lightweight pronunciation hints (Tajweed/phoneme) appear instantly. Periodic AI guidance and emotion hints are also delivered on the fly. When the user stops, the final transcript can be saved and passed through the batch pipeline for full feedback and visualization.

This phase leverages existing NestJS, Mongoose, TypeORM, and React/Vite infrastructure, introducing a second Socket.IO gateway for streaming. Learners benefit from immediate, actionable feedback during practice while still having the depth of batch analysis for later review.



Transition to Phase 5

With the recitation feedback system established—offering both batch and real-time modes—Phase 5 will introduce Competitions, adding gamification elements such as leaderboards, recitation challenges, and community events to further motivate learners.





Phase 5: Competitions



Introductory Overview

Phase 5 enhances the Quran Education AI Platform by adding a dynamic competition layer. Users can engage in recitation challenges, track their rankings on real-time leaderboards, earn achievements, and compete against peers matched by skill level. The system leverages AI-driven recitation evaluation, performance analytics, and event scheduling to ensure fairness and provide actionable insights into participants' progress.



Objectives

Recitation Challenges: Enable users to record and submit recitations for timed or themed challenges.

Leaderboards: Display real-time rankings based on recitation scores.

Achievements: Award badges or trophies for milestones (e.g., “First Challenge,” “Top 10 Finish”).

Skill Matchmaking: Pair users with similar recitation skills using AI for competitive fairness.

Competition Analytics: Provide insights into user and overall competition performance (e.g., accuracy, timing, emotion).

Event Scheduling: Allow creation and management of recitation events with defined start and end dates.

Database Setup

MySQL (via TypeORM)

Purpose: Stores core user records, authentication data, and transactional data (e.g., entry fees).

Configuration: Managed in config/.env (e.g., DB_HOST, DB_PORT, DB_USERNAME, DB_PASSWORD, DB_DATABASE).

Synchronization: Set DB_SYNC=false in production to prevent automatic schema changes.

MongoDB (via Mongoose)

Purpose: Stores competition documents, recitation submissions, leaderboards, and achievements.

Configuration: Connection URI in config/.env (e.g., MONGODB_URI).

Synchronization: Mongoose schemas evolve via code migrations or versioning (no DB_SYNC equivalent).



Backend Implementation

Models

1. User Model

backend/src/models/userModel.ts

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface IUser extends Document {
  name: string;
  email: string;
  password: string;
  score: number;          // Cumulative or latest competition score
  achievements: string[]; // Array of badge IDs or names
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

const userSchema = new Schema<IUser>(
  {
    name: { type: String, required: true },
    email: { type: String, required: true, unique: true },
    password: { type: String, required: true },
    score: { type: Number, default: 0 },
    achievements: { type: [String], default: [] },
  },
  { timestamps: true }
);

export const User = model<IUser>('User', userSchema);


2. Competition Model

backend/src/models/competitionModel.ts

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface ICompetition extends Document {
  name: string;
  description: string;
  startDate: Date;
  endDate: Date;
  participants: string[]; // Array of userIds
  challenges: string[];   // Array of challenge IDs or names
  results: { userId: string; score: number; rank: number }[];
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

const competitionSchema = new Schema<ICompetition>(
  {
    name: { type: String, required: true },
    description: { type: String, required: true },
    startDate: { type: Date, required: true },
    endDate: { type: Date, required: true },
    participants: { type: [String], default: [] },
    challenges: { type: [String], default: [] },
    results: {
      type: [
        {
          userId: { type: String, required: true },
          score: { type: Number, required: true },
          rank: { type: Number, required: true },
        },
      ],
      default: [],
    },
  },
  { timestamps: true }
);

export const Competition = model<ICompetition>('Competition', competitionSchema);




Services

A. RecitationEvaluationAPI (AI-Powered Scoring & Feedback)

backend/src/services/aiAPI.ts

import axios from 'axios';

export class RecitationEvaluationAPI {
  static async evaluate(audioFilePath: string): Promise<{ score: number; feedback: string }> {
    try {
      // 1. Send audio to Google Cloud Speech for transcription
      const audioData = {
        audio: { uri: audioFilePath },
        config: {
          encoding: 'LINEAR16',
          sampleRateHertz: 16000,
          languageCode: 'ar-SA',
        },
      };

      const response = await axios.post(
        'https://speech.googleapis.com/v1/speech:recognize',
        audioData,
        { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.GOOGLE_CLOUD_API_KEY}` } }
      );

      const transcript = response.data.results[0].alternatives[0].transcript;

      // 2. Compute component scores
      const score = this.calculateRecitationScore(transcript, audioFilePath);
      const feedback = this.generateFeedback(transcript, score);

      return { score, feedback };
    } catch (error: any) {
      throw new Error('Error evaluating recitation: ' + error.message);
    }
  }

  static calculateRecitationScore(transcript: string, audioFilePath: string): number {
    const pronunciationScore = this.evaluatePronunciation(audioFilePath);
    const timingScore = this.evaluateTiming(audioFilePath);
    const rhythmScore = this.evaluateRhythm(audioFilePath);
    const emotionalToneScore = this.evaluateEmotionalTone(transcript);

    const finalScore = (pronunciationScore + timingScore + rhythmScore + emotionalToneScore) / 4;
    return Math.min(Math.round(finalScore), 100);
  }

  static evaluatePronunciation(audioFilePath: string): number {
    // Placeholder for an external phoneme accuracy API
    return 90;
  }

  static evaluateTiming(audioFilePath: string): number {
    const idealPacing = 100;
    const actualPacing = 95; // Placeholder from audio analysis
    return Math.max(0, 100 - Math.abs(idealPacing - actualPacing));
  }

  static evaluateRhythm(audioFilePath: string): number {
    // Placeholder for a rhythm analysis algorithm
    return 85;
  }

  static evaluateEmotionalTone(transcript: string): number {
    // Call Google Natural Language for sentiment
    const sentiment = this.analyzeSentiment(transcript);
    return sentiment === 'Positive' ? 90 : sentiment === 'Negative' ? 70 : 80;
  }

  static generateFeedback(transcript: string, score: number): string {
    return `
      Transcript: ${transcript}
      Total Score: ${score}
      Feedback:
      - Pronunciation: Good clarity; focus on challenging letters.
      - Timing: Well-paced; maintain consistent pauses.
      - Rhythm: Smooth flow, though some syllables were rushed.
      - Emotional Tone: Positive tone detected; keep expressing conviction.
    `;
  }

  static async analyzeSentiment(text: string): Promise<string> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(
        'https://language.googleapis.com/v1/documents:analyzeSentiment',
        { document: { type: 'PLAIN_TEXT', content: text } },
        { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.GOOGLE_CLOUD_API_KEY}` } }
      );
      const sentimentScore = response.data.documentSentiment.score;
      if (sentimentScore > 0.1) return 'Positive';
      if (sentimentScore < -0.1) return 'Negative';
      return 'Neutral';
    } catch (error: any) {
      throw new Error('Error analyzing sentiment: ' + error.message);
    }
  }

  // AI-powered matchmaking: returns a matched user profile based on recitation skill
  static async getMatchmaking(userId: string): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(
        'http://localhost:3000/api/competition/matchmaking',
        { userId }
      );
      return response.data;
    } catch (error: any) {
      throw new Error('Error fetching matchmaking data: ' + error.message);
    }
  }

  // AI-powered leaderboard retrieval
  static async getLeaderboard(competitionId: string): Promise<any[]> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.get(
        `http://localhost:3000/api/competition/leaderboard/${competitionId}`
      );
      return response.data;
    } catch (error: any) {
      throw new Error('Error fetching leaderboard data: ' + error.message);
    }
  }
}


B. CompetitionService

backend/src/services/competitionService.ts

import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { Competition } from '../models/competitionModel';
import { User } from '../models/userModel';
import { RecitationEvaluationAPI } from './aiAPI';

@Injectable()
export class CompetitionService {
  // Create a new competition/event
  async createCompetition(competitionData: Partial<Competition>): Promise<Competition> {
    const competition = new Competition(competitionData);
    return competition.save();
  }

  // Register a user as a participant
  async registerParticipant(competitionId: string, userId: string) {
    const competition = await Competition.findById(competitionId);
    if (!competition) throw new Error('Competition not found');
    if (!competition.participants.includes(userId)) {
      competition.participants.push(userId);
      await competition.save();
    }
    return competition;
  }

  // Evaluate a recitation challenge submission
  async evaluateChallenge(
    competitionId: string,
    userId: string,
    audioFilePath: string
  ): Promise<{ score: number; feedback: string }> {
    const competition = await Competition.findById(competitionId);
    if (!competition) throw new Error('Competition not found');

    // AI-powered scoring and feedback
    const { score, feedback } = await RecitationEvaluationAPI.evaluate(audioFilePath);

    // Update competition results
    competition.results.push({ userId, score, rank: 0 });
    competition.results.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);
    competition.results.forEach((r, idx) => (r.rank = idx + 1));
    await competition.save();

    // Update user’s cumulative score and achievements
    const user = await User.findById(userId);
    if (user) {
      user.score = Math.max(user.score, score);
      // Award “Champion” badge if top
      if (competition.results[0].userId === userId && competition.results[0].rank === 1) {
        if (!user.achievements.includes('Champion')) {
          user.achievements.push('Champion');
        }
      }
      await user.save();
    }

    return { score, feedback };
  }

  // Retrieve the current leaderboard for a competition
  async getLeaderboard(competitionId: string): Promise<
    { userId: string; score: number; rank: number }[]
  > {
    const competition = await Competition.findById(competitionId);
    if (!competition) throw new Error('Competition not found');
    return [...competition.results].sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);
  }

  // AI-powered matchmaking
  async getMatchmaking(userId: string): Promise<any> {
    return RecitationEvaluationAPI.getMatchmaking(userId);
  }

  // List upcoming competitions (startDate ≥ now)
  async getUpcomingEvents(): Promise<Competition[]> {
    return Competition.find({ startDate: { $gte: new Date() } })
      .sort({ startDate: 1 })
      .exec();
  }
}




Routes

All routes are mounted under /api/competition in backend/src/routes/competitionRoutes.ts.

import { Router } from 'express';
import { CompetitionService } from '../services/competitionService';
import * as multer from 'multer';

const router = Router();
const competitionService = new CompetitionService();
const upload = multer({ dest: 'uploads/' });

// 1. Create a new competition/event
router.post('/create', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const competitionData = req.body; // { name, description, startDate, endDate, challenges }
    const competition = await competitionService.createCompetition(competitionData);
    res.json({ success: true, competition });
  } catch (error: any) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
});

// 2. Register a participant
router.post('/register/:competitionId/:userId', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { competitionId, userId } = req.params;
    const competition = await competitionService.registerParticipant(competitionId, userId);
    res.json({ success: true, competition });
  } catch (error: any) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
});

// 3. Submit a recitation challenge (file upload + evaluation)
router.post(
  '/challenge/:competitionId/:userId',
  upload.single('audio'),
  async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const { competitionId, userId } = req.params;
      const audioFilePath = (req.file as Express.Multer.File).path;
      const evaluation = await competitionService.evaluateChallenge(
        competitionId,
        userId,
        audioFilePath
      );
      res.json({ success: true, evaluation });
    } catch (error: any) {
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
    }
  }
);

// 4. Fetch leaderboard
router.get('/leaderboard/:competitionId', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { competitionId } = req.params;
    const leaderboard = await competitionService.getLeaderboard(competitionId);
    res.json({ success: true, leaderboard });
  } catch (error: any) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
});

// 5. AI-powered matchmaking
router.post('/matchmaking', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { userId } = req.body;
    const matchData = await competitionService.getMatchmaking(userId);
    res.json({ success: true, match: matchData });
  } catch (error: any) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
});

// 6. List upcoming competitions
router.get('/upcoming', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const upcomingEvents = await competitionService.getUpcomingEvents();
    res.json({ success: true, upcomingEvents });
  } catch (error: any) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
});

export default router;




Frontend Implementation

Below are the main React components that interact with the backend endpoints. Each uses fetch (or can be swapped to TanStack Query) and Material-UI for styling.



1. RecitationChallenge.tsx

Allows a user to record and submit a recitation as part of a competition.

// frontend-vite/src/components/RecitationChallenge.tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import RecitationPlayer from './RecitationPlayer'; // Existing component for recording/analysis
import { Button, Typography } from '@mui/material';

interface RecitationChallengeProps {
  competitionId: string;
  userId: string;
}

const RecitationChallenge: React.FC<RecitationChallengeProps> = ({
  competitionId,
  userId,
}) => {
  const [isSubmitted, setIsSubmitted] = useState(false);
  const [resultMessage, setResultMessage] = useState<string>('');

  // Callback invoked by RecitationPlayer after local analysis
  const handleRecitationSubmit = async (
    score: number,
    feedback: string,
    audioBlob: Blob
  ) => {
    try {
      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append('audio', audioBlob, `${userId}_${Date.now()}.wav`);

      const response = await fetch(
        `/api/competition/challenge/${competitionId}/${userId}`,
        {
          method: 'POST',
          body: formData,
        }
      );
      const data = await response.json();
      if (data.success) {
        setIsSubmitted(true);
        setResultMessage(
          `Submitted! Score: ${data.evaluation.score}. Feedback received.`
        );
      } else {
        setResultMessage('Submission failed. Try again.');
      }
    } catch (err) {
      setResultMessage('Error submitting recitation. Try again later.');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <Typography variant="h5" gutterBottom>
        Recitation Challenge
      </Typography>
      {!isSubmitted ? (
        <RecitationPlayer
          competitionId={competitionId}
          userId={userId}
          onRecitationSubmit={handleRecitationSubmit}
        />
      ) : (
        <Typography color="success.main">{resultMessage}</Typography>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default RecitationChallenge;


Notes

RecitationPlayer must accept competitionId, userId, and a callback onRecitationSubmit(score, feedback, audioBlob). After recording, it analyzes locally (or streams) and passes the final Blob to this callback.

Backend route expects a multipart field named audio.



2. SkillMatchmaking.tsx

Contacts the backend AI to find a matched opponent based on skill.

// frontend-vite/src/components/SkillMatchmaking.tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Button, Typography, CircularProgress, Box } from '@mui/material';

const SkillMatchmaking: React.FC = () => {
  const [matchedUser, setMatchedUser] = useState<any>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const handleMatchmaking = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);

    try {
      const response = await fetch('/api/competition/matchmaking', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ userId: localStorage.getItem('userId') }),
      });
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Network error');
      const data = await response.json();
      setMatchedUser(data.match);
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Error during matchmaking. Please try again.');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <Button variant="contained" onClick={handleMatchmaking} disabled={loading}>
        {loading ? <CircularProgress size={20} /> : 'Find Your Match'}
      </Button>
      {error && <Typography color="error">{error}</Typography>}
      {matchedUser && (
        <Box mt={2}>
          <Typography>
            Matched with <strong>{matchedUser.name}</strong> (Skill Level: {matchedUser.skillLevel})
          </Typography>
          <Typography>Performance Summary: {matchedUser.performanceSummary}</Typography>
        </Box>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default SkillMatchmaking;


Notes

Backend route /api/competition/matchmaking returns { match: { userId, name, skillLevel, performanceSummary } }.

userId is read from localStorage (could also come from Redux or context).



3. Leaderboards.tsx

Fetches and displays the current competition leaderboard, enriched with AI-computed metrics.

// frontend-vite/src/components/Leaderboards.tsx
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Typography, List, ListItem, ListItemText, CircularProgress } from '@mui/material';

interface LeaderboardEntry {
  userId: string;
  score: number;
  rank: number;
  improvementRate: number;  // AI-computed % improvement
  consistencyRate: number;  // % consistency in past scores
  emotionalTone: string;
}

interface LeaderboardsProps {
  competitionId: string;
}

const Leaderboards: React.FC<LeaderboardsProps> = ({ competitionId }) => {
  const [leaderboard, setLeaderboard] = useState<LeaderboardEntry[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchLeaderboard = async () => {
      setLoading(true);
      setError(null);
      try {
        const response = await fetch(`/api/competition/leaderboard/${competitionId}`);
        if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Network error');
        const data = await response.json(); // { success: true, leaderboard: [...] }
        // Enrich with placeholder AI metrics (in production, backend can supply these directly)
        const enriched: LeaderboardEntry[] = data.leaderboard.map((entry: any) => ({
          userId: entry.userId,
          score: entry.score,
          rank: entry.rank,
          improvementRate: Math.round(Math.random() * 20),       // Placeholder
          consistencyRate: Math.round(Math.random() * 20 + 80),   // Placeholder
          emotionalTone: ['Positive', 'Neutral', 'Negative'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)], // Placeholder
        }));
        setLeaderboard(enriched);
      } catch (err) {
        setError('Error fetching leaderboard. Please try again later.');
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    fetchLeaderboard();
  }, [competitionId]);

  if (loading) return <CircularProgress />;
  if (error) return <Typography color="error">{error}</Typography>;
  if (leaderboard.length === 0) return <Typography>No leaderboard data available yet.</Typography>;

  return (
    <div>
      <Typography variant="h5" gutterBottom>
        Leaderboard
      </Typography>
      <List>
        {leaderboard.map((entry) => (
          <ListItem key={entry.userId}>
            <ListItemText
              primary={`${entry.rank}. ${entry.userId} — ${entry.score} pts`}
              secondary={
                <Typography variant="body2">
                  Improvement: {entry.improvementRate}% | Consistency: {entry.consistencyRate}% | Emotional Tone: {entry.emotionalTone}
                </Typography>
              }
            />
          </ListItem>
        ))}
      </List>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Leaderboards;


Notes

Backend endpoint returns { success: true, leaderboard: [ { userId, score, rank } ] }.

For demonstration, AI metrics are randomly generated. In production, have the backend compute and return improvementRate, consistencyRate, emotionalTone.



4. Achievements.tsx

Displays the badges or achievements a user has unlocked.

// frontend-vite/src/components/Achievements.tsx
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Typography, List, ListItem, Avatar, Box } from '@mui/material';

interface Achievement {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  iconUrl: string;
  description: string;
  dateUnlocked: string;
}

interface AchievementsProps {
  userId: string;
}

const Achievements: React.FC<AchievementsProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [achievements, setAchievements] = useState<Achievement[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchAchievements = async () => {
      const response = await fetch(`/api/user/achievements/${userId}`);
      if (response.ok) {
        const data = await response.json(); // { achievements: [ ... ] }
        setAchievements(data.achievements);
      }
    };
    fetchAchievements();
  }, [userId]);

  if (achievements.length === 0) {
    return <Typography>No achievements unlocked yet.</Typography>;
  }

  return (
    <div>
      <Typography variant="h5" gutterBottom>
        Your Achievements
      </Typography>
      <List>
        {achievements.map((ach) => (
          <ListItem key={ach.id}>
            <Avatar src={ach.iconUrl} alt={ach.name} />
            <Box ml={2}>
              <Typography>{ach.name}</Typography>
              <Typography variant="body2" color="textSecondary">
                {ach.description} • Unlocked on{' '}
                {new Date(ach.dateUnlocked).toLocaleDateString()}
              </Typography>
            </Box>
          </ListItem>
        ))}
      </List>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Achievements;


Notes

Backend route /api/user/achievements/:userId returns { achievements: [ { id, name, iconUrl, description, dateUnlocked } ] }.

Achievements could include “First Challenge Completed,” “Top 10 Finish,” “Champion,” or “Consistency Master” (e.g., 5 straight challenges).



5. EventScheduler.tsx

Allows authorized users (e.g., admins) to create new competition events.

// frontend-vite/src/components/EventScheduler.tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { TextField, Button, Box, Typography } from '@mui/material';

interface EventSchedulerProps {
  onEventCreated?: (event: any) => void;
}

const EventScheduler: React.FC<EventSchedulerProps> = ({ onEventCreated }) => {
  const [eventDetails, setEventDetails] = useState({
    name: '',
    description: '',
    startDate: '',
    endDate: '',
  });
  const [message, setMessage] = useState<string>('');

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    try {
      const response = await fetch('/api/competition/create', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(eventDetails),
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      if (data.success) {
        setMessage('Event created successfully!');
        if (onEventCreated) onEventCreated(data.competition);
      } else {
        setMessage('Failed to create event.');
      }
    } catch (err) {
      setMessage('Error creating event. Try again later.');
    }
  };

  return (
    <Box
      component="form"
      onSubmit={handleSubmit}
      sx={{ maxWidth: 400, mx: 'auto', mt: 2 }}
    >
      <Typography variant="h5" gutterBottom>
        Create New Competition
      </Typography>
      <TextField
        fullWidth
        required
        label="Name"
        margin="normal"
        value={eventDetails.name}
        onChange={(e) => setEventDetails({ ...eventDetails, name: e.target.value })}
      />
      <TextField
        fullWidth
        required
        label="Description"
        multiline
        rows={3}
        margin="normal"
        value={eventDetails.description}
        onChange={(e) =>
          setEventDetails({ ...eventDetails, description: e.target.value })
        }
      />
      <TextField
        fullWidth
        required
        type="datetime-local"
        label="Start Date"
        InputLabelProps={{ shrink: true }}
        margin="normal"
        value={eventDetails.startDate}
        onChange={(e) =>
          setEventDetails({ ...eventDetails, startDate: e.target.value })
        }
      />
      <TextField
        fullWidth
        required
        type="datetime-local"
        label="End Date"
        InputLabelProps={{ shrink: true }}
        margin="normal"
        value={eventDetails.endDate}
        onChange={(e) =>
          setEventDetails({ ...eventDetails, endDate: e.target.value })
        }
      />
      <Button type="submit" variant="contained" sx={{ mt: 2 }}>
        Create Event
      </Button>
      {message && (
        <Typography variant="body2" color="success.main" sx={{ mt: 1 }}>
          {message}
        </Typography>
      )}
    </Box>
  );
};

export default EventScheduler;




Integration Details

Backend Integration

Models

User and Competition are defined under backend/src/models/.

Services

RecitationEvaluationAPI in backend/src/services/aiAPI.ts handles AI-driven scoring, sentiment analysis, matchmaking, and leaderboard retrieval.

CompetitionService in backend/src/services/competitionService.ts manages competition creation, registration, scoring, leaderboard, matchmaking, and upcoming events.

Routes

All competition routes are in backend/src/routes/competitionRoutes.ts and mounted via

// in backend/src/app.module.ts or main.ts
app.use('/api/competition', competitionRoutes);


Ensure MONGODB_URI and GOOGLE_CLOUD_API_KEY are set in config/.env.

TypeORM is configured (in app.module.ts) for MySQL to handle user authentication.

Apply Passport-JWT guards to protect certain routes (e.g., creating events or submitting recitations).

Startup

On NestJS bootstrap, connect to both MongoDB and MySQL.

Use @nestjs/config to load environment variables.

Protected routes (e.g., event creation) require valid JWT.

Frontend Integration

Routes & Components

/competition/create → renders EventScheduler

/competition/:id/challenge → renders RecitationChallenge

/competition/:id/leaderboard → renders Leaderboards

/competition/matchmaking → renders SkillMatchmaking

/user/:id/achievements → renders Achievements

State & Data Fetching

Use TanStack Query or plain fetch for GET/POST requests.

Store authenticated userId in Redux or localStorage (read by components).

Styling

Material-UI for consistent theming and responsive layout.

TailwindCSS utility classes for quick styling.

Styled Components can wrap custom styles if needed.

Real-Time Updates (Optional)

If real-time leaderboard updates are desired, integrate Socket.IO on the backend to emit "leaderboardUpdated" whenever Competition.results changes.

Frontend can listen:

import { io } from 'socket.io-client';
const socket = io('http://localhost:3001');

useEffect(() => {
  socket.on('leaderboardUpdated', (competitionId) => {
    if (competitionId === currentCompetitionId) {
      refetchLeaderboard();
    }
  });
  return () => {
    socket.off('leaderboardUpdated');
  };
}, [currentCompetitionId]);


Database Roles

MySQL (TypeORM)

Stores user credentials, JWT tokens, roles/permissions, and any transactional data (e.g., entry fees).

MongoDB (Mongoose)

Stores Competition documents (with participants, challenges, results).

Stores User achievements and cumulative scores.



Summary

Phase 5 delivers a robust competition system:

Backend

New Mongoose models: User (with score, achievements) and Competition (with participants, challenges, results).

RecitationEvaluationAPI service for AI-driven recitation scoring, sentiment analysis, matchmaking, and leaderboard retrieval.

CompetitionService orchestrating competition creation, registration, recitation evaluation, leaderboards, matchmaking, and upcoming events.

Express routes under /api/competition handling creation, registration, challenge submission, leaderboard fetching, matchmaking, and event listing.

Frontend

React components to manage every aspect of competition:

RecitationChallenge (record & submit recitation)

SkillMatchmaking (AI-based opponent pairing)

Leaderboards (real-time ranking with AI metrics)

Achievements (display badges)

EventScheduler (create new competitions)

Features

Recitation Challenges: Users record and submit audio; AI evaluates pronunciation, timing, rhythm, and emotion.

Leaderboards: Computed and enriched with AI-computed improvement and consistency rates.

Achievements: Earn badges based on milestones (first submission, top rank, consistency).

Skill Matchmaking: AI pairs users of comparable skill for fair head-to-head challenges.

Competition Analytics: Backend aggregates user performance over time.

Event Scheduling: Admins create upcoming events with clear start/end times.

This phase integrates seamlessly with the existing NestJS + TypeORM + Mongoose infrastructure and the React + Vite frontend, fostering an engaging, competitive environment that motivates learners to continuously improve their Quranic recitation skills.





Phase 6: Memorisation



Introductory Overview

In Phase 6, the Quran Education AI Platform enhances Quran memorization by leveraging AI to improve retention and provide personalized learning experiences. Key features include adaptive spaced repetition, AI-powered memory coaching, error tracking, scheduled reviews, and progress tracking. The platform aims to boost engagement and retention through tailored guidance, real-time feedback, and visual analytics.



Objectives

Adaptive Spaced Repetition
 Dynamically generate and adjust review schedules based on each user’s performance and forgetting curve.

AI-Powered Memory Coaching
 Deliver personalized feedback and advice—via OpenAI’s GPT-4—on how to improve memorization and recall.

Error Tracking
 Monitor and analyze memorization errors (e.g., missed words, pronunciation slips) to identify weak areas.

Scheduled Reviews
 Automatically schedule review sessions at optimal intervals (e.g., 1 day, 3 days, 7 days) and notify users.

Progress Tracking & Analytics
 Provide visualizations (charts, heatmaps) of error rates, time-spent, and chapters memorized over time.



Main Components

Backend (/backend)

Framework: NestJS (@nestjs/core, @nestjs/common)

ORM/ODM:

Mongoose (@nestjs/mongoose, mongoose) for storing memorization documents, schedules, and analytics.

TypeORM (@nestjs/typeorm, mysql2, typeorm) for core user accounts and authentication in MySQL (if needed).

Authentication: Passport (@nestjs/passport, passport-jwt), JWT (@nestjs/jwt)

Configuration: @nestjs/config

HTTP: Express (bundled with NestJS), @nestjs/axios for external API calls

AI & ML:

OpenAI (openai) for generative memory coaching.

Potential integration with external spaced-repetition APIs.

Cloud Services:

Firebase Admin (firebase-admin) for push notifications or real-time triggers.

Google Cloud Pub/Sub (@google-cloud/pubsub) for scheduling review-recap jobs (optional).

Payments (Optional): Stripe (stripe) if introducing paid memorization tiers.

Scheduling/Jobs: NestJS Scheduler (@nestjs/schedule) to recalculate review schedules daily (optional).

Other: Axios (axios), Bcrypt (bcrypt), Nodemailer (nodemailer)

Frontend (/frontend-vite)

Framework/Library: React (react, react-dom), Vite (vite)

Routing: React Router (react-router-dom)

State Management:

Redux Toolkit (@reduxjs/toolkit, react-redux) for global user/auth state, if needed.

TanStack Query (@tanstack/react-query) for data fetching and caching.

UI Components: Material-UI (@mui/material), Styled Components (styled-components), TailwindCSS (tailwindcss)

Real-Time & Notifications:

Socket.IO Client (socket.io-client) for live updates (optional).

Firebase SDK (firebase) for push notifications.

Visualization:

Recharts or Chart.js (react-chartjs-2) for line charts.

React-Vis or similar for heatmaps.

Linting/Formatting: ESLint (eslint), Prettier (prettier)

TypeScript: (typescript)



Database Setup

MongoDB (via Mongoose)

Purpose: Store memorization state (Memorisation documents), error rates, review schedule, and analytics history.

Connection: URI configured in config/.env (e.g., MONGODB_URI).

Schema Evolution: Manage via code migrations; no direct auto-sync.

MySQL (via TypeORM)

Purpose: Store core user data (credentials, roles, settings).

Connection: Credentials in config/.env (DB_HOST, DB_PORT, DB_USERNAME, DB_PASSWORD, DB_DATABASE).

Synchronization: DB_SYNC=true only in development; set to false in production to avoid unintended schema changes.



Backend Components

1. memorisation.schema.ts (Data Model)

Defines the MongoDB schema for memorization tracking.

typescript

CopyEdit

// backend/src/models/memorisation.schema.ts
import { Schema } from 'mongoose';

export const MemorisationSchema = new Schema(
  {
    userId: { type: String, required: true, index: true },
    memorisedChapters: { type: [String], default: [] },    // List of chapter IDs/names memorized
    reviewSchedule: { type: [Date], default: [] },         // Future review dates
    nextReviewDate: { type: Date, required: true },        // Next upcoming review
    progress: { type: String, default: 'In Progress' },    // “In Progress” | “Completed”
    lastReviewed: { type: Date, default: null },           // Timestamp of last review session
    errorRate: { type: Number, default: 0 },                // Rolling error rate (0–1)
    timeSpent: { type: Number, default: 0 },                // Total seconds spent memorizing
  },
  { timestamps: true }
);

Registers the schema and related providers.

// backend/src/memorisation/memorisation.module.ts
import { Module } from '@nestjs/common';
import { MongooseModule } from '@nestjs/mongoose';
import { MemorisationSchema } from '../models/memorisation.schema';
import { MemorisationService } from './memorisation.service';
import { MemorisationController } from './memorisation.controller';
import { AIModelService } from '../services/ai-model.service';
import { HttpModule } from '@nestjs/axios';

@Module({
  imports: [
    MongooseModule.forFeature([{ name: 'Memorisation', schema: MemorisationSchema }]),
    HttpModule, // For AIModelService HTTP calls
  ],
  providers: [MemorisationService, AIModelService],
  controllers: [MemorisationController],
})
export class MemorisationModule {}




3. memorisation.controller.ts (API Endpoints)

Handles HTTP requests for managing memorization.

typescript

CopyEdit

// backend/src/memorisation/memorisation.controller.ts
import { Controller, Post, Get, Param, Body, HttpException, HttpStatus } from '@nestjs/common';
import { MemorisationService } from './memorisation.service';

@Controller('api/memorisation')
export class MemorisationController {
  constructor(private readonly memorisationService: MemorisationService) {}

  /**
   * POST /api/memorisation/start
   * Body: { userId: string; initialChapters: string[] }
   * Initializes or resets a memorisation plan for the user.
   */
  @Post('start')
  async startMemorisation(@Body() memorisationData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.memorisationService.startMemorisation(memorisationData);
    } catch (err) {
      throw new HttpException(err.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  /**
   * GET /api/memorisation/progress/:userId
   * Returns the user's current memorisation document(s).
   */
  @Get('progress/:userId')
  async getProgress(@Param('userId') userId: string) {
    try {
      return await this.memorisationService.getProgress(userId);
    } catch (err) {
      throw new HttpException(err.message, HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND);
    }
  }

  /**
   * GET /api/memorisation/review-schedule/:userId
   * Returns an array of review schedules for the user.
   */
  @Get('review-schedule/:userId')
  async getReviewSchedule(@Param('userId') userId: string) {
    try {
      return await this.memorisationService.getReviewSchedule(userId);
    } catch (err) {
      throw new HttpException(err.message, HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND);
    }
  }

  /**
   * POST /api/memorisation/complete
   * Body: { userId: string; reviewedChapters: string[]; errors: number; timeSpent: number }
   * Records completion of a memorisation session, updates error rate, time spent, and schedules next review.
   */
  @Post('complete')
  async completeMemorisation(@Body() memorisationData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.memorisationService.completeMemorisation(memorisationData);
    } catch (err) {
      throw new HttpException(err.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  /**
   * GET /api/memorisation/advice/:userId
   * Returns AI-generated memory coaching advice for the user.
   */
  @Get('advice/:userId')
  async getMemoryAdvice(@Param('userId') userId: string) {
    try {
      return await this.memorisationService.getMemoryAdvice(userId);
    } catch (err) {
      throw new HttpException(err.message, HttpStatus.BAD_GATEWAY);
    }
  }

  /**
   * GET /api/memorisation/analytics/:userId
   * Returns basic analytics (e.g., error rates over time).
   */
  @Get('analytics/:userId')
  async getAnalytics(@Param('userId') userId: string) {
    try {
      return await this.memorisationService.getAnalytics(userId);
    } catch (err) {
      throw new HttpException(err.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  /**
   * GET /api/memorisation/heatmap/:userId
   * Returns heatmap data: array of { chapter: number; date: string; errorRate: number }.
   */
  @Get('heatmap/:userId')
  async getHeatmapData(@Param('userId') userId: string) {
    try {
      return await this.memorisationService.getHeatmapData(userId);
    } catch (err) {
      throw new HttpException(err.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }
}




4. memorisation.service.ts (Service)

Implements core business logic, including schedule calculation, error tracking, and integration with AIModelService.

typescript

CopyEdit

// backend/src/memorisation/memorisation.service.ts
import { Injectable, HttpException, HttpStatus, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import { InjectModel } from '@nestjs/mongoose';
import { Model } from 'mongoose';
import { AIModelService } from '../services/ai-model.service';
import { Document } from 'mongoose';

interface IMemorisation extends Document {
  userId: string;
  memorisedChapters: string[];
  reviewSchedule: Date[];
  nextReviewDate: Date;
  progress: string;
  lastReviewed: Date;
  errorRate: number;
  timeSpent: number;
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

@Injectable()
export class MemorisationService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(MemorisationService.name);

  constructor(
    @InjectModel('Memorisation') private readonly memorisationModel: Model<IMemorisation>,
    private readonly aiModelService: AIModelService,
  ) {}

  /**
   * Initializes or resets a memorisation plan.
   * memorisationData: { userId: string; initialChapters: string[] }
   */
  async startMemorisation(memorisationData: any): Promise<IMemorisation> {
    const { userId, initialChapters } = memorisationData;
    if (!userId || !Array.isArray(initialChapters)) {
      throw new HttpException('Invalid input data', HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }

    // Basic spaced repetition: 1d, 3d, 7d intervals from now
    const now = new Date();
    const reviewSchedule = [
      new Date(now.getTime() + 1 * 24 * 3600 * 1000),
      new Date(now.getTime() + 3 * 24 * 3600 * 1000),
      new Date(now.getTime() + 7 * 24 * 3600 * 1000),
    ];

    // Check if a document already exists
    const existing = await this.memorisationModel.findOne({ userId }).exec();
    if (existing) {
      existing.memorisedChapters = initialChapters;
      existing.reviewSchedule = reviewSchedule;
      existing.nextReviewDate = reviewSchedule[0];
      existing.progress = 'In Progress';
      existing.lastReviewed = now;
      existing.errorRate = 0;
      existing.timeSpent = 0;
      return existing.save();
    }

    const newDoc = new this.memorisationModel({
      userId,
      memorisedChapters: initialChapters,
      reviewSchedule,
      nextReviewDate: reviewSchedule[0],
      progress: 'In Progress',
      lastReviewed: now,
      errorRate: 0,
      timeSpent: 0,
    });
    return newDoc.save();
  }

  /**
   * Retrieves the user's memorisation document(s).
   */
  async getProgress(userId: string): Promise<IMemorisation[]> {
    if (!userId) throw new HttpException('UserId required', HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    return this.memorisationModel.find({ userId }).exec();
  }

  /**
   * Returns the user's reviewSchedule arrays (may have multiple documents if re-initialized).
   */
  async getReviewSchedule(userId: string): Promise<Date[][]> {
    if (!userId) throw new HttpException('UserId required', HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    const docs = await this.memorisationModel.find({ userId }).exec();
    return docs.map((m) => m.reviewSchedule);
  }

  /**
   * Completes a memorisation session for the user.
   * memorisationData: { userId: string; reviewedChapters: string[]; errors: number; timeSpent: number }
   */
  async completeMemorisation(memorisationData: any): Promise<{ message: string }> {
    const { userId, reviewedChapters, errors, timeSpent } = memorisationData;
    if (!userId || !Array.isArray(reviewedChapters)) {
      throw new HttpException('Invalid input', HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
    const doc = await this.memorisationModel.findOne({ userId }).exec();
    if (!doc) throw new HttpException('Memorisation not found', HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND);

    // Merge new chapters
    doc.memorisedChapters = Array.from(new Set([...doc.memorisedChapters, ...reviewedChapters]));

    // Update errorRate as rolling average: (prevErrors * prevTime + errors * timeSpent) / (prevTime + timeSpent)
    const prevTotalTime = doc.timeSpent;
    const prevWeightedErrors = doc.errorRate * prevTotalTime;
    const newTotalTime = prevTotalTime + timeSpent;
    doc.errorRate =
      newTotalTime > 0 ? (prevWeightedErrors + errors * timeSpent) / newTotalTime : doc.errorRate;
    doc.timeSpent = newTotalTime;
    doc.lastReviewed = new Date();

    // Recalculate nextReviewDate via AIModelService
    try {
      const nextDateISO = await this.aiModelService.getNextReviewDate(userId, {
        memorisedChapters: doc.memorisedChapters,
        errorRate: doc.errorRate,
        lastReviewed: doc.lastReviewed,
      });
      doc.nextReviewDate = new Date(nextDateISO);
    } catch (err) {
      this.logger.error('Failed to compute next review date', err.message);
      // Fallback: schedule +1 day
      doc.nextReviewDate = new Date(Date.now() + 24 * 3600 * 1000);
    }

    // If user has memorized all 114 chapters, mark as completed
    if (doc.memorisedChapters.length >= 114) {
      doc.progress = 'Completed';
    }

    await doc.save();
    return { message: 'Memorisation session recorded successfully' };
  }

  /**
   * Fetches AI-generated memorisation advice for the user.
   */
  async getMemoryAdvice(userId: string): Promise<{ advice: string }> {
    if (!userId) throw new HttpException('UserId required', HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    const progressDocs = await this.getProgress(userId);
    const adviceText = await this.aiModelService.generateMemorisationAdvice(userId, progressDocs);
    return { advice: adviceText };
  }

  /**
   * Returns simple analytics data (error rates over time).
   */
  async getAnalytics(userId: string): Promise<{ dates: string[]; errorRates: number[] }> {
    if (!userId) throw new HttpException('UserId required', HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    const docs = await this.memorisationModel.find({ userId }).exec();
    // Placeholder: return last two sessions
    if (!docs.length) return { dates: [], errorRates: [] };
    const sorted = docs.sort((a, b) => a.updatedAt.getTime() - b.updatedAt.getTime());
    const dates = sorted.map((d) => d.lastReviewed?.toISOString().split('T')[0] || '');
    const errorRates = sorted.map((d) => d.errorRate);
    return { dates, errorRates };
  }

  /**
   * Returns data suitable for a heatmap: array of { chapter, date, errorRate }.
   */
  async getHeatmapData(
    userId: string
  ): Promise<{ chapter: number; date: string; errorRate: number }[]> {
    if (!userId) throw new HttpException('UserId required', HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    // In a full implementation, fetch per-chapter review logs. Here, return a mock.
    return [
      { chapter: 1, date: '2025-01-01', errorRate: 0.05 },
      { chapter: 2, date: '2025-01-02', errorRate: 0.10 },
      { chapter: 3, date: '2025-01-03', errorRate: 0.02 },
      // …more data
    ];
  }
}




5. ai-model.service.ts (AI Integration Service)

Handles calls to external AI endpoints for advice, next‐review calculation, and difficulty prediction.

typescript

CopyEdit

// backend/src/services/ai-model.service.ts
import { Injectable, HttpException, HttpStatus, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import { HttpService } from '@nestjs/axios';
import { lastValueFrom } from 'rxjs';

@Injectable()
export class AIModelService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(AIModelService.name);

  private readonly openAIAPIUrl = 'https://api.openai.com/v1/completions';
  private readonly spacedRepetitionAPIUrl = 'https://api.spacedrepetition.com/next-review';
  private readonly memorisationDifficultyModelUrl = 'https://api.memorisationdifficulty.com/predict';
  private readonly openAIKey = process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY;

  constructor(private readonly httpService: HttpService) {}

  /**
   * Uses OpenAI to generate personalized memorisation advice.
   */
  async generateMemorisationAdvice(userId: string, progressData: any): Promise<string> {
    const prompt = `User ${userId} has memorised chapters: ${JSON.stringify(
      progressData.map((d: any) => d.memorisedChapters).flat()
    )}. Their current error rates over time are: ${JSON.stringify(
      progressData.map((d: any) => ({ date: d.lastReviewed, errorRate: d.errorRate }))
    )}. Provide personalized advice to improve their Quran memorisation and retention.`;

    try {
      const response = await lastValueFrom(
        this.httpService.post(
          this.openAIAPIUrl,
          {
            model: 'gpt-4',
            prompt,
            max_tokens: 150,
            temperature: 0.7,
            top_p: 1.0,
          },
          {
            headers: {
              Authorization: `Bearer ${this.openAIKey}`,
              'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            },
          }
        )
      );
      return response.data.choices[0].text.trim();
    } catch (error: any) {
      this.logger.error('Error generating memorisation advice:', error.message);
      throw new HttpException('Error generating memorisation advice', HttpStatus.BAD_GATEWAY);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Calculates the next review date via an external spaced-repetition API.
   */
  async getNextReviewDate(userId: string, memorisationData: any): Promise<string> {
    try {
      const response = await lastValueFrom(
        this.httpService.post(this.spacedRepetitionAPIUrl, { userId, memorisationData })
      );
      return response.data.nextReviewDate; // ISO string
    } catch (error: any) {
      this.logger.error('Error calculating next review date:', error.message);
      throw new HttpException('Error calculating next review date', HttpStatus.BAD_GATEWAY);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Predicts difficulty level of new memorisation content for the user.
   */
  async analyzeMemorisationDifficulty(userId: string, memorisationData: any): Promise<string> {
    try {
      const response = await lastValueFrom(
        this.httpService.post(this.memorisationDifficultyModelUrl, { userId, memorisationData })
      );
      return response.data.difficultyLevel; // e.g., “Medium” or “Hard”
    } catch (error: any) {
      this.logger.error('Error predicting memorisation difficulty:', error.message);
      throw new HttpException('Error predicting memorisation difficulty', HttpStatus.BAD_GATEWAY);
    }
  }
}




6. swarm-orchestrator.service.ts (Orchestration Service)

Coordinates multiple memorization services to provide a combined response.

typescript

CopyEdit

// backend/src/services/swarm-orchestrator.service.ts
import { Injectable, HttpException, HttpStatus, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import { MemorisationService } from '../memorisation/memorisation.service';
import { AIModelService } from './ai-model.service';

@Injectable()
export class SwarmOrchestrator {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(SwarmOrchestrator.name);

  constructor(
    private readonly memorisationService: MemorisationService,
    private readonly aiModelService: AIModelService,
  ) {}

  /**
   * Orchestrates a full memorisation update: fetch progress, advice, schedule, difficulty feedback.
   */
  async orchestrateMemorisation(userId: string, memorisedContent: any): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const memorisationProgress = await this.memorisationService.getProgress(userId);
      const memorisationAdvice = await this.memorisationService.getMemoryAdvice(userId);
      const reviewSchedule = await this.memorisationService.getReviewSchedule(userId);
      const difficultyFeedback = await this.aiModelService.analyzeMemorisationDifficulty(
        userId,
        memorisedContent
      );

      return {
        success: true,
        memorisationProgress,
        memorisationAdvice,
        reviewSchedule,
        difficultyFeedback,
      };
    } catch (error: any) {
      this.logger.error('Error orchestrating memorisation process:', error.message);
      throw new HttpException('Error orchestrating memorisation process', HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR);
    }
  }
}

Frontend Components

Below are React/TypeScript components utilizing TanStack Query for data fetching and Material-UI for styling. Each assumes userId is available from authentication context or localStorage.



1. ProgressTracker.tsx

Displays the user’s current memorization progress.

tsx

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/ProgressTracker.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { Typography, Box } from '@mui/material';

interface MemorisationDoc {
  memorisedChapters: string[];
  progress: string;
  nextReviewDate: string;
  errorRate: number;
  timeSpent: number;
}

interface ProgressTrackerProps {
  userId: string;
}

const ProgressTracker: React.FC<ProgressTrackerProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const { data, isLoading, isError } = useQuery<MemorisationDoc[]>(
    ['progress', userId],
    () => fetch(`/api/memorisation/progress/${userId}`).then((res) => res.json())
  );

  if (isLoading) {
    return <Typography>Loading progress...</Typography>;
  }
  if (isError || !data) {
    return <Typography color="error">Failed to load progress.</Typography>;
  }

  // Display the latest memorisation document (sorted by updatedAt)
  const sorted = [...data].sort((a, b) => {
    const dateA = new Date((a as any).updatedAt).getTime();
    const dateB = new Date((b as any).updatedAt).getTime();
    return dateB - dateA;
  });
  const latest = sorted[0];

  return (
    <Box>
      <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
        Your Memorisation Progress
      </Typography>
      <Typography>
        Status: <strong>{latest.progress}</strong>
      </Typography>
      <Typography>
        Chapters Memorised: {latest.memorisedChapters.join(', ') || 'None Yet'}
      </Typography>
      <Typography>
        Next Review Date: {new Date(latest.nextReviewDate).toLocaleDateString()}
      </Typography>
      <Typography>Error Rate: {(latest.errorRate * 100).toFixed(1)}%</Typography>
      <Typography>
        Time Spent: {(latest.timeSpent / 3600).toFixed(2)} hours
      </Typography>
    </Box>
  );
};

export default ProgressTracker;




2. GapAnalysis.tsx

Fetches and displays upcoming review dates (i.e., scheduled reviews).

tsx

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/GapAnalysis.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { Typography, List, ListItem, ListItemText, Box } from '@mui/material';

interface ReviewScheduleResponse {
  schedule: string[]; // Array of ISO date strings
  nextReview: string; // ISO date string
}

interface GapAnalysisProps {
  userId: string;
}

const GapAnalysis: React.FC<GapAnalysisProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const { data, isLoading, isError } = useQuery<ReviewScheduleResponse[]>(
    ['reviewSchedule', userId],
    () => fetch(`/api/memorisation/review-schedule/${userId}`).then((res) => res.json())
  );

  if (isLoading) return <Typography>Loading review schedule...</Typography>;
  if (isError || !data) return <Typography color="error">Failed to load schedule.</Typography>;

  // Flatten multiple schedules (if the user restarted multiple times)
  const flattened: string[] = data.flat().map((d) => new Date(d).toLocaleDateString());

  return (
    <Box>
      <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
        Upcoming Review Schedule
      </Typography>
      {flattened.length === 0 ? (
        <Typography>No scheduled reviews.</Typography>
      ) : (
        <List>
          {flattened.map((dateStr, idx) => (
            <ListItem key={idx}>
              <ListItemText primary={`Review Date: ${dateStr}`} />
            </ListItem>
          ))}
        </List>
      )}
    </Box>
  );
};

export default GapAnalysis;




3. MemoryCoach.tsx

Fetches AI-generated memory coaching advice on demand.

tsx

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/MemoryCoach.tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { Button, Typography, Box, CircularProgress } from '@mui/material';

interface AdviceResponse {
  advice: string;
}

interface MemoryCoachProps {
  userId: string;
}

const MemoryCoach: React.FC<MemoryCoachProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [enabled, setEnabled] = useState(false);
  const { data, isLoading, isError } = useQuery<AdviceResponse>(
    ['memoryAdvice', userId],
    () => fetch(`/api/memorisation/advice/${userId}`).then((res) => res.json()),
    { enabled }
  );

  const handleClick = () => {
    setEnabled(true);
  };

  return (
    <Box>
      <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
        AI-Powered Memory Coach
      </Typography>
      <Button variant="contained" onClick={handleClick} disabled={enabled}>
        {enabled ? 'Fetching Advice…' : 'Get Memory Advice'}
      </Button>
      {isLoading && (
        <Box mt={2}>
          <CircularProgress size={24} />
        </Box>
      )}
      {isError && <Typography color="error">Failed to load advice.</Typography>}
      {data && (
        <Box mt={2}>
          <Typography>{data.advice}</Typography>
        </Box>
      )}
    </Box>
  );
};

export default MemoryCoach;
