5. RecitationPlayer.tsx

Allows users to record or upload recitation audio and receive feedback from Phase 4’s services. Simplified for memorization context.

tsx

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/RecitationPlayer.tsx
import React, { useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { Button, Typography, Box } from '@mui/material';

interface RecitationPlayerProps {
  userId: string;
  onRecitationSubmit?: (score: number, feedback: string, audioBlob: Blob) => void;
}

const RecitationPlayer: React.FC<RecitationPlayerProps> = ({ userId, onRecitationSubmit }) => {
  const [audioURL, setAudioURL] = useState<string>('');
  const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);
  const audioRef = useRef<HTMLAudioElement>(null);

  const handleFileChange = (file: File) => {
    setAudioURL(URL.createObjectURL(file));
    setUploading(true);

    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('file', file);

    fetch('/api/recitation/upload', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: formData,
    })
      .then((res) => res.json())
      .then((data) => {
        // data: { tajweedFeedback, phonemeFeedback, emotionFeedback, aiGuidanceFeedback, swarmFeedback }
        console.log('Feedback:', data);
        setUploading(false);

        // Example: parse numeric score from aiGuidanceFeedback
        const scoreMatch = data.aiGuidanceFeedback?.match(/\d+/);
        const score = scoreMatch ? parseInt(scoreMatch[0], 10) : 0;
        const feedbackText = data.aiGuidanceFeedback || '';

        if (onRecitationSubmit) {
          onRecitationSubmit(score, feedbackText, file);
        }
      })
      .catch((error) => {
        console.error('Error uploading recitation:', error);
        setUploading(false);
      });
  };

  return (
    <Box>
      <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
        Recitation Practice
      </Typography>
      <input
        type="file"
        accept="audio/*"
        onChange={(e) => {
          if (e.target.files && e.target.files[0]) {
            handleFileChange(e.target.files[0]);
          }
        }}
      />
      {uploading && <Typography>Analyzing...</Typography>}
      {audioURL && (
        <Box mt={2}>
          <audio ref={audioRef} controls src={audioURL} />
        </Box>
      )}
    </Box>
  );
};

export default RecitationPlayer;




6. AnalyticsVisualization.tsx

Plots a line chart of error rate over time. (Using react-chartjs-2 as an example.)

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/AnalyticsVisualization.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { Line } from 'react-chartjs-2';
import { Typography, Box } from '@mui/material';
import {
  Chart as ChartJS,
  CategoryScale,
  LinearScale,
  PointElement,
  LineElement,
  Title,
  Tooltip,
  Legend,
} from 'chart.js';

ChartJS.register(CategoryScale, LinearScale, PointElement, LineElement, Title, Tooltip, Legend);

interface AnalyticsData {
  dates: string[];       // e.g., ['2025-01-01', '2025-01-02']
  errorRates: number[];  // e.g., [0.05, 0.08]
}

interface AnalyticsVisualizationProps {
  data: AnalyticsData | null;
}

const AnalyticsVisualization: React.FC<AnalyticsVisualizationProps> = ({ data }) => {
  if (!data) {
    return (
      <Box>
        <Typography variant="h6">Analytics Visualization</Typography>
        <Typography>Loading...</Typography>
      </Box>
    );
  }

  const chartData = {
    labels: data.dates,
    datasets: [
      {
        label: 'Error Rate (%)',
        data: data.errorRates.map((er) => er * 100),
        borderColor: 'rgba(75,192,192,1)',
        backgroundColor: 'rgba(75,192,192,0.2)',
        fill: true,
      },
    ],
  };

  return (
    <Box>
      <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
        Error Rate Over Time
      </Typography>
      <Line data={chartData} />
    </Box>
  );
};

export default AnalyticsVisualization;




7. HeatmapVisualization.tsx

Renders a heatmap of error rates by chapter and date. (Using react-vis as an example.)

tsx

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/HeatmapVisualization.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { Typography, Box } from '@mui/material';
import { XYPlot, XAxis, YAxis, HeatmapSeries, Hint } from 'react-vis';

interface HeatmapItem {
  chapter: number;   // x-axis
  date: string;      // y-axis (ISO date)
  errorRate: number; // 0–1
}

interface HeatmapVisualizationProps {
  data: HeatmapItem[];
}

const HeatmapVisualization: React.FC<HeatmapVisualizationProps> = ({ data }) => {
  // Extract unique sorted chapters & dates
  const uniqueChapters = Array.from(new Set(data.map((d) => d.chapter))).sort((a, b) => a - b);
  const uniqueDates = Array.from(new Set(data.map((d) => d.date))).sort();

  // Map to numeric grid
  const plotData = data.map((d) => ({
    x: uniqueChapters.indexOf(d.chapter),
    y: uniqueDates.indexOf(d.date),
    color: d.errorRate,
    original: d,
  }));

  return (
    <Box>
      <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
        Error Rate Heatmap
      </Typography>
      <XYPlot
        xType="ordinal"
        yType="ordinal"
        width={500}
        height={300}
        margin={{ left: 60, bottom: 60 }}
      >
        <XAxis
          title="Chapter"
          tickValues={uniqueChapters.map((_, idx) => idx)}
          tickFormat={(v) => uniqueChapters[v].toString()}
        />
        <YAxis
          title="Date"
          tickValues={uniqueDates.map((_, idx) => idx)}
          tickFormat={(v) => new Date(uniqueDates[v]).toLocaleDateString()}
        />
        <HeatmapSeries
          className="heatmap-series"
          colorRange={['#ffffff', '#ff0000']} // White to red
          data={plotData}
          opacityType="literal"
          getOpacity={(d: any) => Math.min(1, d.color + 0.1)}
        />
      </XYPlot>
    </Box>
  );
};

export default HeatmapVisualization;

          {heatmapLoading ? (
            <Typography>Loading heatmap...</Typography>
          ) : (
            <HeatmapVisualization data={heatmapData || []} />

        <Typography variant="h5" gutterBottom>
          Practice Recitation
        </Typography>
        <RecitationPlayer userId={userId} />

    </Container>

Integration Details

Backend Integration

Modules & Providers

MemorisationModule imports MongooseModule.forFeature([{ name: 'Memorisation', schema: MemorisationSchema }]) and HttpModule.

Registers MemorisationService, MemorisationController, and AIModelService.

Routes (all under /api/memorisation)

POST /api/memorisation/start → startMemorisation(data: { userId, initialChapters })

GET /api/memorisation/progress/:userId → getProgress(userId)

GET /api/memorisation/review-schedule/:userId → getReviewSchedule(userId)

POST /api/memorisation/complete → completeMemorisation({ userId, reviewedChapters, errors, timeSpent })

GET /api/memorisation/advice/:userId → getMemoryAdvice(userId)

GET /api/memorisation/analytics/:userId → getAnalytics(userId)

GET /api/memorisation/heatmap/:userId → getHeatmapData(userId)

Services

MemorisationService: Manages CRUD operations, computes next review, updates error rates.

AIModelService: Integrates with OpenAI (GPT-4) and spaced-repetition/difficulty endpoints.

SwarmOrchestrator (optional): Coordinates multiple service calls to return a combined payload.

Database

MongoDB stores one Memorisation document per user (indexed by userId).

MySQL (via TypeORM) continues storing user credentials and roles; no new MySQL entities needed specifically for memorization.

Scheduling (Optional)

Use NestJS’s scheduling module (@nestjs/schedule) to run a daily cron job that:

Finds all Memorisation docs whose nextReviewDate is within the next 24 hours.

Sends a push notification (via Firebase Admin) or email reminder (via Nodemailer).



Frontend Integration

Routes & Navigation

Add a new route (e.g., /memorisation) that renders MemorisationDashboard.tsx.

Ensure userId is available from authentication context (e.g., stored in Redux or localStorage).

Data Fetching

TanStack Query (React Query) is used in all components to fetch from endpoints:

['progress', userId] → GET /api/memorisation/progress/${userId}

['reviewSchedule', userId] → GET /api/memorisation/review-schedule/${userId}

['memoryAdvice', userId] → GET /api/memorisation/advice/${userId}

['analytics', userId] → GET /api/memorisation/analytics/${userId}

['heatmap', userId] → GET /api/memorisation/heatmap/${userId}

State Management

Local component state handles loading/error/UI interactions (e.g., enabling advice fetch).

Global Redux state (optional) can store userId, authentication token, and user profile.

Styling & Responsiveness

Use Material-UI’s Container, Box, Typography, List, etc., combined with Tailwind utilities for quick layout adjustments.

Ensure charts and heatmaps scale on mobile (e.g., using width: 100% or responsive container).

Real-Time Notifications (Optional)

If using Firebase Cloud Messaging, register a service worker to receive “Next review due” push notifications.

Alternatively, use Socket.IO to push an event from the backend when nextReviewDate arrives.



Phase 6 Summary

Phase 6: Memorisation introduces a comprehensive system for helping users memorize the Quran:

Backend

MemorisationSchema (MongoDB) tracks memorised chapters, upcoming review dates, progress status, error rates, and total time spent.

MemorisationController exposes REST endpoints for starting/resetting plans, fetching progress, completing sessions, and retrieving AI advice/analytics.

MemorisationService implements core logic: scheduling spaced repetition, updating error rates, recalculating nextReviewDate via AIModelService, and generating analytics.

AIModelService integrates with OpenAI (GPT-4) for memory coaching and an external spaced-repetition API for review scheduling.

SwarmOrchestrator (optional) coordinates multiple service calls for a unified response.

Frontend

ProgressTracker fetches and displays the user’s current memorisation status.

GapAnalysis lists upcoming review dates.

MemoryCoach fetches AI-generated advice on demand.

AdaptiveRepetition displays the spaced repetition schedule.

AnalyticsVisualization renders a line chart of error rate over time.

HeatmapVisualization shows error rates by chapter and date.

RecitationPlayer supports recording/uploading recitations and displays Phase 4 feedback for on-the-fly error correction.

MemorisationDashboard aggregates all components into a cohesive UI.

This phase seamlessly integrates into the existing NestJS and React/Vite architecture, leveraging Mongoose, TypeORM, OpenAI, and Axios on the backend, and Material-UI, TanStack Query, and react-chartjs-2/react-vis on the frontend. By combining adaptive spaced repetition, AI coaching, and visual analytics, Phase 6 empowers users with a data-driven, personalized path to effectively memorize the Quran.



Phase 7: Learning

Introductory Overview

In Phase 7, the Quran Education AI Platform deepens users’ understanding by delivering AI‐powered, context‐rich insights into Quranic verses. The system continuously adapts to each learner’s progress, preferences, and behavior—offering dynamic learning paths, an AI‐powered reading assistant, and real‐time feedback. By integrating advanced LLMs, external scholarly APIs (tafsir & hadith), and emotion‐aware feedback, Phase 7 ensures a truly immersive, personalized learning experience.



Objectives

Personalized Learning Path

Build adaptive, evolving curricula tailored to individual strengths, interests, and progress metrics.

AI‐Powered Reading Assistant

Leverage GPT‐4 to explain linguistic nuances, grammar, and deeper meanings of selected verses on demand.

Contextual Understanding

Fetch and present classical tafsir and relevant hadith from external scholarly APIs, anchored to each verse.

AI‐Enhanced Feedback

Provide real‐time, empathetic guidance (e.g., simpler explanations if confusion is detected) via Emotion AI.

Pathway Builder

Offer tools to create and update a user’s “learning path,” automatically incorporating new content based on prior performance.

Swarm Orchestrator

Use a lightweight Reinforcement Learning (DQN) agent plus collaborative data analysis to optimize each learner’s path.



Backend Components (/backend)

The backend is built with NestJS, using Mongoose for MongoDB (learning paths & insights) and TypeORM for MySQL (core user data, authentication). AI integrations rely on OpenAI, Axios for external calls, and TensorFlow.js for a simple DQN agent. Authentication uses Passport‐JWT, and configuration is managed via @nestjs/config.

1. Data Model – learningPath.ts

Defines the MongoDB schema for each user’s learning path, progress, preferences, and AI‐generated insights.

ts

CopyEdit

// backend/src/models/learningPath.ts
import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface ILearningPath extends Document {
  userId: string;
  path: string[];
  progress: string;
  preferences: any;
  insights: string[];
  feedback: string[];
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

const learningPathSchema = new Schema<ILearningPath>(
  {
    userId:      { type: String, required: true },
    path:        { type: [String], default: [] },
    progress:    { type: String, default: 'In Progress' },
    preferences: { type: Object, default: {} },
    insights:    { type: [String], default: [] },
    feedback:    { type: [String], default: [] },
  },
  { timestamps: true }
);

export const LearningPath = model<ILearningPath>(
  'LearningPath',
  learningPathSchema
);

// backend/src/learning/learningPathController.ts
import { Controller, Post, Get, Param, Body } from '@nestjs/common';
import { LearningPathService } from './learningPathService';

@Controller('learning-path')
export class LearningPathController {
  constructor(
    private readonly learningPathService: LearningPathService
  ) {}

  @Post('start')
  async startLearningPath(@Body() learningPathData: any) {
    return this.learningPathService.startLearningPath(learningPathData);
  }

  @Get('progress/:userId')
  async getLearningPathProgress(@Param('userId') userId: string) {
    return this.learningPathService.getLearningPathProgress(userId);
  }

  @Post('complete')
  async completeLearningPath(@Body() learningPathData: any) {
    return this.learningPathService.completeLearningPath(learningPathData);
  }

  @Post('reading-assistance')
  async getReadingAssistance(@Body() requestData: any) {
    return this.learningPathService.getReadingAssistance(requestData);
  }

  @Post('contextual-insights')
  async getContextualInsights(@Body() requestData: any) {
    return this.learningPathService.getContextualInsights(requestData);
  }
}




3. Service – learningPathService.ts

Contains business logic for learning path CRUD operations and delegates AI calls to AIService.

ts

CopyEdit

// backend/src/learning/learningPathService.ts
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { LearningPath } from '../models/learningPath';
import { AIService } from '../services/aiService';

@Injectable()
export class LearningPathService {
  constructor(private readonly aiService: AIService) {}

  async startLearningPath(learningPathData: any) {
    const learningPath = new LearningPath(learningPathData);
    return learningPath.save();
  }

  async getLearningPathProgress(userId: string) {
    const learningPath = await LearningPath.findOne({ userId });
    if (!learningPath) throw new Error('Learning path not found');
    return learningPath.progress;
  }

  async completeLearningPath(learningPathData: any) {
    return LearningPath.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId: learningPathData.userId },
      { $set: { progress: 'Completed' } },
      { new: true }
    );
  }

  async getReadingAssistance(requestData: any) {
    return this.aiService.provideReadingAssistance(requestData);
  }

  async getContextualInsights(requestData: any) {
    return this.aiService.provideContextualInsights(requestData);
  }
}




4. AI Service – aiService.ts

Integrates with OpenAI (GPT‐4) for advanced verse explanations, and fetches tafsir & hadith via external REST APIs.

ts

CopyEdit

// backend/src/services/aiService.ts
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { Configuration, OpenAIApi } from 'openai';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class AIService {
  private openai: OpenAIApi;

  constructor() {
    const configuration = new Configuration({
      apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY,
    });
    this.openai = new OpenAIApi(configuration);
  }

  async provideReadingAssistance(data: any): Promise<any> {
    const { verse } = data;
    const response = await this.openai.createCompletion({
      model: 'gpt-4',
      prompt: `Provide an advanced explanation of the Quran verse:\n"${verse}"`,
      max_tokens: 250,
    });
    return { explanation: response.data.choices[0].text.trim() };
  }

  async provideContextualInsights(data: any): Promise<any> {
    const { verse } = data;
    const [hadith, tafsir] = await Promise.all([
      this.getHadithRelatedToVerse(verse),
      this.getTafsirRelatedToVerse(verse),
    ]);
    return { relatedHadith: hadith, tafsir };
  }

  private async getHadithRelatedToVerse(verse: string): Promise<any> {
    const response = await axios.get(
      `https://api.sunnah.com/v1/hadiths/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(verse)}`
    );
    return response.data;
  }

  private async getTafsirRelatedToVerse(verse: string): Promise<any> {
    const response = await axios.get(
      `https://api.alquran.cloud/v1/tafseer/${encodeURIComponent(verse)}`
    );
    return response.data;
  }
}




Frontend Components (/frontend-vite)

Built with React + Vite, leveraging TanStack Query for data fetching and Material‐UI for styling. Each component calls the NestJS API endpoints and renders UI accordingly.

1. Pathway Builder – PathwayBuilder.tsx

Allows users to define and save a personalized learning path (topics, preferences).

tsx

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/PathwayBuilder.tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useMutation } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { Button, TextField, Typography } from '@mui/material';

const PathwayBuilder = ({ userId }: { userId: string }) => {
  const [path, setPath] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [preferences, setPreferences] = useState<any>({});

  const { mutate: startLearningPath, isLoading } = useMutation(
    (data: any) =>
      fetch('/api/learning-path/start', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(data),
      }).then((res) => res.json()),
    {
      onSuccess: (result) => {
        setPath(result.path || []);
      },
    }
  );

  const handleSavePathway = () => {
    startLearningPath({ userId, path, preferences });
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <Typography variant="h6">Build Your Quran Learning Pathway</Typography>

      <TextField
        label="Select a topic"
        value={preferences.topic || ''}
        onChange={(e) =>
          setPreferences({ ...preferences, topic: e.target.value })
        }
        margin="normal"
        fullWidth
      />

      <Button
        variant="contained"
        onClick={handleSavePathway}
        disabled={isLoading}
      >
        {isLoading ? 'Saving...' : 'Start Learning'}
      </Button>

      <Typography variant="h6" sx={{ mt: 2 }}>
        Your Learning Path
      </Typography>
      <ul>
        {path.map((step, index) => (
          <li key={index}>{step}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
};

export default PathwayBuilder;




2. AI Reading Assistant – AIReadingAssistant.tsx

Fetches advanced explanations for any Quranic verse via GPT-4.

tsx

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/AIReadingAssistant.tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useMutation } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { Button, TextareaAutosize, Typography } from '@mui/material';

const AIReadingAssistant = ({ userId }: { userId: string }) => {
  const [verse, setVerse] = useState<string>('');
  const [explanation, setExplanation] = useState<string>('');

  const { mutate: getReadingAssistance, isLoading } = useMutation(
    (data: any) =>
      fetch('/api/learning-path/reading-assistance', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(data),
      }).then((res) => res.json()),
    {
      onSuccess: (result) => {
        setExplanation(result.explanation);
      },
    }
  );

  const handleGetAssistance = () => {
    if (verse.trim()) {
      getReadingAssistance({ userId, verse });
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <Typography variant="h6">AI Reading Assistant</Typography>

      <TextareaAutosize
        minRows={3}
        placeholder="Enter Quranic verse"
        style={{ width: '100%', marginTop: 8 }}
        value={verse}
        onChange={(e) => setVerse(e.target.value)}
      />

      <Button
        variant="contained"
        onClick={handleGetAssistance}
        disabled={isLoading || !verse.trim()}
        sx={{ mt: 1 }}
      >
        {isLoading ? 'Fetching...' : 'Get Explanation'}
      </Button>

      {explanation && (
        <Typography sx={{ mt: 2 }}>{explanation}</Typography>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default AIReadingAssistant;




3. Contextual Insights – ContextualInsights.tsx

Fetches tafsir and hadith for a given verse from the backend.

tsx

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/ContextualInsights.tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useMutation } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { Button, TextareaAutosize, Typography } from '@mui/material';

const ContextualInsights = ({ userId }: { userId: string }) => {
  const [verse, setVerse] = useState<string>('');
  const [insights, setInsights] = useState<any>(null);

  const { mutate: getContextualInsights, isLoading } = useMutation(
    (data: any) =>
      fetch('/api/learning-path/contextual-insights', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(data),
      }).then((res) => res.json()),
    {
      onSuccess: (result) => {
        setInsights(result);
      },
    }
  );

  const handleGetInsights = () => {
    if (verse.trim()) {
      getContextualInsights({ userId, verse });
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <Typography variant="h6">Contextual Insights</Typography>

      <TextareaAutosize
        minRows={3}
        placeholder="Enter Quranic verse"
        style={{ width: '100%', marginTop: 8 }}
        value={verse}
        onChange={(e) => setVerse(e.target.value)}
      />

      <Button
        variant="contained"
        onClick={handleGetInsights}
        disabled={isLoading || !verse.trim()}
        sx={{ mt: 1 }}
      >
        {isLoading ? 'Fetching...' : 'Get Insights'}
      </Button>

      {insights && (
        <div style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>
          <Typography variant="h6">Related Hadith</Typography>
          <ul>
            {insights.relatedHadith.map((hadith: string, idx: number) => (
              <li key={idx}>{hadith}</li>
            ))}
          </ul>

          <Typography variant="h6" sx={{ mt: 2 }}>
            Tafsir
          </Typography>
          <Typography>{insights.tafsir}</Typography>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default ContextualInsights;




4. Learning Progress – LearningProgress.tsx

Displays the current progress state of the user’s learning path.

tsx

CopyEdit

// frontend-vite/src/components/LearningProgress.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { Typography } from '@mui/material';

const LearningProgress = ({ userId }: { userId: string }) => {
  const { data: progress, isLoading } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['learningProgress', userId],
    queryFn: () =>
      fetch(`/api/learning-path/progress/${userId}`).then((res) => res.json()),
  });

  if (isLoading) return <Typography>Loading...</Typography>;

  return (
    <div>
      <Typography variant="h6">Your Learning Progress</Typography>
      <Typography>{progress?.progress || 'No progress yet'}</Typography>
    </div>
  );
};

export default LearningProgress;

Integration with Existing Structure

Main Components

Backend (/backend)

NestJS modules register LearningPathController, LearningPathService, and AIService.

Mongoose manages the LearningPath schema in MongoDB; TypeORM remains active for user authentication (MySQL).

OpenAI integration lives in AIService; Axios fetches tafsir/hadith from external APIs.

Passport-JWT secures routes; @nestjs/config handles environment variables.

Frontend (/frontend-vite)

React + Vite build toolchain compiles TSX components.

TanStack Query handles API calls (start path, reading assistance, contextual insights, progress).

Material-UI provides consistent styling; TailwindCSS remains available for utility classes.

Key Technologies

Backend

NestJS for structured APIs (@nestjs/common, @nestjs/platform-express)

Mongoose (@nestjs/mongoose, mongoose) for MongoDB learning‐path data

TypeORM (@nestjs/typeorm, mysql2, typeorm) for MySQL user table

OpenAI SDK (openai) for GPT-4

Axios for REST calls (hadith, tafsir)

Passport & JWT (@nestjs/passport, passport-jwt, @nestjs/jwt) for auth

TensorFlow.js (@tensorflow/tfjs-node) for a minimal DQN agent

Emotion AI (custom emotionAIService) for empathetic feedback

Frontend

React (react, react-dom) + Vite (vite)

React Router (react-router-dom) for navigation (if extended)

TanStack Query (@tanstack/react-query) for data fetching

Redux Toolkit (@reduxjs/toolkit, react-redux) if state sharing is needed later

Material-UI (@mui/material) for theming & responsive layout

TailwindCSS (tailwindcss) for lightweight utility classes

Socket.IO Client (socket.io-client) ready for real-time future enhancements

TypeScript (typescript) for type safety

Database Setup

MySQL (TypeORM)

Stores core user records and authentication details (JWT tokens, roles).

Configured via config/.env with DB_HOST, DB_PORT, DB_USERNAME, DB_PASSWORD, DB_DATABASE.

Set DB_SYNC=false in production to prevent unintended schema changes.

MongoDB (Mongoose)

Stores each user’s LearningPath document and AI‐generated insights.

Connection URI is in config/.env (MONGODB_URI).

No auto‐sync—migrations or versioned schemas handle updates.



Summary

Phase 7 introduces AI‐driven, personalized learning that helps users go beyond rote memorization—offering:

A Pathway Builder for curated, adaptive curricula

AI Reading Assistance with GPT-4 explanations

Contextual Insights via classical tafsir and hadith APIs

Real‐time Progress Tracking and Emotion‐aware Feedback

This phase integrates seamlessly with the existing NestJS + React/Vite architecture, leveraging MongoDB for flexible user pathways and MySQL for core user data. By the end of Phase 7, learners will benefit from an interactive, deeply contextualized Quran study experience—paving the way for Phase 8: Teaching.

Phase 8: Teaching

In Phase 8, the focus is on empowering teachers with AI-driven tools to enhance their teaching capabilities and streamline classroom management. These tools provide real-time insights, personalized lesson plans, and support for interactive student engagement.

Key Features and Components:

Teacher Dashboard: An intuitive interface for teachers to monitor student progress, track areas for improvement, and manage classroom activities effectively.

Lesson Planning Tool: AI-powered lesson plans tailored to individual student data and learning preferences, enabling a personalized approach to teaching.

Collaborative Session Tool: Real-time collaboration tools for teachers and students to engage interactively and work on shared learning goals.

Real-Time Classroom Analytics: AI-driven analytics that provides real-time insights to optimize teaching methods and improve student engagement.

Resource Sharing: A feature that enables teachers to easily share educational materials with their students, promoting resource accessibility.

AI-Powered Swarm Orchestrator: A dynamic system that adapts lesson delivery based on real-time student performance, ensuring optimal engagement and understanding.



Backend Components

Teaching Data Model (teaching.ts)

This model represents teaching-related data in the system, which includes student progress, lesson plans, shared resources, and real-time analytics.

typescript

Copy code

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

// Define the interface for the Teaching document
export interface ITeaching extends Document {
  userId: string;
  studentProgress: StudentProgress;
  lessonPlans: LessonPlan[];
  resourcesShared: Resource[];
  orchestratorStatus: string;
  emotionAnalysis: EmotionAnalysis | null;
  predictivePerformance: PredictivePerformance | null;
  adaptiveContent: string[];
  collaborativeSessions: CollaborativeSession[];
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

export interface StudentProgress {
  totalLessonsCompleted: number;
  currentLesson: string;
  performanceMetrics: { accuracy: number; timeSpent: number };
}

export interface LessonPlan {
  planId: string;
  subject: string;
  learningObjectives: string[];
  resources: string[];
  schedule: Date;
}

export interface Resource {
  resourceId: string;
  resourceName: string;
  resourceLink: string;
  sharedAt: Date;
}

export interface EmotionAnalysis {
  emotion: string;
  confidence: number;
  timestamp: Date;
}

export interface PredictivePerformance {
  predictedGrade: string;
  confidence: number;
  keyLearningAreas: string[];
}

export interface CollaborativeSession {
  sessionId: string;
  sessionStart: Date;
  sessionEnd: Date;
  participantCount: number;
  sessionNotes: string;
}

const teachingSchema = new Schema<ITeaching>({
  userId: { type: String, required: true },
  studentProgress: {
    type: Object,
    required: true,
    default: { totalLessonsCompleted: 0, currentLesson: '', performanceMetrics: { accuracy: 0, timeSpent: 0 } },
  },
  lessonPlans: { type: [{ planId: String, subject: String, learningObjectives: [String], resources: [String], schedule: Date }], default: [] },
  resourcesShared: { type: [{ resourceId: String, resourceName: String, resourceLink: String, sharedAt: Date }], default: [] },
  orchestratorStatus: { type: String, default: 'Inactive' },
  emotionAnalysis: { type: { emotion: String, confidence: Number, timestamp: Date }, default: null },
  predictivePerformance: { type: { predictedGrade: String, confidence: Number, keyLearningAreas: [String] }, default: null },
  adaptiveContent: { type: [String], default: [] },
  collaborativeSessions: { type: [{ sessionId: String, sessionStart: Date, sessionEnd: Date, participantCount: Number, sessionNotes: String }], default: [] },
}, { timestamps: true });

export const Teaching = model<ITeaching>('Teaching', teachingSchema);




TeachingController (teaching.controller.ts)

This controller handles HTTP requests related to teaching activities like fetching student progress, creating lesson plans, sharing resources, and more.

typescript

Copy code

import { Controller, Get, Post, Body, Param, HttpException, HttpStatus } from '@nestjs/common';
import { TeachingService } from './teachingService';
import { StudentProgress } from './interfaces/studentProgress.interface';
import { CreateLessonDto } from './dto/createLesson.dto';
import { ShareResourceDto } from './dto/shareResource.dto';
import { PredictPerformanceDto } from './dto/predictPerformance.dto';

@Controller('teaching')
export class TeachingController {
  constructor(private readonly teachingService: TeachingService) {}

  @Get('progress/:userId')
  async getStudentProgress(@Param('userId') userId: string): Promise<StudentProgress> {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.getStudentProgress(userId);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('lesson-plan')
  async createLessonPlan(@Body() lessonPlanData: CreateLessonDto) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.createLessonPlan(lessonPlanData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('share-resource')
  async shareResource(@Body() resourceData: ShareResourceDto) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.shareResource(resourceData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('real-time-analytics')
  async getRealTimeAnalytics(@Body() sessionData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.getRealTimeAnalytics(sessionData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('collaborative-session')
  async startCollaborativeSession(@Body() sessionData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.startCollaborativeSession(sessionData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('predict-performance')
  async predictStudentPerformance(@Body() predictData: PredictPerformanceDto) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.predictStudentPerformance(predictData.userId);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('adjust-teaching-strategy')
  async adjustTeachingStrategy(@Body() sessionData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.adjustTeachingStrategy(sessionData.userId, sessionData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('analyze-emotion')
  async analyzeEmotion(@Body() imageData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.analyzeEmotion(imageData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('provide-text-feedback')
  async provideTextFeedback(@Body() studentText: string) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.provideTextFeedback(studentText);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('analyze-voice')
  async analyzeVoice(@Body() audioData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.analyzeVoice(audioData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('generate-adaptive-content')
  async generateAdaptiveContent(@Body() studentProgress: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.generateAdaptiveContent(studentProgress);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }
}




TeachingService (teachingService.ts)

This service interacts with multiple AI-powered tools for student performance prediction, emotion recognition, voice analysis, and adaptive content generation, enhancing the teaching experience.

typescript

Copy code

import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { Teaching } from './teachingModel';
import { AIService } from './aiService';
import { SwarmOrchestratorService } from './swarmOrchestratorService';
import { StudentProgress } from './interfaces/studentProgress.interface';
import { ReinforcementLearningService } from './reinforcementLearningService';
import { PredictiveAnalyticsService } from './predictiveAnalyticsService';
import { EmotionRecognitionService } from './emotionRecognitionService';
import { NLPFeedbackService } from './nlpFeedbackService';
import { VoiceRecognitionService } from './voiceRecognitionService';
import { AdaptiveContentService } from './adaptiveContentService';

@Injectable()
export class TeachingService {
  constructor(
    private readonly aiService: AIService,
    private readonly swarmOrchestratorService: SwarmOrchestratorService,
    private readonly reinforcementLearningService: ReinforcementLearningService,
    private readonly predictiveAnalyticsService: PredictiveAnalyticsService,
    private readonly emotionRecognitionService: EmotionRecognitionService,
    private readonly nlpFeedbackService: NLPFeedbackService,
    private readonly voiceRecognitionService: VoiceRecognitionService,
    private readonly adaptiveContentService: AdaptiveContentService,
  ) {}

  async getStudentProgress(userId: string): Promise<StudentProgress> {
    const dashboard = await Teaching.findOne({ userId });
    if (!dashboard) throw new Error('Teaching data not found');
    return dashboard.studentProgress as StudentProgress;
  }

  async createLessonPlan(lessonPlanData: any) {
    try {
      const lessonPlan = await this.aiService.generateLessonPlan(lessonPlanData);
      return lessonPlan;
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to create lesson plan');
    }
  }

  async shareResource(resourceData: any) {
    try {
      return await Teaching.findOneAndUpdate(
        { userId: resourceData.userId },
        { $push: { resourcesShared: resourceData } },
        { new: true }
      );
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to share resource');
    }
  }

  async getRealTimeAnalytics(sessionData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.swarmOrchestratorService.getRealTimeAnalytics(sessionData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to retrieve real-time analytics');
    }
  }

  async startCollaborativeSession(sessionData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.swarmOrchestratorService.startCollaborativeSession(sessionData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to start collaborative session');
    }
  }

  async predictStudentPerformance(userId: string) {
    try {
      return await this.predictiveAnalyticsService.predictPerformance(userId);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to predict student performance');
    }
  }

  async adjustTeachingStrategy(userId: string, sessionData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.reinforcementLearningService.adjustTeachingStrategy(userId, sessionData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to adjust teaching strategy');
    }
  }

  async analyzeEmotion(imageData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.emotionRecognitionService.analyzeEmotion(imageData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to analyze emotion');
    }
  }

  async provideTextFeedback(studentText: string) {
    try {
      return await this.nlpFeedbackService.provideFeedback(studentText);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to provide feedback');
    }
  }

  async analyzeVoice(audioData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.voiceRecognitionService.analyzeVoice(audioData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to analyze voice');
    }
  }

  async generateAdaptiveContent(studentProgress: any) {
    try {
      return await this.adaptiveContentService.generateAdaptiveContent(studentProgress);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to generate adaptive content');
    }
  }
}

Key Components Summary:

TeachingController: Manages teaching-related HTTP requests, including student progress, lesson plans, resources, real-time analytics, emotion analysis, and more.

TeachingService: Provides business logic for teaching activities, integrating with various AI services like emotion analysis, voice recognition, and reinforcement learning.

AI Tools: Integrated with AI-driven lesson planning, predictive performance analytics, and swarm intelligence for real-time classroom management.

This structure will allow the platform to offer a personalized, dynamic, and intelligent teaching experience by leveraging AI for both student and teacher support.

1. AIService (aiService.ts)

This service now uses OpenAI GPT-4 to generate lesson plans and provides real-world, practical functionality.

typescript

Copy code

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class AIService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(AIService.name);

  async generateLessonPlan(lessonPlanData: any): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('https://api.openai.com/v1/completions', {
        model: 'gpt-4',
        prompt: `Create a lesson plan for ${lessonPlanData.subject} with the following learning objectives: ${lessonPlanData.learningObjectives.join(', ')}.`,
        max_tokens: 500,
      }, {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY}`,
        }
      });

      return response.data.choices[0].text.trim();
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error generating lesson plan', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to generate lesson plan');
    }
  }
}




2. SwarmOrchestratorService (swarmOrchestratorService.ts)

This service integrates real-time collaboration using WebSocket and a custom swarm intelligence API.

typescript

Copy code

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';
import * as WebSocket from 'ws';

@Injectable()
export class SwarmOrchestratorService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(SwarmOrchestratorService.name);

  // Real-time analytics (example using a swarm intelligence platform API)
  async getRealTimeAnalytics(sessionData: any): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('https://api.swarm-platform.com/analytics', sessionData, {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${process.env.SWARM_API_KEY}`,
        }
      });
      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error fetching real-time analytics', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to fetch real-time analytics');
    }
  }

  // Starting a collaborative swarm session via WebSocket
  startCollaborativeSession(sessionData: any): WebSocket {
    const socket = new WebSocket('wss://collaboration-platform.com/socket', {
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${process.env.COLLAB_API_KEY}`,
      }
    });

    socket.on('open', () => {
      socket.send(JSON.stringify({ action: 'start', data: sessionData }));
    });

    socket.on('message', (message: string) => {
      this.logger.log('Received message:', message);
    });

    socket.on('error', (error) => {
      this.logger.error('WebSocket error', error);
    });

    socket.on('close', () => {
      this.logger.log('WebSocket connection closed');
    });

    return socket;
  }
}




3. ReinforcementLearningService (reinforcementLearningService.ts)

This service integrates reinforcement learning using Google Cloud AI Platform.

typescript

Copy code

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class ReinforcementLearningService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(ReinforcementLearningService.name);

  async adjustTeachingStrategy(userId: string, sessionData: any): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('https://us-central1-ml.googleapis.com/v1/projects/my-project-id/models/adjust-strategy:predict', {
        instances: [
          { userId, sessionData }
        ]
      }, {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${process.env.GCP_API_KEY}`,
        }
      });
      return response.data.predictions;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error adjusting teaching strategy', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to adjust teaching strategy');
    }
  }
}




4. PredictiveAnalyticsService (predictiveAnalyticsService.ts)

This service leverages Azure Machine Learning for predictive analytics.

typescript

Copy code

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class PredictiveAnalyticsService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(PredictiveAnalyticsService.name);

  async predictPerformance(userId: string): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('https://api.cognitive.microsoft.com/forecast/predict', {
        modelId: 'student-performance-model',
        data: { userId }
      }, {
        headers: {
          'Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key': process.env.AZURE_PREDICT_API_KEY,
        }
      });

      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error predicting student performance', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to predict student performance');
    }
  }
}




5. EmotionRecognitionService (emotionRecognitionService.ts)

This service integrates Microsoft Azure’s Emotion API for real-time emotion recognition.

typescript

Copy code

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class EmotionRecognitionService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(EmotionRecognitionService.name);

  async analyzeEmotion(imageData: Buffer): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('https://westus.api.cognitive.microsoft.com/emotion/v1.0/recognize', imageData, {
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/octet-stream',
          'Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key': process.env.AZURE_EMOTION_API_KEY,
        }
      });

      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error analyzing emotion', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to analyze emotion');
    }
  }
}

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class NLPFeedbackService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(NLPFeedbackService.name);

  async provideFeedback(studentText: string): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('https://api.openai.com/v1/completions', {
        model: 'gpt-4',
        prompt: `Provide constructive feedback on the following student text: "${studentText}"`,
        max_tokens: 150,
      }, {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY}`,
        }
      });

      return response.data.choices[0].text.trim();
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error providing feedback', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to provide feedback');
    }
  }
}




7. VoiceRecognitionService (voiceRecognitionService.ts)

This service uses Google Cloud Speech-to-Text API for speech recognition.

typescript

Copy code

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class VoiceRecognitionService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(VoiceRecognitionService.name);

  async analyzeVoice(audioData: any): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('https://speech.googleapis.com/v1/speech:recognize', {
        config: {
          encoding: 'LINEAR16',
          sampleRateHertz: 16000,
          languageCode: 'en-US',
        },
        audio: {
          content: audioData.toString('base64'),
        },
      }, {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${process.env.GOOGLE_API_KEY}`,
        }
      });

      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error analyzing voice', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to analyze voice');
    }
  }
}

studentProgress.interface.ts

This interface defines the structure for student progress data.

typescript

Copy code

export interface StudentProgress {
  userId: string;
  subject: string;
  currentLevel: number;
  performanceData: PerformanceData;
  lastCompletedLesson: string;
  timeSpentOnLessons: number; // in minutes
}

interface PerformanceData {
  accuracy: number; // % of correct answers
  engagementLevel: number; // on a scale of 0 to 10
  quizScores: number[];
}


Here is the regenerated version of the components:



1. LessonPlanComponent.tsx

This component allows users to request AI-generated lesson plans from the backend. It communicates with the AIService via an API call.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const LessonPlanComponent = () => {
  const [lessonData, setLessonData] = useState({
    subject: '',
    learningObjectives: [''],
  });
  const [generatedLessonPlan, setGeneratedLessonPlan] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  const handleGenerateLessonPlan = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('/api/ai/lesson-plan', lessonData);
      setGeneratedLessonPlan(response.data.lessonPlan);
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Error generating lesson plan.');
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  const handleInputChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>, index: number) => {
    const { name, value } = e.target;
    const updatedLessonData = { ...lessonData };
    if (name === 'subject') {
      updatedLessonData.subject = value;
    } else if (name === 'learningObjectives') {
      updatedLessonData.learningObjectives[index] = value;
    }
    setLessonData(updatedLessonData);
  };

  const addLearningObjective = () => {
    setLessonData({
      ...lessonData,
      learningObjectives: [...lessonData.learningObjectives, ''],
    });
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Generate AI Lesson Plan</h2>
      <input
        type="text"
        name="subject"
        placeholder="Subject"
        value={lessonData.subject}
        onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, -1)}
      />
      <div>
        {lessonData.learningObjectives.map((objective, index) => (
          <input
            key={index}
            type="text"
            name="learningObjectives"
            placeholder={`Learning Objective ${index + 1}`}
            value={objective}
            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, index)}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
      <button onClick={addLearningObjective}>Add Learning Objective</button>
      <button onClick={handleGenerateLessonPlan} disabled={loading}>
        {loading ? 'Generating...' : 'Generate Lesson Plan'}
      </button>
      {error && <p style={{ color: 'red' }}>{error}</p>}
      {generatedLessonPlan && (
        <div>
          <h3>Generated Lesson Plan</h3>
          <pre>{generatedLessonPlan}</pre>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default LessonPlanComponent;




2. CollaborativeSessionComponent.tsx

This component manages the real-time collaboration using WebSockets with the backend.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const CollaborativeSessionComponent = () => {
  const [sessionData, setSessionData] = useState({});
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [socket, setSocket] = useState<WebSocket | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Initialize WebSocket on component mount
    const newSocket = new WebSocket('wss://collaboration-platform.com/socket', {
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${process.env.REACT_APP_COLLAB_API_KEY}`,
      }
    });

    newSocket.onopen = () => {
      console.log('WebSocket connection established');
    };

    newSocket.onmessage = (message) => {
      setMessages((prevMessages) => [...prevMessages, message.data]);
    };

    newSocket.onerror = (error) => {
      console.error('WebSocket error:', error);
    };

    newSocket.onclose = () => {
      console.log('WebSocket connection closed');
    };

    setSocket(newSocket);

    return () => {
      newSocket.close();
    };
  }, []);

  const startCollaborativeSession = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await axios.post('/api/swarm/start-session', sessionData);
      if (socket) {
        socket.send(JSON.stringify({ action: 'start', data: sessionData }));
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error starting collaborative session:', err);
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Start Collaborative Session</h2>
      <button onClick={startCollaborativeSession} disabled={loading}>
        {loading ? 'Starting...' : 'Start Session'}
      </button>
      <div>
        <h3>Messages</h3>
        <ul>
          {messages.map((message, index) => (
            <li key={index}>{message}</li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default CollaborativeSessionComponent;

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const StudentPerformancePredictionComponent = () => {
  const [userId, setUserId] = useState('');
  const [prediction, setPrediction] = useState<any>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  const handlePredictPerformance = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('/api/predict-performance', { userId });
      setPrediction(response.data);
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Error predicting student performance.');
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Predict Student Performance</h2>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={userId}
        onChange={(e) => setUserId(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Student ID"
      />
      <button onClick={handlePredictPerformance} disabled={loading}>
        {loading ? 'Predicting...' : 'Predict Performance'}
      </button>
      {error && <p style={{ color: 'red' }}>{error}</p>}
      {prediction && (
        <div>
          <h3>Prediction Result</h3>
          <pre>{JSON.stringify(prediction, null, 2)}</pre>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

4. EmotionRecognitionComponent.tsx

This component handles real-time emotion recognition using webcam input.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const EmotionRecognitionComponent = () => {
  const [emotionData, setEmotionData] = useState<any>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  const captureImageAndAnalyze = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      // Capture webcam image and send to backend for emotion analysis
      const imageData = await captureImageFromWebcam();
      const response = await axios.post('/api/emotion/analyze', imageData);
      setEmotionData(response.data);
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Error recognizing emotion.');
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  const captureImageFromWebcam = () => {
    // Capture image logic (could use WebRTC, Canvas API, etc.)
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      const video = document.createElement('video');
      navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ video: true })
        .then((stream) => {
          video.srcObject = stream;
          video.play();
          setTimeout(() => {
            canvas.width = video.videoWidth;
            canvas.height = video.videoHeight;
            canvas.getContext('2d')?.drawImage(video, 0, 0);
            const imageData = canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg');
            resolve(imageData);
          }, 1000);
        })
        .catch(reject);
    });
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Emotion Recognition</h2>
      <button onClick={captureImageAndAnalyze} disabled={loading}>
        {loading ? 'Analyzing...' : 'Analyze Emotion'}
      </button>
      {error && <p style={{ color: 'red' }}>{error}</p>}
      {emotionData && (
        <div>
          <h3>Emotion Analysis</h3>
          <pre>{JSON.stringify(emotionData, null, 2)}</pre>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default EmotionRecognitionComponent;

TextAnalysisComponent.tsx
This component analyzes student-written texts for understanding, grammar, and overall quality.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const TextAnalysisComponent = () => {
  const [text, setText] = useState<string>('');
  const [analysisResult, setAnalysisResult] = useState<any>(null);

  const handleTextChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLTextAreaElement>) => {
    setText(event.target.value);
  };

  const analyzeText = async () => {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('/api/text/analysis', { text });
      setAnalysisResult(response.data);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error analyzing text', error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="text-analysis-container">
      <h3>Text Analysis</h3>
      <textarea
        value={text}
        onChange={handleTextChange}
        rows={5}
        placeholder="Write or paste text here..."
      ></textarea>
      <button onClick={analyzeText}>Analyze</button>
      {analysisResult && (
        <div>
          <h4>Analysis Results</h4>
          <p>Grammar Score: {analysisResult.grammarScore}</p>
          <p>Understanding: {analysisResult.understanding}</p>
          <p>Suggestions: {analysisResult.suggestions}</p>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default TextAnalysisComponent;




PeerTutoringComponent.tsx
This component facilitates peer-to-peer tutoring where students can help each other with academic queries.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const PeerTutoringComponent = () => {
  const [tutorList, setTutorList] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [tutorRequest, setTutorRequest] = useState<string>('');

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchTutors = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await axios.get('/api/peer-tutoring/tutors');
        setTutorList(response.data);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching tutor list', error);
      }
    };
    fetchTutors();
  }, []);

  const handleRequestTutor = async () => {
    try {
      await axios.post('/api/peer-tutoring/request', { query: tutorRequest });
      alert('Tutor request sent!');
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error requesting tutor', error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="peer-tutoring-container">
      <h3>Peer Tutoring</h3>
      <div>
        <h4>Available Tutors</h4>
        <ul>
          {tutorList.map((tutor, index) => (
            <li key={index}>{tutor.name}</li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
      <textarea
        value={tutorRequest}
        onChange={(e) => setTutorRequest(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Describe your question or query"
      />
      <button onClick={handleRequestTutor}>Request a Tutor</button>
    </div>
  );
};

export default PeerTutoringComponent;




SpeechToTextComponent.tsx
This component converts speech to text in real-time using the Web Speech API.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const SpeechToTextComponent = () => {
  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState<string>('');
  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState<boolean>(false);

  const startListening = () => {
    const recognition = new (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition();
    recognition.lang = 'en-US';
    recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {
      const newTranscript = event.results[0][0].transcript;
      setTranscript(newTranscript);
    };
    recognition.start();
    setIsListening(true);
  };

  const stopListening = () => {
    const recognition = new (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition();
    recognition.stop();
    setIsListening(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Speech-to-Text</h3>
      <button onClick={startListening} disabled={isListening}>
        Start Listening
      </button>
      <button onClick={stopListening} disabled={!isListening}>
        Stop Listening
      </button>
      <p>Transcript: {transcript}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

export default SpeechToTextComponent;

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const VoiceFeedbackComponent = () => {
  const [text, setText] = useState<string>('');
  const [feedback, setFeedback] = useState<string>('');

  const handleTextChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    setText(e.target.value);
  };

  const provideFeedback = () => {
    const feedbackMessage = `You said: ${text}`;
    setFeedback(feedbackMessage);
    const speech = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(feedbackMessage);
    speechSynthesis.speak(speech);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Voice Feedback</h3>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={text}
        onChange={handleTextChange}
        placeholder="Say something"
      />
      <button onClick={provideFeedback}>Provide Feedback</button>
      {feedback && <p>{feedback}</p>}
    </div>
  );
};

export default VoiceFeedbackComponent;




PeerReviewComponent.tsx
This component allows students to peer review each other’s work.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const PeerReviewComponent = () => {
  const [workList, setWorkList] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [reviewText, setReviewText] = useState<string>('');
  const [selectedWork, setSelectedWork] = useState<any>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchWorkList = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await axios.get('/api/peer-review/work');
        setWorkList(response.data);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching work list', error);
      }
    };
    fetchWorkList();
  }, []);

  const handleSelectWork = (work: any) => {
    setSelectedWork(work);
  };

  const handleSubmitReview = async () => {
    try {
      await axios.post('/api/peer-review/submit', { reviewText, workId: selectedWork.id });
      alert('Review submitted!');
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error submitting review', error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Peer Review</h3>
      <div>
        <h4>Select Work to Review</h4>
        <ul>
          {workList.map((work, index) => (
            <li key={index} onClick={() => handleSelectWork(work)}>
              {work.title}
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
      {selectedWork && (
        <div>
          <h4>Review {selectedWork.title}</h4>
          <textarea
            value={reviewText}
            onChange={(e) => setReviewText(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Write your review here..."
          />
          <button onClick={handleSubmitReview}>Submit Review</button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default PeerReviewComponent;

1. PersonalizedFeedbackComponent.tsx

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const PersonalizedFeedbackComponent = () => {
  const [userProgress, setUserProgress] = useState<any>(null);
  const [feedback, setFeedback] = useState<string>('');

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchProgress = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await axios.get('/api/user/progress');
        setUserProgress(response.data);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching user progress', error);
      }
    };
    fetchProgress();
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (userProgress) {
      const feedbackMessage = `You have completed ${userProgress.completedLessons} out of ${userProgress.totalLessons}. Keep it up!`;
      setFeedback(feedbackMessage);
    }
  }, [userProgress]);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Personalized Feedback</h3>
      <p>{feedback}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

export default PersonalizedFeedbackComponent;

const GamificationComponent = () => {

  useEffect(() => {

        setBadges(response.data.badges);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching gamification data', error);
      }

    fetchGamificationData();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Gamification</h3>

        <h4>Badges</h4>

3. VoiceRecognitionComponent.tsx

This component uses voice recognition technology to interpret student responses and provide real-time feedback.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const VoiceRecognitionComponent = () => {
  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState<string>('');
  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState<boolean>(false);

  const startListening = () => {
    const recognition = new (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition();
    recognition.lang = 'en-US';
    recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {
      const newTranscript = event.results[0][0].transcript;
      setTranscript(newTranscript);
    };
    recognition.start();
    setIsListening(true);
  };

  const stopListening = () => {
    const recognition = new (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition();
    recognition.stop();
    setIsListening(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Voice Recognition</h3>
      <button onClick={startListening} disabled={isListening}>Start Listening</button>
      <button onClick={stopListening} disabled={!isListening}>Stop Listening</button>
      <p>Transcript: {transcript}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

export default VoiceRecognitionComponent;

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const VideoConferencingComponent = () => {
  const [isConnected, setIsConnected] = useState<boolean>(false);
  const [videoUrl, setVideoUrl] = useState<string>('');

  const startVideoCall = () => {
    // Start video call logic, could use WebRTC or third-party APIs (e.g., Zoom, WebEx)
    setVideoUrl('https://somevideoconferencingplatform.com/meetingroom');
    setIsConnected(true);
  };

  const stopVideoCall = () => {
    setVideoUrl('');
    setIsConnected(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Video Conferencing</h3>
      {!isConnected ? (
        <button onClick={startVideoCall}>Start Video Call</button>
      ) : (
        <>
          <p>You're connected to the video call!</p>
          <iframe src={videoUrl} title="Video Call" width="600" height="400"></iframe>
          <button onClick={stopVideoCall}>End Call</button>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default VideoConferencingComponent;

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const AIAgentsComponent = () => {
  const [agentMessage, setAgentMessage] = useState<string>('');
  const [isInteracting, setIsInteracting] = useState<boolean>(false);

  const interactWithAgent = async () => {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('/api/ai/agent-interaction', { message: agentMessage });
      setAgentMessage(response.data.reply);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error interacting with agent', error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>AI Agents</h3>
      <textarea
        value={agentMessage}
        onChange={(e) => setAgentMessage(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Ask the AI agent a question"
      />
      <button onClick={interactWithAgent}>Send</button>
      {isInteracting && <p>AI Agent: {agentMessage}</p>}
    </div>
  );
};
