1. Backend

1.1. Teaching Data Model (teaching.model.ts)

Create backend/src/teaching/teaching.model.ts:

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface ITeaching extends Document {
  userId: string;
  studentProgress: {
    totalLessonsCompleted: number;
    currentLesson: string;
    performanceMetrics: { accuracy: number; timeSpent: number };
  };
  lessonPlans: {
    planId: string;
    subject: string;
    learningObjectives: string[];
    resources: string[];
    schedule: Date;
  }[];
  resourcesShared: {
    resourceId: string;
    resourceName: string;
    resourceLink: string;
    sharedAt: Date;
  }[];
  orchestratorStatus: string;
  emotionAnalysis: {
    emotion: string;
    confidence: number;
    timestamp: Date;
  } | null;
  predictivePerformance: {
    predictedGrade: string;
    confidence: number;
    keyLearningAreas: string[];
  } | null;
  adaptiveContent: string[];
  collaborativeSessions: {
    sessionId: string;
    sessionStart: Date;
    sessionEnd: Date;
    participantCount: number;
    sessionNotes: string;
  }[];
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

const teachingSchema = new Schema<ITeaching>(
  {
    userId: { type: String, required: true },
    studentProgress: {
      type: Object,
      required: true,
      default: {
        totalLessonsCompleted: 0,
        currentLesson: '',
        performanceMetrics: { accuracy: 0, timeSpent: 0 },
      },
    },
    lessonPlans: {
      type: [
        {
          planId: String,
          subject: String,
          learningObjectives: [String],
          resources: [String],
          schedule: Date,
        },
      ],
      default: [],
    },
    resourcesShared: {
      type: [
        {
          resourceId: String,
          resourceName: String,
          resourceLink: String,
          sharedAt: Date,
        },
      ],
      default: [],
    },
    orchestratorStatus: { type: String, default: 'Inactive' },
    emotionAnalysis: {
      type: { emotion: String, confidence: Number, timestamp: Date },
      default: null,
    },
    predictivePerformance: {
      type: {
        predictedGrade: String,
        confidence: Number,
        keyLearningAreas: [String],
      },
      default: null,
    },
    adaptiveContent: { type: [String], default: [] },
    collaborativeSessions: {
      type: [
        {
          sessionId: String,
          sessionStart: Date,
          sessionEnd: Date,
          participantCount: Number,
          sessionNotes: String,
        },
      ],
      default: [],
    },
  },
  { timestamps: true }
);

export const Teaching = model<ITeaching>('Teaching', teachingSchema);




1.2. Teaching Controller (teaching.controller.ts)

Create backend/src/teaching/teaching.controller.ts:

import {
  Controller,
  Get,
  Post,
  Body,
  Param,
  HttpException,
  HttpStatus,
} from '@nestjs/common';
import { TeachingService } from './teaching.service';

@Controller('teaching')
export class TeachingController {
  constructor(private readonly teachingService: TeachingService) {}

  @Get('progress/:userId')
  async getStudentProgress(@Param('userId') userId: string) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.getStudentProgress(userId);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('lesson-plan')
  async createLessonPlan(@Body() lessonPlanData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.createLessonPlan(lessonPlanData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('share-resource')
  async shareResource(@Body() resourceData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.shareResource(resourceData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('real-time-analytics')
  async getRealTimeAnalytics(@Body() sessionData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.getRealTimeAnalytics(sessionData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('collaborative-session')
  async startCollaborativeSession(@Body() sessionData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.startCollaborativeSession(sessionData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('predict-performance')
  async predictStudentPerformance(@Body() predictData: { userId: string }) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.predictStudentPerformance(
        predictData.userId
      );
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('adjust-teaching-strategy')
  async adjustTeachingStrategy(@Body() sessionData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.adjustTeachingStrategy(
        sessionData.userId,
        sessionData
      );
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('analyze-emotion')
  async analyzeEmotion(@Body() imageData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.analyzeEmotion(imageData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('provide-text-feedback')
  async provideTextFeedback(@Body() studentText: string) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.provideTextFeedback(studentText);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('analyze-voice')
  async analyzeVoice(@Body() audioData: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.analyzeVoice(audioData);
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }

  @Post('generate-adaptive-content')
  async generateAdaptiveContent(@Body() studentProgress: any) {
    try {
      return await this.teachingService.generateAdaptiveContent(
        studentProgress
      );
    } catch (error) {
      throw new HttpException(error.message, HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST);
    }
  }
}




1.3. Teaching Service (teaching.service.ts)

Create backend/src/teaching/teaching.service.ts:

import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { Teaching } from './teaching.model';
import { AIService } from './services/ai.service';
import { SwarmOrchestratorService } from './services/swarm-orchestrator.service';
import { ReinforcementLearningService } from './services/reinforcement-learning.service';
import { PredictiveAnalyticsService } from './services/predictive-analytics.service';
import { EmotionRecognitionService } from './services/emotion-recognition.service';
import { NLPFeedbackService } from './services/nlp-feedback.service';
import { VoiceRecognitionService } from './services/voice-recognition.service';
import { AdaptiveContentService } from './services/adaptive-content.service';

@Injectable()
export class TeachingService {
  constructor(
    private readonly aiService: AIService,
    private readonly swarmOrchestratorService: SwarmOrchestratorService,
    private readonly reinforcementLearningService: ReinforcementLearningService,
    private readonly predictiveAnalyticsService: PredictiveAnalyticsService,
    private readonly emotionRecognitionService: EmotionRecognitionService,
    private readonly nlpFeedbackService: NLPFeedbackService,
    private readonly voiceRecognitionService: VoiceRecognitionService,
    private readonly adaptiveContentService: AdaptiveContentService
  ) {}

  async getStudentProgress(userId: string) {
    const record = await Teaching.findOne({ userId });
    return record?.studentProgress || {};
  }

  async createLessonPlan(lessonPlanData: any) {
    return this.aiService.generateLessonPlan(lessonPlanData);
  }

  async shareResource(resourceData: any) {
    return Teaching.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId: resourceData.userId },
      { $push: { resourcesShared: resourceData } },
      { new: true }
    );
  }

  async getRealTimeAnalytics(sessionData: any) {
    return this.swarmOrchestratorService.getRealTimeAnalytics(sessionData);
  }

  async startCollaborativeSession(sessionData: any) {
    return this.swarmOrchestratorService.startCollaborativeSession(sessionData);
  }

  async predictStudentPerformance(userId: string) {
    return this.predictiveAnalyticsService.predictPerformance(userId);
  }

  async adjustTeachingStrategy(userId: string, sessionData: any) {
    return this.reinforcementLearningService.adjustTeachingStrategy(
      userId,
      sessionData
    );
  }

  async analyzeEmotion(imageData: any) {
    return this.emotionRecognitionService.analyzeEmotion(imageData);
  }

  async provideTextFeedback(studentText: string) {
    return this.nlpFeedbackService.provideFeedback(studentText);
  }

  async analyzeVoice(audioData: any) {
    return this.voiceRecognitionService.analyzeVoice(audioData);
  }

  async generateAdaptiveContent(studentProgress: any) {
    return this.adaptiveContentService.generateAdaptiveContent(
      studentProgress
    );
  }
}




1.4. AI Services (in backend/src/teaching/services/)

AIService (ai.service.ts):

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class AIService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(AIService.name);

  async generateLessonPlan(data: {
    subject: string;
    learningObjectives: string[];
  }): Promise<string> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(
        'https://api.openai.com/v1/completions',
        {
          model: 'gpt-4',
          prompt: `Create a lesson plan for ${data.subject} with objectives: ${data.learningObjectives.join(
            ', '
          )}.`,
          max_tokens: 500,
        },
        {
          headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY}` },
        }
      );
      return response.data.choices[0].text.trim();
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error generating lesson plan', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to generate lesson plan');
    }
  }
}


SwarmOrchestratorService (swarm-orchestrator.service.ts):

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';
import * as WebSocket from 'ws';

@Injectable()
export class SwarmOrchestratorService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(SwarmOrchestratorService.name);

  async getRealTimeAnalytics(sessionData: any): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(
        'https://api.swarm-platform.com/analytics',
        sessionData,
        { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.SWARM_API_KEY}` } }
      );
      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error fetching real-time analytics', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to fetch real-time analytics');
    }
  }

  startCollaborativeSession(sessionData: any): WebSocket {
    const socket = new WebSocket('wss://collaboration-platform.com/socket', {
      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.COLLAB_API_KEY}` },
    });

    socket.on('open', () =>
      socket.send(JSON.stringify({ action: 'start', data: sessionData }))
    );
    socket.on('message', (msg) => this.logger.log(`WS message: ${msg}`));
    socket.on('error', (err) => this.logger.error('WebSocket error', err));
    socket.on('close', () => this.logger.log('WebSocket closed'));
    return socket;
  }
}


ReinforcementLearningService (reinforcement-learning.service.ts):

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class ReinforcementLearningService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(ReinforcementLearningService.name);

  async adjustTeachingStrategy(
    userId: string,
    sessionData: any
  ): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(
        'https://us-central1-ml.googleapis.com/v1/projects/my-project-id/models/adjust-strategy:predict',
        { instances: [{ userId, sessionData }] },
        { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.GCP_API_KEY}` } }
      );
      return response.data.predictions;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error adjusting teaching strategy', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to adjust teaching strategy');
    }
  }
}


PredictiveAnalyticsService (predictive-analytics.service.ts):

@Injectable()
export class PredictiveAnalyticsService {

  async predictPerformance(userId: string): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(
        'https://api.cognitive.microsoft.com/forecast/predict',
        { modelId: 'student-performance-model', data: { userId } },
        { headers: { 'Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key': process.env.AZURE_PREDICT_API_KEY } }
      );
      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error predicting student performance', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to predict student performance');
    }
  }
}

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';

@Injectable()
export class EmotionRecognitionService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(EmotionRecognitionService.name);

  async analyzeEmotion(imageData: Buffer): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(
        'https://westus.api.cognitive.microsoft.com/emotion/v1.0/recognize',
        imageData,
        {
          headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'application/octet-stream',
            'Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key': process.env.AZURE_EMOTION_API_KEY,
          },
        }
      );
      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error analyzing emotion', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to analyze emotion');
    }
  }
}

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';

@Injectable()
export class NLPFeedbackService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(NLPFeedbackService.name);

  async provideFeedback(studentText: string): Promise<string> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(
        'https://api.openai.com/v1/completions',
        {
          model: 'gpt-4',
          prompt: `Provide constructive feedback on the following student text: "${studentText}"`,
          max_tokens: 150,
        },
        { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY}` } }
      );
      return response.data.choices[0].text.trim();
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error providing feedback', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to provide feedback');
    }
  }
}


VoiceRecognitionService (voice-recognition.service.ts):

import { Injectable, Logger } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class VoiceRecognitionService {
  private readonly logger = new Logger(VoiceRecognitionService.name);

  async analyzeVoice(audioData: Buffer): Promise<any> {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(
        'https://speech.googleapis.com/v1/speech:recognize',
        {
          config: { encoding: 'LINEAR16', sampleRateHertz: 16000, languageCode: 'en-US' },
          audio: { content: audioData.toString('base64') },
        },
        { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.GOOGLE_API_KEY}` } }
      );
      return response.data;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Error analyzing voice', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to analyze voice');
    }
  }
}

2. Frontend (React + Vite)

Create frontend-vite/src/components/teaching/ and add:

2.1. LessonPlanComponent (LessonPlanComponent.tsx)

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const LessonPlanComponent = () => {
  const [lessonData, setLessonData] = useState({
    subject: '',
    learningObjectives: [''],
  });
  const [generatedLessonPlan, setGeneratedLessonPlan] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  const handleGenerateLessonPlan = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('/teaching/lesson-plan', lessonData);
      setGeneratedLessonPlan(response.data);
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Error generating lesson plan.');
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  const handleInputChange = (
    e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>,
    index: number
  ) => {
    const { name, value } = e.target;
    const updatedLessonData = { ...lessonData };
    if (name === 'subject') {
      updatedLessonData.subject = value;
    } else if (name === 'learningObjectives') {
      updatedLessonData.learningObjectives[index] = value;
    }
    setLessonData(updatedLessonData);
  };

  const addLearningObjective = () => {
    setLessonData({
      ...lessonData,
      learningObjectives: [...lessonData.learningObjectives, ''],
    });
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Generate AI Lesson Plan</h2>
      <input
        type="text"
        name="subject"
        placeholder="Subject"
        value={lessonData.subject}
        onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, -1)}
      />
      <div>
        {lessonData.learningObjectives.map((objective, idx) => (
          <input
            key={idx}
            type="text"
            name="learningObjectives"
            placeholder={`Learning Objective ${idx + 1}`}
            value={objective}
            onChange={(e) => handleInputChange(e, idx)}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
      <button onClick={addLearningObjective}>Add Learning Objective</button>
      <button onClick={handleGenerateLessonPlan} disabled={loading}>
        {loading ? 'Generating...' : 'Generate Lesson Plan'}
      </button>
      {error && <p style={{ color: 'red' }}>{error}</p>}
      {generatedLessonPlan && (
        <div>
          <h3>Generated Lesson Plan</h3>
          <pre>{generatedLessonPlan}</pre>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default LessonPlanComponent;




2.2. CollaborativeSessionComponent (CollaborativeSessionComponent.tsx)

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const CollaborativeSessionComponent = () => {
  const [sessionData, setSessionData] = useState({});
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [socket, setSocket] = useState<WebSocket | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const newSocket = new WebSocket('wss://collaboration-platform.com/socket', {
      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${import.meta.env.VITE_COLLAB_API_KEY}` },
    });

    newSocket.onopen = () => console.log('WebSocket connection established');
    newSocket.onmessage = (event) =>
      setMessages((prev) => [...prev, event.data]);
    newSocket.onerror = (err) => console.error('WebSocket error:', err);
    newSocket.onclose = () => console.log('WebSocket connection closed');

    setSocket(newSocket);
    return () => newSocket.close();
  }, []);

  const startCollaborativeSession = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      await axios.post('/teaching/collaborative-session', sessionData);
      if (socket) {
        socket.send(JSON.stringify({ action: 'start', data: sessionData }));
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error starting collaborative session:', err);
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Start Collaborative Session</h2>
      <button onClick={startCollaborativeSession} disabled={loading}>
        {loading ? 'Starting...' : 'Start Session'}
      </button>
      <div>
        <h3>Messages</h3>
        <ul>
          {messages.map((msg, idx) => (
            <li key={idx}>{msg}</li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default CollaborativeSessionComponent;

2.4. EmotionRecognitionComponent (Webcam) (EmotionRecognitionComponent.tsx)

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const EmotionRecognitionComponent = () => {
  const [emotionData, setEmotionData] = useState<any>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  const captureImageAndAnalyze = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      // Capture webcam image and send to backend for emotion analysis
      const imageData = await captureImageFromWebcam();
      const response = await axios.post('/teaching/analyze-emotion', {
        image: imageData,
      });
      setEmotionData(response.data);
    } catch (err) {
      setError('Error recognizing emotion.');
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  const captureImageFromWebcam = () => {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      const video = document.createElement('video');
      navigator.mediaDevices
        .getUserMedia({ video: true })
        .then((stream) => {
          video.srcObject = stream;
          video.play();
          setTimeout(() => {
            canvas.width = video.videoWidth;
            canvas.height = video.videoHeight;
            canvas.getContext('2d')?.drawImage(video, 0, 0);
            const imageData = canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg');
            resolve(imageData);
          }, 1000);
        })
        .catch(reject);
    });
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Emotion Recognition</h2>
      <button onClick={captureImageAndAnalyze} disabled={loading}>
        {loading ? 'Analyzing...' : 'Analyze Emotion'}
      </button>
      {error && <p style={{ color: 'red' }}>{error}</p>}
      {emotionData && (
        <div>
          <h3>Emotion Analysis</h3>
          <pre>{JSON.stringify(emotionData, null, 2)}</pre>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default EmotionRecognitionComponent;

const PeerTutoringComponent = () => {

        const response = await axios.get('/api/peer-tutoring/tutors');
        setTutorList(response.data);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching tutor list', error);
      }
    };
    fetchTutors();
  }, []);

  const handleRequestTutor = async () => {
    try {
      await axios.post('/api/peer-tutoring/request', { query: tutorRequest });

      console.error('Error requesting tutor', error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="peer-tutoring-container">
      <h3>Peer Tutoring</h3>
      <div>
        <h4>Available Tutors</h4>
        <ul>
          {tutorList.map((tutor, index) => (
            <li key={index}>{tutor.name}</li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
      <textarea
        value={tutorRequest}
        onChange={(e) => setTutorRequest(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Describe your question or query"
      />

    </div>
  );

2.7. SpeechToTextComponent (SpeechToTextComponent.tsx)

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const SpeechToTextComponent = () => {
  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');
  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);

  const startListening = () => {
    const recognition = new (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition();
    recognition.lang = 'en-US';
    recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {
      const newTranscript = event.results[0][0].transcript;
      setTranscript(newTranscript);
    };
    recognition.start();
    setIsListening(true);
  };

  const stopListening = () => {
    const recognition = new (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition();
    recognition.stop();
    setIsListening(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Speech-to-Text</h3>
      <button onClick={startListening} disabled={isListening}>
        Start Listening
      </button>
      <button onClick={stopListening} disabled={!isListening}>
        Stop Listening
      </button>
      <p>Transcript: {transcript}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

export default SpeechToTextComponent;

2.9. PeerReviewComponent (PeerReviewComponent.tsx)

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const PeerReviewComponent = () => {
  const [workList, setWorkList] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [reviewText, setReviewText] = useState('');
  const [selectedWork, setSelectedWork] = useState<any>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchWorkList = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await axios.get('/api/peer-review/work');
        setWorkList(response.data);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching work list', error);
      }
    };
    fetchWorkList();
  }, []);

  const handleSelectWork = (work: any) => {
    setSelectedWork(work);
  };

  const handleSubmitReview = async () => {
    try {
      await axios.post('/api/peer-review/submit', {
        reviewText,
        workId: selectedWork.id,
      });
      alert('Review submitted!');
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error submitting review', error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Peer Review</h3>
      <div>
        <h4>Select Work to Review</h4>
        <ul>
          {workList.map((work, index) => (
            <li key={index} onClick={() => handleSelectWork(work)}>
              {work.title}
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
      {selectedWork && (
        <div>
          <h4>Review {selectedWork.title}</h4>
          <textarea
            value={reviewText}
            onChange={(e) => setReviewText(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Write your review here..."
          />
          <button onClick={handleSubmitReview}>Submit Review</button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default PeerReviewComponent;

const PersonalizedFeedbackComponent = () => {

  const [feedback, setFeedback] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchProgress = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await axios.get('/api/user/progress');
        setUserProgress(response.data);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching user progress', error);
      }
    };
    fetchProgress();
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (userProgress) {
      const feedbackMessage = `You have completed ${userProgress.completedLessons} out of ${userProgress.totalLessons}. Keep it up!`;
      setFeedback(feedbackMessage);
    }
  }, [userProgress]);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Personalized Feedback</h3>
      <p>{feedback}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

2.11. GamificationComponent (GamificationComponent.tsx)

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const GamificationComponent = () => {
  const [userScore, setUserScore] = useState(0);
  const [badges, setBadges] = useState<any[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchGamificationData = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await axios.get('/api/gamification/status');
        setUserScore(response.data.score);
        setBadges(response.data.badges);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching gamification data', error);
      }
    };
    fetchGamificationData();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Gamification</h3>
      <p>Score: {userScore}</p>
      <div>
        <h4>Badges</h4>
        <ul>
          {badges.map((badge, index) => (
            <li key={index}>{badge.name}</li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default GamificationComponent;




2.12. VoiceRecognitionComponent (VoiceRecognitionComponent.tsx)

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const VoiceRecognitionComponent = () => {
  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');
  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);

  const startListening = () => {
    const recognition = new (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition();
    recognition.lang = 'en-US';
    recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {
      const newTranscript = event.results[0][0].transcript;
      setTranscript(newTranscript);
    };
    recognition.start();
    setIsListening(true);
  };

  const stopListening = () => {
    const recognition = new (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition();
    recognition.stop();
    setIsListening(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Voice Recognition</h3>
      <button onClick={startListening} disabled={isListening}>
        Start Listening
      </button>
      <button onClick={stopListening} disabled={!isListening}>
        Stop Listening
      </button>
      <p>Transcript: {transcript}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

export default VoiceRecognitionComponent;




2.13. VideoConferencingComponent (VideoConferencingComponent.tsx)

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const VideoConferencingComponent = () => {
  const [isConnected, setIsConnected] = useState(false);
  const [videoUrl, setVideoUrl] = useState('');

  const startVideoCall = () => {
    // Start video call logic (e.g., WebRTC or third-party)
    setVideoUrl('https://somevideoconferencingplatform.com/meetingroom');
    setIsConnected(true);
  };

  const stopVideoCall = () => {
    setVideoUrl('');
    setIsConnected(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Video Conferencing</h3>
      {!isConnected ? (
        <button onClick={startVideoCall}>Start Video Call</button>
      ) : (
        <>
          <p>You're connected to the video call!</p>
          <iframe
            src={videoUrl}
            title="Video Call"
            width="600"
            height="400"
          ></iframe>
          <button onClick={stopVideoCall}>End Call</button>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default VideoConferencingComponent;

2.15. AIAgentsComponent (AIAgentsComponent.tsx)

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const AIAgentsComponent = () => {
  const [agentMessage, setAgentMessage] = useState('');
  const [isInteracting, setIsInteracting] = useState(false);

  const interactWithAgent = async () => {
    setIsInteracting(true);
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('/api/ai/agent-interaction', {
        message: agentMessage,
      });
      setAgentMessage(response.data.reply);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error interacting with agent', error);
    }
    setIsInteracting(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>AI Agents</h3>
      <textarea
        value={agentMessage}
        onChange={(e) => setAgentMessage(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Ask the AI agent a question"
      />
      <button onClick={interactWithAgent} disabled={isInteracting}>
        Send
      </button>
      {isInteracting && <p>AI Agent: {agentMessage}</p>}
    </div>
  );
};

export default AIAgentsComponent;

Phase 9: Community

Phase 9 emphasizes building a vibrant and engaging community for the Quranic Education AI Platform. This phase integrates advanced AI technologies to ensure a safe, dynamic, and collaborative user environment. Users can participate in forums, Q&A sessions, and event suggestions while benefiting from AI-driven moderation and swarm orchestration to foster a supportive and enriching space.

Objectives

Forums: Allow users to create, view, and engage in discussions.

Q&A Section: Enable users to ask and answer questions.

Event Suggestions: Facilitate collaborative event planning.

AI-Driven Content Moderation: Ensure a safe and respectful environment.

Swarm Orchestration: Dynamically manage community activity and engagement.

Seamless Integration: Provide a user-friendly interface and robust backend to support these features.



Backend Implementation

Unified Model (community.model.ts)

typescript

CopyEdit

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface ICommunityPost extends Document {
  userId: string;
  type: 'forum' | 'qanda' | 'event';
  title?: string;
  content?: string;
  question?: string;
  answer?: string;
  eventDetails?: string;
  isApproved?: boolean;
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

const communitySchema = new Schema<ICommunityPost>(
  {
    userId: { type: String, required: true },
    type: { type: String, required: true, enum: ['forum', 'qanda', 'event'] },
    title: { type: String },
    content: { type: String },
    question: { type: String },
    answer: { type: String },
    eventDetails: { type: String },
    isApproved: { type: Boolean, default: true },
  },
  { timestamps: true }
);

export const CommunityPost = model<ICommunityPost>('CommunityPost', communitySchema);




Controller (community.controller.ts)

typescript

CopyEdit

import { Controller, Get, Post, Put, Param, Body } from '@nestjs/common';
import { CommunityService } from './community.service';
import { CreateCommunityPostDto } from './dto/createCommunityPost.dto';
import { ModerateContentDto } from './dto/moderateContent.dto';

@Controller('community')
export class CommunityController {
  constructor(private readonly communityService: CommunityService) {}

  @Get()
  async getAllPosts() {
    return this.communityService.findAllPosts();
  }

  @Get(':id')
  async getPostById(@Param('id') id: string) {
    return this.communityService.findPostById(id);
  }

  @Post()
  async createPost(@Body() createCommunityPostDto: CreateCommunityPostDto) {
    return this.communityService.createPost(createCommunityPostDto);
  }

  @Put('moderate/:id')
  async moderatePost(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() moderateContentDto: ModerateContentDto
  ) {
    return this.communityService.moderateContent(id, moderateContentDto);
  }
}




Service (community.service.ts)

typescript

CopyEdit

import { Injectable, NotFoundException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { CommunityPost, ICommunityPost } from './community.model';
import { AIContentModerationService } from './aiContentModeration.service';
import { SwarmOrchestratorService } from './swarmOrchestrator.service';

@Injectable()
export class CommunityService {
  constructor(
    private readonly aiModeration: AIContentModerationService,
    private readonly swarmOrchestrator: SwarmOrchestratorService
  ) {}

  async findAllPosts(): Promise<ICommunityPost[]> {
    this.swarmOrchestrator.adjustCommunityEngagement();
    return CommunityPost.find();
  }

  async findPostById(id: string): Promise<ICommunityPost | null> {
    return CommunityPost.findById(id);
  }

  async createPost(data: Partial<ICommunityPost>): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const isApproved = await this.aiModeration.moderateContent(data.content || data.question || '');
    const newPost = new CommunityPost({ ...data, isApproved });
    return newPost.save();
  }

  async moderateContent(id: string, update: { isApproved: boolean }): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const post = await CommunityPost.findById(id);
    if (!post) throw new NotFoundException('Post not found');
    post.isApproved = update.isApproved;
    return post.save();
  }
}




AI Content Moderation Service (aiContentModeration.service.ts)

typescript

CopyEdit

import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import axios from 'axios';

@Injectable()
export class AIContentModerationService {
  async moderateContent(content: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const response = await axios.post('https://commentanalyzer.googleapis.com/v1alpha1/comments:analyze', {
      comment: { text: content },
      languages: ['en'],
      requestedAttributes: { TOXICITY: {}, INSULT: {}, SPAM: {} },
      doNotStore: true,
    }, {
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.PERSPECTIVE_API_KEY}`,
      },
    });

    const toxicityScore = response.data.attributeScores.TOXICITY.summaryScore.value;
    const insultScore = response.data.attributeScores.INSULT.summaryScore.value;
    const spamScore = response.data.attributeScores.SPAM.summaryScore.value;

    return toxicityScore < 0.7 && insultScore < 0.7 && spamScore < 0.7; // Approve if scores are below thresholds
  }
}

import { Module } from '@nestjs/common';
import { MongooseModule } from '@nestjs/mongoose';
import { CommunityController } from './community.controller';
import { CommunityService } from './community.service';
import { AIContentModerationService } from './aiContentModeration.service';
import { SwarmOrchestratorService } from './swarmOrchestrator.service';
import { CommunityPost } from './community.model';

@Module({
  imports: [MongooseModule.forFeature([{ name: 'CommunityPost', schema: CommunityPost }])],
  controllers: [CommunityController],
  providers: [CommunityService, AIContentModerationService, SwarmOrchestratorService],
})
export class CommunityModule {}




Frontend Implementation

Forum Component

tsx

CopyEdit

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const Forum = () => {
  const [forums, setForums] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('/api/community?type=forum')
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(data => setForums(data.filter(post => post.isApproved)));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Community Forum</h3>
      {forums.map((forum, index) => (
        <div key={index}>
          <h4>{forum.title}</h4>
          <p>{forum.content}</p>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};

export default Forum;




Q&A Component

tsx

CopyEdit

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const QandA = () => {
  const [question, setQuestion] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState([]);

  const submitQuestion = async () => {
    const response = await fetch('/api/community', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({ type: 'qanda', question, userId: '123' }),
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    setQuestions([...questions, data]);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Ask a Question</h3>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={question}
        onChange={(e) => setQuestion(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Enter your question"
      />
      <button onClick={submitQuestion}>Submit</button>
    </div>
  );
};

export default QandA;




Event Suggestions Component

tsx

CopyEdit

import React, { useState } from 'react';

const EventSuggestions = () => {
  const [events, setEvents] = useState([]);
  const [eventName, setEventName] = useState('');
  const [eventDetails, setEventDetails] = useState('');

  const suggestEvent = async () => {
    const response = await fetch('/api/community', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({
        type: 'event',
        title: eventName,
        content: eventDetails,
        userId: '123',
      }),
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
    const data = await response.json();
    setEvents([...events, data]);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Suggest an Event</h3>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={eventName}
        onChange={(e) => setEventName(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Event Name"
      />
      <textarea
        value={eventDetails}
        onChange={(e) => setEventDetails(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Event Details"
      />
      <button onClick={suggestEvent}>Submit</button>
    </div>
  );
};

export default EventSuggestions;

1. Backend

1.1. Unified Community Model (extended)

Update backend/src/community/community.model.ts to accommodate new features:

import { Schema, model, Document, Types } from 'mongoose';

export interface ICommunityPost extends Document {
  userId: Types.ObjectId;
  type:
    | 'forum'
    | 'qanda'
    | 'event'
    | 'studyCircle'
    | 'recitationRoom'
    | 'askScholar';
  title?: string;
  content?: string;
  question?: string;
  answer?: string;
  eventDetails?: {
    description: string;
    date?: Date;
    location?: string;
  };
  studyCircleDetails?: {
    topic: string;
    scheduledAt: Date;
    members: Types.ObjectId[];
  };
  recitationRoomDetails?: {
    tajwidFocus: string;
    scheduledAt: Date;
    participants: Types.ObjectId[];
  };
  askScholarDetails?: {
    scholarId: Types.ObjectId;
    scheduledAt: Date;
    status: 'pending' | 'answered';
    answerText?: string;
  };
  isApproved: boolean;
  likes: Types.ObjectId[];
  shares: number;
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

const communitySchema = new Schema<ICommunityPost>(
  {
    userId: { type: Types.ObjectId, required: true, ref: 'User' },
    type: {
      type: String,
      required: true,
      enum: [
        'forum',
        'qanda',
        'event',
        'studyCircle',
        'recitationRoom',
        'askScholar',
      ],
    },
    title: { type: String },
    content: { type: String },
    question: { type: String },
    answer: { type: String },
    eventDetails: {
      description: { type: String },
      date: { type: Date },
      location: { type: String },
    },
    studyCircleDetails: {
      topic: { type: String },
      scheduledAt: { type: Date },
      members: [{ type: Types.ObjectId, ref: 'User' }],
    },
    recitationRoomDetails: {
      tajwidFocus: { type: String },
      scheduledAt: { type: Date },
      participants: [{ type: Types.ObjectId, ref: 'User' }],
    },
    askScholarDetails: {
      scholarId: { type: Types.ObjectId, ref: 'User' },
      scheduledAt: { type: Date },
      status: { type: String, enum: ['pending', 'answered'], default: 'pending' },
      answerText: { type: String },
    },
    isApproved: { type: Boolean, default: false },
    likes: [{ type: Types.ObjectId, ref: 'User', default: [] }],
    shares: { type: Number, default: 0 },
  },
  { timestamps: true }
);

export const CommunityPost = model<ICommunityPost>(
  'CommunityPost',
  communitySchema
);


Notes:

New type values:

studyCircle for virtual study groups.

recitationRoom for peer-to-peer tajwīd/practice rooms.

askScholar for scheduled “ask a scholar” sessions.

studyCircleDetails, recitationRoomDetails, and askScholarDetails store scheduling and participant data.

All posts still go through AI moderation (isApproved).

1.3. Certification & Credentials Models

import { Schema, model, Document, Types } from 'mongoose';

export interface ICertificate extends Document {
  userId: Types.ObjectId;
  courseId: Types.ObjectId;
  level: string;            // e.g., “Beginner,” “Intermediate,” “Advanced”
  issuedAt: Date;
  expiresAt?: Date;
  credentialHash: string;    // e.g., JWT or blockchain hash
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
}

const certificateSchema = new Schema<ICertificate>(
  {
    userId: { type: Types.ObjectId, required: true, ref: 'User' },
    courseId: { type: Types.ObjectId, required: true, ref: 'Course' },
    level: { type: String, required: true },
    issuedAt: { type: Date, required: true, default: Date.now },
    expiresAt: { type: Date },
    credentialHash: { type: String, required: true },
  },
  { timestamps: true }
);

export const Certificate = model<ICertificate>(
  'Certificate',
  certificateSchema
);

1.5. Community Controller (extended)

Update backend/src/community/community.controller.ts or create new controllers for sub-features:

import {
  Controller,
  Get,
  Post,
  Put,
  Param,
  Body,
  Query,
  UseGuards,
  NotFoundException,
} from '@nestjs/common';
import { CommunityService } from './community.service';
import { CreateCommunityPostDto } from './dto/createCommunityPost.dto';
import { ModerateContentDto } from './dto/moderateContent.dto';
import { LikePostDto } from './dto/likePost.dto';
import { SharePostDto } from './dto/sharePost.dto';
import { CreateStudyCircleDto } from './dto/createStudyCircle.dto';
import { CreateRecitationRoomDto } from './dto/createRecitationRoom.dto';
import { CreateAskScholarDto } from './dto/askScholar.dto';
import { ApproveAskScholarDto } from './dto/approveAskScholar.dto';
import { AuthGuard } from '../auth/auth.guard';

@Controller('community')
export class CommunityController {
  constructor(private readonly communityService: CommunityService) {}

  @Get()
  async getAllPosts(
    @Query('type') type?: string,
    @Query('userId') userId?: string
  ) {
    return this.communityService.findAllPosts({ type, userId });
  }

  @Get(':id')
  async getPostById(@Param('id') id: string) {
    const post = await this.communityService.findPostById(id);
    if (!post) throw new NotFoundException('Post not found');
    return post;
  }

  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Post()
  async createPost(@Body() dto: CreateCommunityPostDto) {
    return this.communityService.createPost(dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Put('like/:id')
  async likePost(@Param('id') id: string, @Body() dto: LikePostDto) {
    return this.communityService.toggleLike(id, dto.userId);
  }

  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Put('share/:id')
  async sharePost(@Param('id') id: string, @Body() dto: SharePostDto) {
    return this.communityService.incrementShare(id);
  }

  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Put('moderate/:id')
  async moderatePost(@Param('id') id: string, @Body() dto: ModerateContentDto) {
    return this.communityService.moderateContent(id, dto);
  }

  // Virtual Study Circle
  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Post('study-circle')
  async createStudyCircle(@Body() dto: CreateStudyCircleDto) {
    return this.communityService.createStudyCircle(dto);
  }

  // Recitation Room
  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Post('recitation-room')
  async createRecitationRoom(@Body() dto: CreateRecitationRoomDto) {
    return this.communityService.createRecitationRoom(dto);
  }

  // Ask a Scholar
  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Post('ask-scholar')
  async askScholar(@Body() dto: CreateAskScholarDto) {
    return this.communityService.createAskScholar(dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Put('ask-scholar/:id/answer')
  async answerAskScholar(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: ApproveAskScholarDto
  ) {
    return this.communityService.answerAskScholar(id, dto.answerText);
  }
}


1.6. Community Service (extended)

Update backend/src/community/community.service.ts:

import {
  Injectable,
  NotFoundException,
  HttpException,
  HttpStatus,
} from '@nestjs/common';
import { CommunityPost, ICommunityPost } from './community.model';
import { AIContentModerationService } from './aiContentModeration.service';
import { SwarmOrchestratorService } from './swarmOrchestrator.service';
import { Types } from 'mongoose';

interface FindAllOptions {
  type?: string;
  userId?: string;
}

@Injectable()
export class CommunityService {
  constructor(
    private readonly aiModeration: AIContentModerationService,
    private readonly swarmOrchestrator: SwarmOrchestratorService
  ) {}

  async findAllPosts(options: FindAllOptions): Promise<ICommunityPost[]> {
    const filter: any = { isApproved: true };
    if (options.type) filter.type = options.type;
    if (options.userId) filter.userId = new Types.ObjectId(options.userId);

    this.swarmOrchestrator.adjustCommunityEngagement();
    return CommunityPost.find(filter).sort({ createdAt: -1 });
  }

  async findPostById(id: string): Promise<ICommunityPost | null> {
    return CommunityPost.findById(id);
  }

  async createPost(data: Partial<ICommunityPost>): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const rawText =
      data.content ||
      data.question ||
      data.eventDetails?.description ||
      data.studyCircleDetails?.topic ||
      data.recitationRoomDetails?.tajwidFocus ||
      data.askScholarDetails?.question ||
      '';
    const isApproved = await this.aiModeration.moderateContent(rawText);

    const newPost = new CommunityPost({
      userId: new Types.ObjectId(data.userId),
      type: data.type,
      title: data.title,
      content: data.content,
      question: data.question,
      answer: data.answer,
      eventDetails: data.eventDetails
        ? {
            description: data.eventDetails.description,
            date: data.eventDetails.date,
            location: data.eventDetails.location,
          }
        : undefined,
      studyCircleDetails: data.studyCircleDetails
        ? {
            topic: data.studyCircleDetails.topic,
            scheduledAt: data.studyCircleDetails.scheduledAt,
            members: data.studyCircleDetails.members.map(
              (id) => new Types.ObjectId(id)
            ),
          }
        : undefined,
      recitationRoomDetails: data.recitationRoomDetails
        ? {
            tajwidFocus: data.recitationRoomDetails.tajwidFocus,
            scheduledAt: data.recitationRoomDetails.scheduledAt,
            participants: data.recitationRoomDetails.participants.map(
              (id) => new Types.ObjectId(id)
            ),
          }
        : undefined,
      askScholarDetails: data.askScholarDetails
        ? {
            scholarId: new Types.ObjectId(data.askScholarDetails.scholarId),
            scheduledAt: data.askScholarDetails.scheduledAt,
            status: 'pending',
          }
        : undefined,
      isApproved,
      likes: [],
      shares: 0,
    });

    return newPost.save();
  }

  async toggleLike(postId: string, userId: string): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const post = await CommunityPost.findById(postId);
    if (!post) throw new NotFoundException('Post not found');
    const idx = post.likes.findIndex((id) => id.toString() === userId);
    if (idx >= 0) {
      post.likes.splice(idx, 1);
    } else {
      post.likes.push(new Types.ObjectId(userId));
    }
    return post.save();
  }

  async incrementShare(postId: string): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const post = await CommunityPost.findById(postId);
    if (!post) throw new NotFoundException('Post not found');
    post.shares += 1;
    return post.save();
  }

  async moderateContent(
    id: string,
    update: { isApproved: boolean }
  ): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const post = await CommunityPost.findById(id);
    if (!post) throw new NotFoundException('Post not found');
    post.isApproved = update.isApproved;
    return post.save();
  }

  // Virtual Study Circle
  async createStudyCircle(data: {
    userId: string;
    topic: string;
    scheduledAt: string;
    members: string[];
  }): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const dto: Partial<ICommunityPost> = {
      userId: new Types.ObjectId(data.userId),
      type: 'studyCircle',
      studyCircleDetails: {
        topic: data.topic,
        scheduledAt: new Date(data.scheduledAt),
        members: data.members.map((id) => new Types.ObjectId(id)),
      },
      isApproved: true, // automatically approve study circles
      likes: [],
      shares: 0,
    };
    return new CommunityPost(dto).save();
  }

  // Recitation Room
  async createRecitationRoom(data: {
    userId: string;
    tajwidFocus: string;
    scheduledAt: string;
    participants: string[];
  }): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const dto: Partial<ICommunityPost> = {
      userId: new Types.ObjectId(data.userId),
      type: 'recitationRoom',
      recitationRoomDetails: {
        tajwidFocus: data.tajwidFocus,
        scheduledAt: new Date(data.scheduledAt),
        participants: data.participants.map((id) => new Types.ObjectId(id)),
      },
      isApproved: true,
      likes: [],
      shares: 0,
    };
    return new CommunityPost(dto).save();
  }

  // Ask a Scholar
  async createAskScholar(data: {
    userId: string;
    scholarId: string;
    scheduledAt: string;
    question: string;
  }): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const rawText = data.question;
    const isApproved = await this.aiModeration.moderateContent(rawText);

    const dto: Partial<ICommunityPost> = {
      userId: new Types.ObjectId(data.userId),
      type: 'askScholar',
      askScholarDetails: {
        scholarId: new Types.ObjectId(data.scholarId),
        scheduledAt: new Date(data.scheduledAt),
        status: 'pending',
      },
      question: data.question,
      isApproved,
      likes: [],
      shares: 0,
    };
    return new CommunityPost(dto).save();
  }

  async answerAskScholar(
    postId: string,
    answerText: string
  ): Promise<ICommunityPost> {
    const post = await CommunityPost.findById(postId);
    if (!post || post.type !== 'askScholar')
      throw new NotFoundException('Ask Scholar session not found');
    post.askScholarDetails.answerText = answerText;
    post.askScholarDetails.status = 'answered';
    return post.save();
  }
}

import {

  Post,

  Param,
  Body,

  NotFoundException,
} from '@nestjs/common';

import { AuthGuard } from '../auth/auth.guard';

@Controller('events')
export class EventController {
  constructor(private readonly eventService: EventService) {}

  @Get()
  async getAllEvents() {
    return this.eventService.findAllEvents();
  }

  @Get(':id')
  async getEventById(@Param('id') id: string) {
    const ev = await this.eventService.findEventById(id);
    if (!ev) throw new NotFoundException('Event not found');
    return ev;
  }

  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Post()
  async createEvent(@Body() dto: CreateEventDto) {
    return this.eventService.createEvent(dto);
  }

  @Put(':id/rsvp')

}


Create backend/src/community/event.service.ts:

import { Injectable, NotFoundException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { Event, IEvent } from './event.model';
import { Types } from 'mongoose';

@Injectable()
export class EventService {
  async findAllEvents(): Promise<IEvent[]> {
    return Event.find().sort({ startDate: 1 });
  }

  async findEventById(id: string): Promise<IEvent | null> {
    return Event.findById(id);
  }

  async createEvent(data: Partial<IEvent>): Promise<IEvent> {
    const newEvent = new Event({
      creatorId: new Types.ObjectId(data.creatorId),
      title: data.title,
      description: data.description,
      startDate: data.startDate,
      endDate: data.endDate,
      location: data.location,
      type: data.type,
      attendees: [],
    });
    return newEvent.save();
  }

  async toggleRsvp(eventId: string, userId: string): Promise<IEvent> {
    const ev = await Event.findById(eventId);
    if (!ev) throw new NotFoundException('Event not found');
    const idx = ev.attendees.findIndex((id) => id.toString() === userId);
    if (idx >= 0) {
      ev.attendees.splice(idx, 1);
    } else {
      ev.attendees.push(new Types.ObjectId(userId));
    }
    return ev.save();
  }
}

Create backend/src/analytics/analytics.service.ts:

import { Injectable, NotFoundException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { UserAnalytics, IUserAnalytics } from './analytics.model';
import { EducatorInsights, IEducatorInsights } from './educator.model';
import { Types } from 'mongoose';

@Injectable()
export class AnalyticsService {
  async getUserAnalytics(userId: string): Promise<IUserAnalytics | null> {
    return UserAnalytics.findOne({ userId: new Types.ObjectId(userId) });
  }

  async updateUserAnalytics(dto: {
    userId: string;
    masteryScore?: number;
    tajwidDate?: string;
    tajwidAccuracy?: number;
    memorizationProgress?: {
      surah: string;
      versesMemorized: number;
    };
    engagementDate?: string;
    engagementScore?: number;
  }): Promise<IUserAnalytics> {
    let stats = await UserAnalytics.findOne({
      userId: new Types.ObjectId(dto.userId),
    });
    if (!stats) {
      stats = new UserAnalytics({ userId: new Types.ObjectId(dto.userId) });
    }
    if (dto.masteryScore !== undefined) {
      // Example: push or update a subject’s mastery—this is simplified
      const subject = 'General'; // in real use, pass subject in DTO
      stats.masteryScores.set(subject, dto.masteryScore);
    }
    if (dto.tajwidDate && dto.tajwidAccuracy !== undefined) {
      stats.tajwidAccuracy.push({
        date: new Date(dto.tajwidDate),
        accuracy: dto.tajwidAccuracy,
      });
    }
    if (dto.memorizationProgress) {
      stats.memorizationProgress.push({
        surah: dto.memorizationProgress.surah,
        versesMemorized: dto.memorizationProgress.versesMemorized,
      });
    }
    if (dto.engagementDate && dto.engagementScore !== undefined) {
      stats.emotionalEngagement.push({
        date: new Date(dto.engagementDate),
        score: dto.engagementScore,
      });
    }
    return stats.save();
  }

  async getEducatorInsights(classId: string): Promise<IEducatorInsights | null> {
    // In production, compute or fetch pre-computed insights
    return EducatorInsights.findOne({ classId: new Types.ObjectId(classId) });
  }
}


1.9. Certification Controller & Service

Create backend/src/certs/certificate.controller.ts:

import {
  Controller,
  Post,
  Get,
  Param,
  Body,
  UseGuards,
  NotFoundException,
} from '@nestjs/common';
import { CertificateService } from './certificate.service';
import { IssueCertificateDto } from './dto/issueCertificate.dto';
import { AuthGuard } from '../auth/auth.guard';

@Controller('certificates')
export class CertificateController {
  constructor(private readonly certificateService: CertificateService) {}

  @UseGuards(AuthGuard)
  @Post('issue')
  async issueCertificate(@Body() dto: IssueCertificateDto) {
    return this.certificateService.issueCertificate(dto);
  }

  @Get('user/:id')
  async getUserCertificates(@Param('id') id: string) {
    return this.certificateService.getUserCertificates(id);
  }

  @Get(':id/verify')
  async verifyCertificate(@Param('id') id: string) {
    const cert = await this.certificateService.getCertificateById(id);
    if (!cert) throw new NotFoundException('Certificate not found');
    return this.certificateService.verifyCertificate(id);
  }
}


Create backend/src/certs/certificate.service.ts:

import { Injectable, NotFoundException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { Certificate, ICertificate } from './certificate.model';
import { Types } from 'mongoose';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';

@Injectable()
export class CertificateService {
  async issueCertificate(data: {
    userId: string;
    courseId: string;
    level: string;
    issuedAt: string;
    expiresAt?: string;
  }): Promise<ICertificate> {
    // Generate a signed JWT as credentialHash (sharia-compliant details can be included)
    const payload = {
      userId: data.userId,
      courseId: data.courseId,
      level: data.level,
      issuedAt: data.issuedAt,
      expiresAt: data.expiresAt,
    };
    const credentialHash = jwt.sign(payload, process.env.JWT_SECRET, {
      algorithm: 'HS256',
    });

    const cert = new Certificate({
      userId: new Types.ObjectId(data.userId),
      courseId: new Types.ObjectId(data.courseId),
      level: data.level,
      issuedAt: new Date(data.issuedAt),
      expiresAt: data.expiresAt ? new Date(data.expiresAt) : undefined,
      credentialHash,
    });
    return cert.save();
  }

  async getUserCertificates(userId: string): Promise<ICertificate[]> {
    return Certificate.find({ userId: new Types.ObjectId(userId) });
  }

  async getCertificateById(id: string): Promise<ICertificate | null> {
    return Certificate.findById(id);
  }

  async verifyCertificate(id: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const cert = await Certificate.findById(id);
    if (!cert) throw new NotFoundException('Certificate not found');

    try {
      jwt.verify(cert.credentialHash, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
      return true;
    } catch (err) {
      return false;
    }
  }
}

2.3. Event Suggestions Component (extended)

Update frontend-vite/src/components/community/EventSuggestions.tsx to include RSVP counts:

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
import PostActions from '../social/PostActions';

interface IEventPost {
  _id: string;
  title: string;
  eventDetails: {
    description: string;
    date: string;
    location?: string;
  };
  attendees: string[];
  likes: string[];
  shares: number;
}

const EventSuggestions: React.FC = () => {
  const [events, setEvents] = useState<IEventPost[]>([]);
  const [eventName, setEventName] = useState('');
  const [eventDetails, setEventDetails] = useState('');
  const [eventDate, setEventDate] = useState('');
  const [eventLocation, setEventLocation] = useState('');
  const currentUserId = localStorage.getItem('userId') || 'UNKNOWN';

  useEffect(() => {
    axios
      .get('/events')
      .then((res) => setEvents(res.data))
      .catch((err) => console.error('Error fetching events', err));
  }, []);

  const suggestEvent = async () => {
    try {
      const payload = {
        creatorId: currentUserId,
        title: eventName,
        description: eventDetails,
        startDate: eventDate,
        type: 'online',
      };
      if (eventLocation.trim()) payload.location = eventLocation;
      const res = await axios.post('/events', payload);
      setEvents([res.data, ...events]);
      setEventName('');
      setEventDetails('');
      setEventDate('');
      setEventLocation('');
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error suggesting event', err);
    }
  };

  const toggleRsvp = async (evId: string) => {
    try {
      await axios.put(`/events/${evId}/rsvp`, { userId: currentUserId });
      setEvents((prev) =>
        prev.map((ev) =>
          ev._id === evId
            ? {
                ...ev,
                attendees: ev.attendees.includes(currentUserId)
                  ? ev.attendees.filter((id) => id !== currentUserId)
                  : [...ev.attendees, currentUserId],
              }
            : ev
        )
      );
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error RSVPing', err);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-4">
      <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Suggest an Event</h3>
      <div className="space-y-2 mb-4">
        <input
          type="text"
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={eventName}
          onChange={(e) => setEventName(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Event Name"
        />
        <textarea
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={eventDetails}
          onChange={(e) => setEventDetails(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Event Description"
        />
        <input
          type="date"
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={eventDate}
          onChange={(e) => setEventDate(e.target.value)}
        />
        <input
          type="text"
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={eventLocation}
          onChange={(e) => setEventLocation(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Location (optional)"
        />
        <button
          onClick={suggestEvent}
          className="px-4 py-2 bg-green-500 text-white rounded-lg"
        >
          Submit
        </button>
      </div>

      <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Upcoming Events</h3>
      {events.map((evt) => (
        <div
          key={evt._id}
          className="mb-6 p-4 border rounded-lg shadow-sm"
        >
          <h4 className="text-xl font-semibold">{evt.title}</h4>
          <p className="mt-1 text-gray-700">
            {evt.eventDetails.description}
          </p>
          <p className="text-gray-600 mt-1">
            Date: {new Date(evt.eventDetails.date).toLocaleDateString()}
          </p>
          {evt.eventDetails.location && (
            <p className="text-gray-600">Location: {evt.eventDetails.location}</p>
          )}
          <div className="mt-3 flex items-center space-x-4">
            <button onClick={() => toggleRsvp(evt._id)}>
              {evt.attendees.includes(currentUserId) ? 'Cancel RSVP' : 'RSVP'}
              {' '}({evt.attendees.length})
            </button>
            <PostActions
              postId={evt._id}
              userId={currentUserId}
              initialLikes={evt.likes}
              initialShares={evt.shares}
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};

export default EventSuggestions;


Notes:

Now shows RSVP count and lets user toggle RSVP.

Uses POST /events and PUT /events/:id/rsvp.

2.4. Study Circle Component

Create frontend-vite/src/components/community/StudyCircle.tsx:

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
import PostActions from '../social/PostActions';

interface IStudyCircle {
  _id: string;
  studyCircleDetails: {
    topic: string;
    scheduledAt: string;
    members: string[];
  };
  likes: string[];
  shares: number;
}

const StudyCircle: React.FC = () => {
  const [circles, setCircles] = useState<IStudyCircle[]>([]);
  const [topic, setTopic] = useState('');
  const [scheduledAt, setScheduledAt] = useState('');
  const [members, setMembers] = useState<string>(''); // comma-separated user IDs
  const currentUserId = localStorage.getItem('userId') || 'UNKNOWN';

  useEffect(() => {
    axios
      .get('/community?type=studyCircle')
      .then((res) => setCircles(res.data))
      .catch((err) => console.error('Error fetching study circles', err));
  }, []);

  const createCircle = async () => {
    try {
      const payload = {
        userId: currentUserId,
        topic,
        scheduledAt,
        members: members.split(',').map((id) => id.trim()),
      };
      const res = await axios.post('/community/study-circle', payload);
      setCircles([res.data, ...circles]);
      setTopic('');
      setScheduledAt('');
      setMembers('');
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error creating study circle', err);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-4">
      <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Virtual Study Circles</h3>
      <div className="space-y-2 mb-4">
        <input
          type="text"
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={topic}
          onChange={(e) => setTopic(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Study Topic"
        />
        <input
          type="datetime-local"
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={scheduledAt}
          onChange={(e) => setScheduledAt(e.target.value)}
        />
        <input
          type="text"
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={members}
          onChange={(e) => setMembers(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Member IDs (comma-separated)"
        />
        <button
          onClick={createCircle}
          className="px-4 py-2 bg-indigo-500 text-white rounded-lg"
        >
          Create Circle
        </button>
      </div>

      <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Upcoming Circles</h3>
      {circles.map((circle) => (
        <div
          key={circle._id}
          className="mb-6 p-4 border rounded-lg shadow-sm"
        >
          <h4 className="text-xl font-semibold">{circle.studyCircleDetails.topic}</h4>
          <p className="text-gray-600">
            Scheduled: {new Date(circle.studyCircleDetails.scheduledAt).toLocaleString()}
          </p>
          <p className="text-gray-600">
            Members: {circle.studyCircleDetails.members.join(', ')}
          </p>
          <PostActions
            postId={circle._id}
            userId={currentUserId}
            initialLikes={circle.likes}
            initialShares={circle.shares}
          />
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};

export default StudyCircle;

  };

  shares: number;
}

const RecitationRoom: React.FC = () => {

2.6. Ask a Scholar Component

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
import PostActions from '../social/PostActions';

interface IAskScholar {
  _id: string;
  question: string;
  askScholarDetails: {
    scholarId: string;
    scheduledAt: string;
    status: string;
    answerText?: string;
  };
  likes: string[];
  shares: number;
}

const AskScholar: React.FC = () => {
  const [requests, setRequests] = useState<IAskScholar[]>([]);
  const [scholarId, setScholarId] = useState('');
  const [scheduledAt, setScheduledAt] = useState('');
  const [question, setQuestion] = useState('');
  const currentUserId = localStorage.getItem('userId') || 'UNKNOWN';

  useEffect(() => {
    axios
      .get('/community?type=askScholar')
      .then((res) => setRequests(res.data))
      .catch((err) => console.error('Error fetching requests', err));
  }, []);

  const createRequest = async () => {
    try {
      const payload = {
        userId: currentUserId,
        scholarId,
        scheduledAt,
        question,
      };
      const res = await axios.post('/community/ask-scholar', payload);
      setRequests([res.data, ...requests]);
      setScholarId('');
      setScheduledAt('');
      setQuestion('');
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error requesting scholar session', err);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-4">
      <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Ask a Scholar</h3>
      <div className="space-y-2 mb-4">
        <input
          type="text"
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={scholarId}
          onChange={(e) => setScholarId(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Scholar User ID"
        />
        <input
          type="datetime-local"
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={scheduledAt}
          onChange={(e) => setScheduledAt(e.target.value)}
        />
        <textarea
          className="w-full p-2 border rounded-lg"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => setQuestion(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Your Question"
        />
        <button
          onClick={createRequest}
          className="px-4 py-2 bg-orange-500 text-white rounded-lg"
        >
          Submit Request
        </button>
      </div>

      <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Pending & Completed Requests</h3>
      {requests.map((req) => (
        <div
          key={req._id}
          className="mb-6 p-4 border rounded-lg shadow-sm"
        >
          <p>
            <strong>Question:</strong> {req.question}
          </p>
          <p className="text-gray-600">
            Scheduled with Scholar ID: {req.askScholarDetails.scholarId} on{' '}
            {new Date(req.askScholarDetails.scheduledAt).toLocaleString()}
          </p>
          <p className="text-gray-600">
            Status: {req.askScholarDetails.status}
          </p>
          {req.askScholarDetails.status === 'answered' && (
            <p className="mt-2 text-gray-700">
              <strong>Answer:</strong> {req.askScholarDetails.answerText}
            </p>
          )}
          <PostActions
            postId={req._id}
            userId={currentUserId}
            initialLikes={req.likes}
            initialShares={req.shares}
          />
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
};

export default AskScholar;


2.7. Analytics Dashboard Component

Create frontend-vite/src/components/analytics/UserDashboard.tsx:

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
import { Line } from 'recharts';

interface IUserAnalytics {
  masteryScores: { [subject: string]: number };
  tajwidAccuracy: { date: string; accuracy: number }[];
  memorizationProgress: { surah: string; versesMemorized: number }[];
  emotionalEngagement: { date: string; score: number }[];
}

const UserDashboard: React.FC<{ userId: string }> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [analytics, setAnalytics] = useState<IUserAnalytics | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    axios
      .get(`/analytics/user/${userId}`)
      .then((res) => setAnalytics(res.data))
      .catch((err) => console.error('Error fetching analytics', err));
  }, [userId]);

  if (!analytics) return <div>Loading analytics...</div>;

  return (
    <div className="p-4">
      <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Your Learning Dashboard</h3>

      <div className="mb-6">
        <h4 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Mastery Scores</h4>
        <ul>
          {Object.entries(analytics.masteryScores).map(([subject, score]) => (
            <li key={subject}>
              {subject}: {score}%
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>

      <div className="mb-6">
        <h4 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Tajwīd Accuracy Over Time</h4>
        <Line
          data={analytics.tajwidAccuracy.map((d) => ({
            date: new Date(d.date).toLocaleDateString(),
            accuracy: d.accuracy,
          }))}
          dataKey="accuracy"
          name="Accuracy"
          xAxis="date"
          yAxis="accuracy"
        />
      </div>

      <div className="mb-6">
        <h4 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Memorization Progress</h4>
        <ul>
          {analytics.memorizationProgress.map((m) => (
            <li key={m.surah}>
              {m.surah}: {m.versesMemorized} verses
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>

      <div>
        <h4 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Emotional Engagement</h4>
        <Line
          data={analytics.emotionalEngagement.map((d) => ({
            date: new Date(d.date).toLocaleDateString(),
            score: d.score,
          }))}
          dataKey="score"
          name="Engagement"
          xAxis="date"
          yAxis="score"
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default UserDashboard;


Notes:

Uses Recharts’ <Line> chart to plot accuracy and engagement trends.

Displays mastery scores and memorization progress in simple lists.

2.8. Educator Insights Component

Create frontend-vite/src/components/analytics/EducatorInsights.tsx:

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface IEducatorInsights {
  averageMastery: { [subject: string]: number };
  weakSpots: { subject: string; averageScore: number }[];
  recommendedExercises: { subject: string; exerciseIds: string[] }[];
}

const EducatorInsights: React.FC<{ classId: string }> = ({ classId }) => {
  const [insights, setInsights] = useState<IEducatorInsights | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    axios
      .get(`/analytics/educator/${classId}`)
      .then((res) => setInsights(res.data))
      .catch((err) => console.error('Error fetching insights', err));
  }, [classId]);

  if (!insights) return <div>Loading educator insights...</div>;

  return (
    <div className="p-4">
      <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Class Performance Insights</h3>

      <div className="mb-6">
        <h4 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Average Mastery by Subject</h4>
        <ul>
          {Object.entries(insights.averageMastery).map(([subject, avg]) => (
            <li key={subject}>
              {subject}: {avg}%
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>

      <div className="mb-6">
        <h4 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Common Weak Spots</h4>
        <ul>
          {insights.weakSpots.map((w) => (
            <li key={w.subject}>
              {w.subject}: {w.averageScore}%
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>

      <div>
        <h4 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2">Recommended Group Exercises</h4>
        {insights.recommendedExercises.map((r) => (
          <div key={r.subject} className="mb-2">
            <strong>{r.subject}:</strong> Exercise IDs {r.exerciseIds.join(', ')}
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default EducatorInsights;


2.9. Certificates Component

Create frontend-vite/src/components/certs/Certificates.tsx:

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface ICertificate {
  _id: string;
  courseId: string;
  level: string;
  issuedAt: string;
  expiresAt?: string;
  credentialHash: string;
}

const Certificates: React.FC<{ userId: string }> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [certs, setCerts] = useState<ICertificate[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    axios
      .get(`/certificates/user/${userId}`)
      .then((res) => setCerts(res.data))
      .catch((err) => console.error('Error fetching certificates', err));
  }, [userId]);

  return (
    <div className="p-4">
      <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold mb-4">Your Certificates</h3>
      <ul>
        {certs.map((c) => (
          <li key={c._id} className="mb-4 border p-4 rounded-lg shadow-sm">
            <p>
              <strong>Course ID:</strong> {c.courseId}
            </p>
            <p>
              <strong>Level:</strong> {c.level}
            </p>
            <p>
              <strong>Issued At:</strong>{' '}
              {new Date(c.issuedAt).toLocaleDateString()}
            </p>
            {c.expiresAt && (
              <p>
                <strong>Expires At:</strong>{' '}
                {new Date(c.expiresAt).toLocaleDateString()}
              </p>
            )}
            <button
              onClick={async () => {
                const verified = await axios.get(
                  `/certificates/${c._id}/verify`
                );
                alert(
                  verified.data
                    ? 'Certificate is valid'
                    : 'Certificate is invalid'
                );
              }}
              className="mt-2 px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded-lg"
            >
              Verify Certificate
            </button>
          </li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Certificates;


Notes:

Fetches GET /certificates/user/:id.

Lets user click “Verify” to call GET /certificates/:id/verify.

import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route } from 'react-router-dom';
import Forum from './components/community/Forum';
import QandA from './components/community/QandA';

import Certificates from './components/certs/Certificates';
