import FollowList from './components/social/FollowList';
// … other imports

export default function App() {
  return (
    <Router>
      <Routes>
        {/* Community */}
        <Route path="/community/forum" element={<Forum />} />
        <Route path="/community/qanda" element={<QandA />} />

          path="/users/:userId/profile"

          path="/dashboard/user/:userId"

          path="/dashboard/educator/:classId"

        {/* Certificates */}
        <Route
          path="/certificates/:userId"
          element={<Certificates userId={window.location.pathname.split('/')[2]} />}
        />

        {/* … other existing routes */}
      </Routes>
    </Router>
  );
}


Adjust how you extract route parameters depending on your React Router version. Wrapping components in small hooks or wrappers that read useParams() is recommended in production.

6. Verification & Testing

6.1. Backend

Run

cd backend
npm run build
npm run start:dev


Test API Endpoints:

Community

GET /community → list all approved posts.

GET /community?type=forum → only “forum” posts.

GET /community/:id → fetch a single post.

POST /community → create new “forum,” “qanda,” “event,” “studyCircle,” “recitationRoom,” or “askScholar” post.

PUT /community/like/:id → toggle like (body: { userId }).

PUT /community/share/:id → increment share.

PUT /community/moderate/:id → set { isApproved: true|false }.

POST /community/study-circle → create a study circle.

POST /community/recitation-room → create a recitation room.

POST /community/ask-scholar → request “ask a scholar.”

PUT /community/ask-scholar/:id/answer → provide answer text.

Events

GET /events → list all events.

GET /events/:id → fetch one event.

POST /events → create a new event (body: { creatorId, title, description, startDate, [endDate], [location], type }).

PUT /events/:id/rsvp → toggle RSVP (body: { userId }).

User/Profile

GET /users/:id/profile → fetch profile + recent posts.

POST /users/follow → toggle { currentUserId, targetUserId }.

GET /users/:id/followers → list followers.

GET /users/:id/following → list following.

Analytics

GET /analytics/user/:id → fetch user analytics.

POST /analytics/user/update → update analytics fields.

GET /analytics/educator/:classId → fetch educator insights.

Certificates

POST /certificates/issue → issue a new certificate (body: { userId, courseId, level, issuedAt, [expiresAt] }).

GET /certificates/user/:userId → list user’s certificates.

GET /certificates/:id/verify → verify a specific certificate’s JWT.

Backend Implementation for Phase 10

Backend Module for Video Streaming:

 To facilitate video conferencing, we integrate AWS MediaLive for live streaming and AWS S3 for storing and managing recorded video content.

Video Session Schema (MongoDB – videoSessionSchema.ts):

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface IVideoSession extends Document {
  title: string;
  description: string;
  hostId: string;
  participants: string[];
  startTime: Date;
  endTime?: Date;
  streamUrl: string;
}

const videoSessionSchema = new Schema<IVideoSession>({
  title: { type: String, required: true },
  description: { type: String, required: true },
  hostId: { type: String, required: true },
  participants: { type: [String], default: [] },
  startTime: { type: Date, required: true },
  endTime: { type: Date },
  streamUrl: { type: String, required: true },  // URL for live stream
}, { timestamps: true });

export const VideoSession = model<IVideoSession>('VideoSession', videoSessionSchema);


Video Controller for Streaming (videoController.ts):

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { VideoSession } from './videoSession';
import AWS from 'aws-sdk';

const s3 = new AWS.S3();
const mediaService = new AWS.MediaLive();  // AWS MediaLive for video streaming

// Function to generate a stream URL (simulating AWS MediaLive URL generation)
const generateStreamUrl = (): string => {
  const streamId = `stream-${Date.now()}`;
  return `https://streaming.quranedu.com/${streamId}`;  // Simulated stream URL
};

// API Endpoint for creating a video session
export const createSession = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const streamUrl = generateStreamUrl();
    const session = new VideoSession({ ...req.body, streamUrl });
    await session.save();
    res.status(201).json({ success: true, data: session });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

// API Endpoint for retrieving a session by ID
export const getSession = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const session = await VideoSession.findById(req.params.id);
    if (!session) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'Session not found' });
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: session });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

// API Endpoint for retrieving all sessions
export const getAllSessions = async (_req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const sessions = await VideoSession.find();
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: sessions });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};


Video Routes (Routing for Session Management – videoRoutes.ts):

import { Router } from 'express';

Real-Time Communication for Live Chat & Whiteboard

Real-time messaging and interactive whiteboards are essential for effective collaboration during video sessions.

Chat Controller (Handling Real-Time Messages – chatController.ts):

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { Message } from './messageModel';  // Model for storing messages

export const sendMessage = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { sessionId, userId, message } = req.body;
  try {
    const newMessage = new Message({ sessionId, userId, message });
    await newMessage.save();
    req.app.get('socketIo').emit('chatMessage', newMessage);  // Emit message to all participants
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: newMessage });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};


Message Model (messageModel.ts):

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface IMessage extends Document {
  sessionId: string;
  userId: string;
  message: string;
}

const messageSchema = new Schema<IMessage>({
  sessionId: { type: String, required: true },
  userId: { type: String, required: true },
  message: { type: String, required: true }
}, { timestamps: true });

export const Message = model<IMessage>('Message', messageSchema);

import { Server } from 'socket.io';

const io = new Server(3001, {
  cors: { origin: '*' }
});

// Initialize socket server
export const initSocket = (server) => {
  io.attach(server);
  io.on('connection', (socket) => {
    console.log('User connected');
    socket.on('disconnect', () => {
      console.log('User disconnected');
    });
  });
};

export const getSocket = () => io;




Session Recording Storage (Using AWS S3)

Recordings are stored on AWS S3, enabling easy access and retrieval.

AWS S3 File Upload Service (awsS3Service.ts):

import AWS from 'aws-sdk';

const s3 = new AWS.S3();

// Function to upload files to AWS S3
export const uploadFile = async (fileBuffer: Buffer, fileName: string) => {
  const params = {
    Bucket: 'your-bucket-name',
    Key: fileName,
    Body: fileBuffer,
    ContentType: 'video/mp4',
  };

  try {
    const data = await s3.upload(params).promise();
    return data.Location;  // Return URL of uploaded file
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error uploading file:', error);
    throw new Error('File upload failed');
  }
};


Session Recording Controller (sessionRecordingController.ts):

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { uploadFile } from './awsS3Service';  // File upload service
import { VideoSession } from './videoSession';

// API Endpoint for session recording and saving to S3
export const recordSession = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const { videoData, sessionId } = req.body;
    const videoBuffer = Buffer.from(videoData, 'base64');  // Assuming video is base64 encoded

    // Save to S3
    const fileName = `session-${sessionId}-${Date.now()}.mp4`;
    const fileUrl = await uploadFile(videoBuffer, fileName);

    // Save the recording URL to the database
    await VideoSession.findByIdAndUpdate(sessionId, { recordingUrl: fileUrl });

    res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: 'Recording saved', videoUrl: fileUrl });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};




AI Interaction Integration (OpenAI API)

Integrate OpenAI for live session assistance.

AI Assistant Service (aiAssistantService.ts):

import axios from 'axios';

// Function to interact with OpenAI for real-time assistance during sessions
export const getAIResponse = async (query: string) => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.post('https://api.openai.com/v1/completions', {
      model: 'text-davinci-003', // Example model
      prompt: query,
      max_tokens: 150,
      temperature: 0.7,
    }, {
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer YOUR_API_KEY`,
      },
    });

    return response.data.choices[0].text;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('AI Assistant failed:', error);
    throw new Error('Unable to get AI response.');
  }
};

Frontend Components

Full Integration

VideoPlayer.tsx (Video Streaming Component)

 This component fetches the live video stream URL from the backend and displays the video.

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const VideoPlayer = ({ sessionId }: { sessionId: string }) => {
  const [streamUrl, setStreamUrl] = useState<string>('');

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchStreamUrl = async () => {
      const response = await fetch(`/api/video/sessions/${sessionId}`);
      const data = await response.json();
      if (data.success) {
        setStreamUrl(data.data.streamUrl);
      }
    };
    fetchStreamUrl();
  }, [sessionId]);

  return (
    <div>
      {streamUrl ? (
        <video src={streamUrl} controls autoPlay style={{ width: '100%' }} />
      ) : (
        <p>Loading stream...</p>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default VideoPlayer;


ScreenShare.tsx (Screen Sharing Component)

 This component allows users to share their screen with other participants.

import React, { useRef } from 'react';

const ScreenShare = () => {
  const videoRef = useRef<HTMLVideoElement>(null);

  const startScreenShare = async () => {
    try {
      const stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getDisplayMedia({ video: true });
      if (videoRef.current) {
        videoRef.current.srcObject = stream;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Screen sharing failed:', error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <button onClick={startScreenShare}>Start Screen Sharing</button>
      <video ref={videoRef} autoPlay style={{ width: '100%' }} />
    </div>
  );
};

export default ScreenShare;


Whiteboard.tsx (Collaborative Whiteboard Component)

 Allows users to draw on a shared whiteboard.

import React, { useRef } from 'react';

const Whiteboard = () => {
  const canvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement>(null);

  const draw = (event: React.MouseEvent<HTMLCanvasElement>) => {
    if (canvasRef.current) {
      const ctx = canvasRef.current.getContext('2d');
      if (ctx) {
        ctx.lineTo(event.clientX, event.clientY);
        ctx.stroke();
      }
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <canvas
        ref={canvasRef}
        onMouseMove={draw}
        width={800}
        height={600}
        style={{ border: '1px solid black' }}
      />
    </div>
  );
};

export default Whiteboard;


SessionRecording.tsx (Session Recording Component)

 This component allows users to record the session and play it back.

import React, { useRef, useState } from 'react';

const SessionRecording = () => {
  const mediaRecorderRef = useRef<MediaRecorder | null>(null);
  const [recording, setRecording] = useState(false);
  const [videoUrl, setVideoUrl] = useState('');

  const startRecording = async () => {
    const stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ video: true, audio: true });
    const mediaRecorder = new MediaRecorder(stream);
    const chunks: BlobPart[] = [];

    mediaRecorder.ondataavailable = (event) => chunks.push(event.data);
    mediaRecorder.onstop = () => setVideoUrl(URL.createObjectURL(new Blob(chunks, { type: 'video/mp4' })));

    mediaRecorderRef.current = mediaRecorder;
    mediaRecorder.start();
    setRecording(true);
  };

  const stopRecording = () => {
    mediaRecorderRef.current?.stop();
    setRecording(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <button onClick={recording ? stopRecording : startRecording}>
        {recording ? 'Stop Recording' : 'Start Recording'}
      </button>
      {videoUrl && <video src={videoUrl} controls style={{ width: '100%' }} />}
    </div>
  );
};

export default SessionRecording;


AIInteractionAssistant.tsx (AI-Powered Assistant for Real-Time Interactions)

 The assistant component handles user queries and fetches responses from the backend’s AI assistant.

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { getAIResponse } from './aiAssistantService';

const AIInteractionAssistant = () => {
  const [response, setResponse] = useState('');
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('');

  const handleUserQuery = async () => {
    try {
      const aiResponse = await getAIResponse(query);
      setResponse(aiResponse);
    } catch (error) {
      setResponse('Error: Unable to get a response.');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>AI Assistant</h3>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={query}
        onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Ask the assistant..."
      />
      <button onClick={handleUserQuery}>Ask</button>
      <p>Response: {response}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchStatus = async () => {
      const response = await fetch('/api/swarmaI/status');
      const data = await response.json();
      setStatus(data.data.status);
    };

    fetchStatus();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Session Optimization Status</h3>

    </div>
  );

1. Backend Module for Video Streaming:
 To facilitate video conferencing, we integrate AWS MediaLive for live streaming and AWS S3 for storing and managing recorded video content.

Video Session Schema (MongoDB - videoSessionSchema.ts):

typescript

CopyEdit

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface IVideoSession extends Document {
  title: string;
  description: string;
  hostId: string;
  participants: string[];
  startTime: Date;
  endTime?: Date;
  streamUrl: string;
}

const videoSessionSchema = new Schema<IVideoSession>({
  title: { type: String, required: true },
  description: { type: String, required: true },
  hostId: { type: String, required: true },
  participants: { type: [String], default: [] },
  startTime: { type: Date, required: true },
  endTime: { type: Date },
  streamUrl: { type: String, required: true },  // URL for live stream
}, { timestamps: true });

export const VideoSession = model<IVideoSession>('VideoSession', videoSessionSchema);


Video Controller for Streaming (videoController.ts):

typescript

CopyEdit

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { VideoSession } from './videoSession';
import AWS from 'aws-sdk';

const s3 = new AWS.S3();
const mediaService = new AWS.MediaLive();  // AWS MediaLive for video streaming

// Function to generate a stream URL (simulating AWS MediaLive URL generation)
const generateStreamUrl = (): string => {
  const streamId = `stream-${Date.now()}`;
  return `https://streaming.quranedu.com/${streamId}`;  // Simulated stream URL
};

// API Endpoint for creating a video session
export const createSession = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const streamUrl = generateStreamUrl();
    const session = new VideoSession({ ...req.body, streamUrl });
    await session.save();
    res.status(201).json({ success: true, data: session });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

// API Endpoint for retrieving a session by ID
export const getSession = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const session = await VideoSession.findById(req.params.id);
    if (!session) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'Session not found' });
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: session });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

// API Endpoint for retrieving all sessions
export const getAllSessions = async (_req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const sessions = await VideoSession.find();
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: sessions });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

Chat Controller (Handling Real-Time Messages - chatController.ts):

typescript

CopyEdit

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { Message } from './messageModel';  // Model for storing messages

export const sendMessage = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { sessionId, userId, message } = req.body;
  try {
    const newMessage = new Message({ sessionId, userId, message });
    await newMessage.save();
    req.app.get('socketIo').emit('chatMessage', newMessage);  // Emit message to all participants
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: newMessage });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

  cors: { origin: '*' }
});

// Initialize socket server
export const initSocket = (server) => {
  io.attach(server);
  io.on('connection', (socket) => {
    console.log('User connected');
    socket.on('disconnect', () => {
      console.log('User disconnected');
    });
  });
};

3. Session Recording Storage (Using AWS S3):

Recordings are stored on AWS S3, enabling easy access and retrieval.

AWS S3 File Upload Service (awsS3Service.ts):

typescript

CopyEdit

import AWS from 'aws-sdk';

const s3 = new AWS.S3();

// Function to upload files to AWS S3
export const uploadFile = async (fileBuffer: Buffer, fileName: string) => {
  const params = {
    Bucket: 'your-bucket-name',
    Key: fileName,
    Body: fileBuffer,
    ContentType: 'video/mp4',
  };

  try {
    const data = await s3.upload(params).promise();
    return data.Location;  // Return URL of uploaded file
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error uploading file:', error);
    throw new Error('File upload failed');
  }
};


Session Recording Controller (sessionRecordingController.ts):

typescript

CopyEdit

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { uploadFile } from './awsS3Service';  // File upload service

// API Endpoint for session recording and saving to S3
export const recordSession = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const { videoData, sessionId } = req.body;
    const videoBuffer = Buffer.from(videoData, 'base64');  // Assuming video is base64 encoded

    // Save to S3
    const fileName = `session-${sessionId}-${Date.now()}.mp4`;
    const fileUrl = await uploadFile(videoBuffer, fileName);

    // Save the recording URL to the database
    await VideoSession.findByIdAndUpdate(sessionId, { recordingUrl: fileUrl });

    res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: 'Recording saved', videoUrl: fileUrl });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};




4. AI Interaction Integration (OpenAI API):

Integrate OpenAI for live session assistance.

AI Assistant Service (aiAssistantService.ts):

typescript

CopyEdit

import axios from 'axios';

// Function to interact with OpenAI for real-time assistance during sessions
export const getAIResponse = async (query: string) => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.post('https://api.openai.com/v1/completions', {
      model: 'text-davinci-003', // Example model
      prompt: query,
      max_tokens: 150,
      temperature: 0.7,
    }, {
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer YOUR_API_KEY`,
      },
    });

    return response.data.choices[0].text;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('AI Assistant failed:', error);
    throw new Error('Unable to get AI response.');
  }
};

  useNewUrlParser: true,
  useUnifiedTopology: true,
}).then(() => {
  console.log('MongoDB connected');
}).catch(err => {
  console.error('MongoDB connection error:', err);

Frontend Components: Full Integration

VideoPlayer.tsx (Video Streaming Component)
 This component fetches the live video stream URL from the backend and displays the video.

tsx

CopyEdit

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const VideoPlayer = ({ sessionId }: { sessionId: string }) => {
  const [streamUrl, setStreamUrl] = useState<string>('');

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchStreamUrl = async () => {
      const response = await fetch(`/api/video/sessions/${sessionId}`);
      const data = await response.json();
      if (data.success) {
        setStreamUrl(data.data.streamUrl);
      }
    };
    fetchStreamUrl();
  }, [sessionId]);

  return (
    <div>
      {streamUrl ? (
        <video src={streamUrl} controls autoPlay style={{ width: '100%' }} />
      ) : (
        <p>Loading stream...</p>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default VideoPlayer;


ScreenShare.tsx (Screen Sharing Component)
 This component allows users to share their screen with other participants.

tsx

CopyEdit

import React, { useRef } from 'react';

const ScreenShare = () => {
  const videoRef = useRef<HTMLVideoElement>(null);

  const startScreenShare = async () => {
    try {
      const stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getDisplayMedia({ video: true });
      if (videoRef.current) {
        videoRef.current.srcObject = stream;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Screen sharing failed:', error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <button onClick={startScreenShare}>Start Screen Sharing</button>
      <video ref={videoRef} autoPlay style={{ width: '100%' }} />
    </div>
  );
};

export default ScreenShare;


Whiteboard.tsx (Collaborative Whiteboard Component)
 Allows users to draw on a shared whiteboard.

tsx

CopyEdit

import React, { useRef } from 'react';

const Whiteboard = () => {
  const canvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement>(null);

  const draw = (event: React.MouseEvent<HTMLCanvasElement>) => {
    if (canvasRef.current) {
      const ctx = canvasRef.current.getContext('2d');
      if (ctx) {
        ctx.lineTo(event.clientX, event.clientY);
        ctx.stroke();
      }
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <canvas
        ref={canvasRef}
        onMouseMove={draw}
        width={800}
        height={600}
        style={{ border: '1px solid black' }}
      />
    </div>
  );
};

export default Whiteboard;


SessionRecording.tsx (Session Recording Component)
 This component allows users to record the session and play it back.

tsx

CopyEdit

import React, { useRef, useState } from 'react';

const SessionRecording = () => {
  const mediaRecorderRef = useRef<MediaRecorder | null>(null);
  const [recording, setRecording] = useState(false);
  const [videoUrl, setVideoUrl] = useState('');

  const startRecording = async () => {
    const stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ video: true, audio: true });
    const mediaRecorder = new MediaRecorder(stream);
    const chunks: BlobPart[] = [];

    mediaRecorder.ondataavailable = (event) => chunks.push(event.data);
    mediaRecorder.onstop = () => setVideoUrl(URL.createObjectURL(new Blob(chunks, { type: 'video/mp4' })));

    mediaRecorderRef.current = mediaRecorder;
    mediaRecorder.start();
    setRecording(true);
  };

  const stopRecording = () => {
    mediaRecorderRef.current?.stop();
    setRecording(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <button onClick={recording ? stopRecording : startRecording}>
        {recording ? 'Stop Recording' : 'Start Recording'}
      </button>
      {videoUrl && <video src={videoUrl} controls style={{ width: '100%' }} />}
    </div>
  );
};

export default SessionRecording;

Phase 11: VR/AR Integration

🟦 Overview

This phase integrates Virtual Reality (VR) and Augmented Reality (AR) technologies into the Quranic Education Platform, offering highly immersive and personalized learning and teaching experiences. The goal is to enhance the educational journey through dynamic, interactive environments that cater to both learners and teachers.

✅ Objectives

VR-based Recitation Immersion: Provide an environment for users to practice Quranic recitation in full immersion (A-Frame + Three.js).

AR Visualization for Tajwīd: Assist learners in mastering proper pronunciation by rendering correct mouth‐shape 3D models in real time (Three.js).

Virtual Classroom: Enable interactive, WebRTC-based, real-time learning with peers and instructors (using existing RTCService + SocketService).

AI-generated Visual Enhancements: Dynamically personalize VR/AR experiences via TensorFlow.js‐driven phoneme detection.

Swarm Intelligence Optimization: Optimize system performance and manage user activity across AR/VR sessions via SwarmService.



1. Models

models/VRSessionModel.ts

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface IVRSession extends Document {
  sessionName: string;
  hostId: string;
  participants: string[];
  startTime: Date;
  endTime?: Date;
  vrFeatures: string[];
}

const vrSessionSchema = new Schema<IVRSession>({
  sessionName: { type: String, required: true },
  hostId: { type: String, required: true },
  participants: { type: [String], default: [] },
  startTime: { type: Date, required: true },
  endTime: { type: Date },
  vrEnhancements: { type: [String], required: true },
});

export const VRSession = model<IVRSession>('VRSession', vrSessionSchema);

import { Schema, model, Document } from 'mongoose';

export interface IARSession extends Document {
  sessionName: string;
  hostId: string;
  participants: string[];
  startTime: Date;
  endTime?: Date;
  arFeatures: string[];
}

const arSessionSchema = new Schema<IARSession>({
  sessionName: { type: String, required: true },
  hostId: { type: String, required: true },
  participants: { type: [String], default: [] },
  startTime: { type: Date, required: true },
  endTime: { type: Date },
  arEnhancements: { type: [String], required: true },
});

export const ARSession = model<IARSession>('ARSession', arSessionSchema);

2. Services

services/SwarmService.ts

import * as os from 'os';

export const getSystemLoad = async () => {
  const load = os.loadavg();
  const memoryUsage = os.freemem() / os.totalmem();
  return { load, memoryUsage };
};

export const optimizeSessionService = async (sessionData: any) => {
  const userActivity = sessionData.participants.length;
  const { load, memoryUsage } = await getSystemLoad();

  const optimizedSessionData = {
    ...sessionData,
    loadBalancing: optimizeLoadBalancing(userActivity, load),
    sessionMonitoring: adjustResources(userActivity, memoryUsage),
  };

  return optimizedSessionData;
};

const optimizeLoadBalancing = (userActivity: number, systemLoad: number[]) => {
  if (systemLoad[0] > 2.5) {
    return 'Reduce session load, optimize resources';
  } else if (userActivity > 50) {
    return 'Distribute users to alternate servers';
  } else {
    return 'Maintain standard load balancing';
  }
};

const adjustResources = (userActivity: number, memoryUsage: number) => {
  if (memoryUsage > 0.8) {
    return 'Allocate more memory resources to handle higher user load';
  } else if (userActivity > 50) {
    return 'Allocate more processing power to manage high traffic';
  } else {
    return 'Standard resource allocation';
  }
};


services/RTCService.ts

import * as WebRTC from 'simple-peer';

export const initializeRTCServer = (server: any) => {
  const io = require('socket.io')(server);

  io.on('connection', (socket: any) => {
    socket.on('signal', (data: any) => {
      socket.broadcast.emit('signal', data);
    });

    socket.on('disconnect', () => {
      console.log('User disconnected');
    });
  });
};


services/SocketService.ts

import { Server } from 'socket.io';

export const initializeSocketServer = (server: any) => {
  const io = new Server(server);

  io.on('connection', (socket: any) => {
    console.log('New client connected:', socket.id);

    socket.on('message', (msg: string) => {
      console.log('Message received:', msg);
      socket.broadcast.emit('message', msg);
    });

    socket.on('disconnect', () => {
      console.log('Client disconnected:', socket.id);
    });
  });
};


services/3DRenderingService.ts

import * as THREE from 'three';

// Basic scene initialization (for testing or fallback)
export const initialize3DScene = () => {
  const scene = new THREE.Scene();
  const camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(75, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
  const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer();
  renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
  document.body.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

  const geometry = new THREE.BoxGeometry();
  const material = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x00ff00 });
  const cube = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, material);
  scene.add(cube);

  camera.position.z = 5;

  function animate() {
    requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    cube.rotation.x += 0.01;
    cube.rotation.y += 0.01;
    renderer.render(scene, camera);
  }

  animate();
};

services/transcriptionService.ts (OPTIONAL)

import { SpeechClient } from '@google-cloud/speech';

const client = new SpeechClient();

// Transcribe a small audio chunk to text
export const transcribeAudioChunk = async (audioBuffer: Buffer) => {
  const audioBytes = audioBuffer.toString('base64');
  const request = {
    audio: { content: audioBytes },
    config: {
      encoding: 'LINEAR16',
      sampleRateHertz: 48000,
      languageCode: 'ar-SA',
      enableAutomaticPunctuation: true,
    },
  };
  const [response] = await client.recognize(request);
  return response.results.map(r => r.alternatives[0].transcript).join(' ');
};

};

export const endVRSessionService = async (sessionId: string) => {
  return await VRSession.findOneAndUpdate(
    { _id: sessionId },
    { endTime: new Date() },
    { new: true }
  );
};

import firebase from "firebase/app";
import "firebase/storage";

const firebaseConfig = {
  apiKey: "YOUR_API_KEY",
  authDomain: "YOUR_PROJECT.firebaseapp.com",
  projectId: "YOUR_PROJECT_ID",
  storageBucket: "YOUR_PROJECT.appspot.com",
};

firebase.initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
const storage = firebase.storage();

// Base CDN URL (reservable for dynamic asset URLs)
export const CDN_BASE_URL = storage.ref().getDownloadURL().then(url => {
  // Remove token segment to form base path
  return url.replace(/\/[^\/]+$/, "");
});


Upload all AR/VR assets (e.g., mouthModels/*.glb, mosqueModels/*.glb, panoramas/*.jpg) to Firebase Storage.

Use the CDN_BASE_URL in components to fetch specific files, e.g., ${CDN_BASE_URL}/mouthModels/ka.glb.

6.1 hooks/useLivePhonemeDetection.ts

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import * as speechCommands from "@tensorflow-models/speech-commands";

export const useLivePhonemeDetection = (): string => {
  const [phoneme, setPhoneme] = useState<string>("");

  useEffect(() => {
    let model: speechCommands.SpeechCommandRecognizer;

    const loadModel = async () => {
      model = await speechCommands.create(
        "BROWSER_FFT",
        undefined,
        "https://cdn.example.com/models/speech-commands/model.json",
        "https://cdn.example.com/models/speech-commands/metadata.json"
      );
      await model.ensureModelLoaded();
      model.listen(result => {
        const scores = result.scores;
        const maxIndex = scores.indexOf(Math.max(...scores));
        const detected = model.wordLabels()[maxIndex];
        setPhoneme(detected);
      }, { probabilityThreshold: 0.85 });
    };

    loadModel();

    return () => {
      if (model) model.stopListening();
    };
  }, []);

  return phoneme;
};


6.2 ar/ARTajwidOverlay.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import * as THREE from "three";
import { useLivePhonemeDetection } from "../hooks/useLivePhonemeDetection";
import { CDN_BASE_URL } from "../services/firebaseConfig";

const ARTajwidOverlay = () => {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const detectedPhoneme = useLivePhonemeDetection();
  const [sceneReady, setSceneReady] = useState(false);
  const [mouthModel, setMouthModel] = useState<THREE.Object3D | null>(null);
  const [scene, setScene] = useState<THREE.Scene | null>(null);
  const [renderer, setRenderer] = useState<THREE.WebGLRenderer | null>(null);
  const [camera, setCamera] = useState<THREE.PerspectiveCamera | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Initialize Three.js scene, camera, and transparent renderer
    const sc = new THREE.Scene();
    const cam = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(70, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
    const rend = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ alpha: true });
    rend.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
    containerRef.current?.appendChild(rend.domElement);

    cam.position.set(0, 1.6, 2);
    setScene(sc);
    setCamera(cam);
    setRenderer(rend);
    setSceneReady(true);

    // Animation loop
    const animate = () => {
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      if (rend && sc && cam) {
        rend.render(sc, cam);
      }
    };
    animate();
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!sceneReady || !scene || !detectedPhoneme) return;

    // Load appropriate mouth model based on detected phoneme
    const loadMouthModel = async () => {
      const baseURL = await CDN_BASE_URL;
      const modelURL = `${baseURL}/mouthModels/${detectedPhoneme}.glb`;
      const loader = new (THREE as any).GLTFLoader();
      loader.load(modelURL, (gltf: any) => {
        if (mouthModel) scene.remove(mouthModel);

        const model = gltf.scene;
        model.scale.set(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
        model.position.set(0, 1.6, 1.8);
        scene.add(model);
        setMouthModel(model);
      });
    };

    loadMouthModel();
  }, [detectedPhoneme, sceneReady]);

  return <div ref={containerRef} style={{ position: "absolute", top: 0, left: 0 }} />;
};

export default ARTajwidOverlay;


6.3 vr/QuranicHistoryWalkthrough.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import * as THREE from "three";
import { CDN_BASE_URL } from "../services/firebaseConfig";

const QuranicHistoryWalkthrough = () => {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const scene = new THREE.Scene();
    const camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(75, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
    const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer();
    renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
    containerRef.current?.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

    camera.position.set(0, 0, 0);

    // Load 360° panorama from Firebase CDN
    (async () => {
      const baseURL = await CDN_BASE_URL;
      const imageURL = `${baseURL}/quranic_history/medina_panorama.jpg`;
      const loader = new THREE.TextureLoader();
      loader.load(imageURL, texture => {
        const sphereGeo = new THREE.SphereGeometry(500, 60, 40);
        sphereGeo.scale(-1, 1, 1);
        const sphereMat = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ map: texture });
        const sphere = new THREE.Mesh(sphereGeo, sphereMat);
        scene.add(sphere);
      });
    })();

    const animate = () => {
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      renderer.render(scene, camera);
    };
    animate();
  }, []);

  return <div ref={containerRef} style={{ width: "100%", height: "100vh" }} />;
};

export default QuranicHistoryWalkthrough;


6.4 vr/VirtualMosqueScene.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import * as THREE from "three";
import { GLTFLoader } from "three/examples/jsm/loaders/GLTFLoader";
import { CDN_BASE_URL } from "../services/firebaseConfig";

const VirtualMosqueScene = () => {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const scene = new THREE.Scene();
    scene.background = new THREE.Color(0xdddddd);

    const camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(75, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
    camera.position.set(0, 1.6, 3);

    const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true });
    renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
    containerRef.current?.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

    // Lights
    const ambLight = new THREE.AmbientLight(0xffffff, 0.8);
    scene.add(ambLight);

    const dirLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffffff, 0.5);
    dirLight.position.set(5, 10, 7.5);
    scene.add(dirLight);

    // Load mosque model from Firebase CDN
    (async () => {
      const baseURL = await CDN_BASE_URL;
      const gltfURL = `${baseURL}/mosqueModels/virtual_mosque.glb`;
      const loader = new GLTFLoader();
      loader.load(gltfURL, gltf => {
        gltf.scene.scale.set(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
        scene.add(gltf.scene);
      });
    })();

    // Floor
    const floorGeo = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(10, 10);
    const floorMat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({ color: 0xf0f0f0 });
    const floor = new THREE.Mesh(floorGeo, floorMat);
    floor.rotation.x = -Math.PI / 2;
    scene.add(floor);

    const animate = () => {
      requestAnimationFrame(animate);
      renderer.render(scene, camera);
    };
    animate();
  }, []);

  return <div ref={containerRef} style={{ width: "100%", height: "100vh" }} />;
};

export default VirtualMosqueScene;

import React from "react";

9. Completion Criteria

AR Tajwīd Overlay:

Real-time phoneme detection via useLivePhonemeDetection hook.

Correct mouth‐shape GLB models render over the camera in ARTajwidOverlay.tsx.

Assets load quickly from Firebase CDN.

VR Environments:

“Virtual Mosque” scene loads and renders correctly on desktop and WebXR headsets.

“Quranic History” 360° panorama displays properly and allows user navigation.

All 3D assets are served from Firebase Storage via CDN URLs.

Seamless UX:

React routing integrates AR/VR components under /ar/tajwid, /vr/history, and /vr/mosque.

Users can easily switch between standard lessons and immersive modes without page reload.

Performance is optimized (lazy loading, CDN‐served assets, minimal bundle size).



10. Next Step

Phase 12 – Settings & Personalization

 Add features to customize:

AR overlay sensitivity (phoneme detection threshold).

VR environment settings (ambient lighting, crowd density).

Notification preferences (Tajwīd reminders, session schedules).

Accessibility (font size, color themes, audio/video quality).

Please implement and test thoroughly. Once merged, we can begin drafting Phase 12 documentation and UI mockups.



Phase 11: VR/AR Integration

Overview: This phase integrates Virtual Reality (VR) and Augmented Reality (AR) technologies into the Quranic Education Platform, offering highly immersive and personalized learning and teaching experiences. The goal is to enhance the educational journey through dynamic, interactive environments that cater to both learners and teachers.

Objectives:

VR-based recitation immersion: Provide an environment for users to practice Quranic recitation in full immersion.

AR visualization for Tajweed: Assist learners in mastering proper pronunciation and articulation of Quranic verses.

Virtual classroom: Enable interactive, real-time learning with peers and instructors through WebRTC.

AI-generated visual enhancements: Dynamically personalize VR/AR experiences to suit individual learning needs.

Swarm intelligence optimization: Optimize system performance and manage user activities efficiently for a seamless experience.

AIService.ts

import * as tensorflow from '@tensorflow/tfjs-node';
import { SpeechClient } from '@google-cloud/speech';

const client = new SpeechClient();

export const initializeAIModel = async () => {
  const emotionModel = await tensorflow.loadLayersModel('path/to/emotionDetectionModel');
  const speechModel = await tensorflow.loadLayersModel('path/to/speechRecognitionModel');
  return { emotionModel, speechModel };
};

export const analyzeSpeech = async (audioInput: any) => {
  const audioText = await convertSpeechToText(audioInput);
  const emotion = await detectEmotion(audioText);
  return { text: audioText, emotion };
};

const convertSpeechToText = async (audioInput: any) => {
  const audioBytes = audioInput.toString('base64');
  const request = {
    audio: { content: audioBytes },
    config: {
      encoding: 'LINEAR16',
      sampleRateHertz: 16000,
      languageCode: 'en-US',
    },
  };

  const [response] = await client.recognize(request);
  return response.results.map(result => result.alternatives[0].transcript).join(' ');
};

const detectEmotion = async (text: string) => {
  const emotionModel = await initializeAIModel();
  const prediction = emotionModel.emotionModel.predict(text);
  return prediction;
};


VRService.ts

import { VRSessionModel } from '../models/VRSessionModel';

export const startVRSessionService = async (sessionData: any) => {
  const session = new VRSessionModel(sessionData);
  return await session.save();
};

export const endVRSessionService = async (sessionId: string) => {
  return await VRSessionModel.findOneAndUpdate(
    { sessionId },
    { endTime: new Date() },
    { new: true }
  );
};

Frontend Components:

1. ImmersiveRecitation.tsx

This component integrates Three.js for VR recitation, enabling immersive Quranic recitation.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import * as THREE from 'three';

const ImmersiveRecitation = () => {
  const [isRecording, setIsRecording] = useState(false);

  const startRecording = () => {
    // Initialize the Three.js scene for VR recitation
    const scene = new THREE.Scene();
    const camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(75, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
    const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer();
    renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
    document.body.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

    // Start VR session (potentially with WebXR)
    navigator.xr.requestSession('immersive-vr').then(session => {
      // Session logic for VR rendering and recitation
      setIsRecording(true);
    }).catch(error => console.error('Error starting VR session:', error));
  };

  const stopRecording = () => {
    // Stop VR recitation session
    setIsRecording(false);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Immersive Quranic Recitation</h2>
      <button onClick={startRecording} disabled={isRecording}>Start Recording</button>
      <button onClick={stopRecording} disabled={!isRecording}>Stop Recording</button>
      <div>{isRecording ? 'Recording in VR environment...' : 'Not recording'}</div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default ImmersiveRecitation;

    // AR.js Markers and interaction for Tajweed visualization

    tajweedRules.forEach(rule => {
      // Render AR content based on Tajweed rule (markers, colors)
      // This is a placeholder and can be customized further with AR.js

    }

    animate();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Interactive Tajweed Visualization</h3>

    </div>

3. VirtualClassroom.tsx

The virtual classroom component uses A-Frame (a 3D framework) to render the VR classroom environment, allowing for interaction with peers and instructors.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useEffect } from 'react';
import 'aframe';

const VirtualClassroom = () => {
  useEffect(() => {
    // VR setup for virtual classroom using A-Frame
    const scene = document.createElement('a-scene');
    const camera = document.createElement('a-camera');
    const instructorPodium = document.createElement('a-box');
    instructorPodium.setAttribute('position', '0 1.5 -3');
    instructorPodium.setAttribute('color', '#4CC3D9');

    scene.appendChild(camera);
    scene.appendChild(instructorPodium);

    document.body.appendChild(scene);
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>Virtual Classroom</h3>
      <div>3D VR classroom environment rendered here using A-Frame.</div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default VirtualClassroom;

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

const AIVisualEnhancements = () => {
  const [enhancements, setEnhancements] = useState('Awaiting AI adjustments...');

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchEnhancements = async () => {
      // Fetch AI-enhanced visual data from backend API
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-enhancements');
      const data = await response.json();
      setEnhancements(data.visualEnhancements);
    };

    fetchEnhancements();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>AI Visual Enhancements</h3>
      <p>{enhancements}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

const SwarmOrchestrator = () => {

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchStatus = async () => {
      const response = await fetch('/api/swarm-status');
      const data = await response.json();
      setStatus(data.status);
    };

    fetchStatus();
  }, []);

7. UnifiedLearningEnvironment.tsx

This component integrates AR/VR visualization tools into a unified learning environment for Quranic education.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

// Import necessary libraries for AR and VR
import * as THREE from 'three';  // Three.js for 3D rendering
import AR from 'ar.js';  // AR.js for Augmented Reality
import { VRButton } from 'three/examples/jsm/webxr/VRButton';  // For VR support

// Import components for the different phases (Recitation, Memory, Learning, and Teaching)
import RecitationDashboard from './RecitationDashboard';
import MemoryDashboard from './MemoryDashboard';
import LearningDashboard from './LearningDashboard';
import TeachingDashboard from './TeachingDashboard';

// AR/VR visualization for Tajweed (Using an external API for visualization)
import { ARTajweedVisualizer } from './ARTajweedVisualizer'; // External library for Tajweed AR
import { VRRoom } from './VRRoom';  // Import VR environment component
import { ARVisualization } from './ARVisualization'; // Import AR visualization component
import { InteractiveTajweed } from './InteractiveTajweed'; // AR Tajweed visualization
import { AIVisualEnhancements } from './AIVisualEnhancements';  // AI-driven visual enhancements
import { SwarmOrchestrator } from './SwarmOrchestrator'; // Swarm AI for optimization
import { startARLesson, triggerARContent } from './ARUtils'; // Utility functions for AR
import { startVRSession, endVRSession } from './VRUtils'; // Utility functions for VR sessions

const UnifiedLearningEnvironment = () => {
  const [activePhase, setActivePhase] = useState<string>('Recitation');
  const [isVRActive, setIsVRActive] = useState(false);
  const [arLessonStatus, setArLessonStatus] = useState('Start AR Lesson');
  const [aiEnhancements, setAIEnhancements] = useState('Loading AI visual adjustments...');
  const [swarmStatus, setSwarmStatus] = useState('Fetching swarm status...');

  // Initialize AR/VR scene
  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchAIEnhancements = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/ai-enhancements');
        const data = await response.json();
        setAIEnhancements(data.visualEnhancements);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching AI visual enhancements:', error);
      }
    };

    fetchAIEnhancements();

    // Fetch swarm intelligence status
    const fetchSwarmStatus = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/swarm-status');
        const data = await response.json();
        setSwarmStatus(data.status);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching swarm status:', error);
      }
    };

    fetchSwarmStatus();
  }, []);

  const handleStartARLesson = () => {
    setArLessonStatus('Starting AR lesson...');
    triggerARContent(); // Function for triggering AR-based content
    setArLessonStatus('AR Lesson ongoing...');
  };

  const handleStartVR = () => {
    startVRSession(); // Start VR session logic
    setIsVRActive(true);
  };

  const handleStopVR = () => {
    endVRSession(); // End VR session logic
    setIsVRActive(false);
  };

  const handlePhaseChange = (newPhase: string) => {
    setActivePhase(newPhase);
  };

  return (
    <div className="learning-environment">
      <h1>Phase 11: VR/AR Integration</h1>

      {/* Immersive VR Recitation */}
      <div className="vr-recitation">
        <h2>Immersive Quranic Recitation</h2>
        <button onClick={handleStartVR} disabled={isVRActive}>Start VR Session</button>
        <button onClick={handleStopVR} disabled={!isVRActive}>Stop VR Session</button>
        <p>{isVRActive ? 'Recording in VR environment...' : 'Not recording'}</p>
      </div>

      {/* AR-based Tajweed Visualization */}
      <div className="tajweed-visualization">
        <h3>Interactive Tajweed Visualization</h3>
        <InteractiveTajweed />  {/* AR interaction for Tajweed visualization */}
      </div>

      {/* Virtual Classroom */}
      <div className="virtual-classroom">
        <h3>Virtual Classroom</h3>
        <VRRoom />  {/* 3D Virtual classroom */}
      </div>

      {/* Interactive AR Lessons */}
      <div className="ar-interactive-lessons">
        <h3>Interactive AR Lessons</h3>
        <button onClick={handleStartARLesson}>Start AR Lesson</button>
        <p>{arLessonStatus}</p>
        <ARVisualization /> {/* AR rendering of interactive lessons */}
      </div>

      {/* AI-driven Visual Enhancements */}
      <div className="ai-visual-enhancements">
        <h3>AI Visual Enhancements</h3>
        <p>{aiEnhancements}</p>
      </div>

      {/* Swarm Intelligence Session Optimization */}
      <div className="swarm-orchestrator">
        <h3>Session Optimization Status (Swarm AI)</h3>
        <p>{swarmStatus}</p>
      </div>

      {/* Phase Navigation */}
      <nav>
        <ul>
          <li onClick={() => handlePhaseChange('Recitation')}>Recitation</li>
          <li onClick={() => handlePhaseChange('Memory')}>Memory</li>
          <li onClick={() => handlePhaseChange('Learning')}>Learning</li>
          <li onClick={() => handlePhaseChange('Teaching')}>Teaching</li>
        </ul>
      </nav>

      {/* Phase Dashboards */}
      {activePhase === 'Recitation' && <RecitationDashboard />}
      {activePhase === 'Memory' && <MemoryDashboard />}
      {activePhase === 'Learning' && <LearningDashboard />}
      {activePhase === 'Teaching' && <TeachingDashboard />}
    </div>
  );
};

export default UnifiedLearningEnvironment;




Summary:

Phase 11 introduces immersive Virtual Reality (VR) and Augmented Reality (AR) technologies to the Quran Education AI Platform, providing a highly engaging and interactive learning experience. Key features include VR recitation, AR-based Tajweed visualization, virtual classrooms, and AI-driven visual enhancements. Swarm AI optimizes the VR/AR sessions to ensure personalized and efficient content delivery.

Transition to Phase 12: Settings

Phase 12 will focus on comprehensive settings features to allow users to customize their learning environment and platform preferences for both educators and learners.





Prompt for Jules: Update Main Branch with Phase 12 – Offline & Global Access, Secure Billing, and Settings & Customization

 Jules, please update the main branch of the Quran Education AI Platform repository to integrate Phase 12: Offline & Global Access, Secure Billing & Donations, and Settings & Customization. This includes backend models, controllers, routes, and frontend components for:

Offline & Global Access: Core recitation lessons, memorization flashcards, and Qur’anic texts available offline; data sync queue to upload progress and recordings when connectivity resumes.

Secure Billing & Donations: Subscription tiers (free basic, advanced paid, institutional licensing) compliant with Islamic finance (no riba); a Zakat-eligible donation module with transparent fund allocation and impact reporting.

Settings & Customization: Multi-language support, offline mode via service workers, accessibility options, notification preferences, privacy management, and personalized learning settings.

Please ensure you:

Add or update backend models (SettingsModel.ts) to store each user’s settings and global billing/donation configurations.

Implement controllers for user settings, language, notification, privacy, offline mode, and personalization as provided.

Create/extend routes (settingsRoutes.ts) under /api/settings and register them in app.ts.

Write middleware (authenticateUser.ts) to ensure only authenticated users can access settings endpoints.

Add offline sync logic: a data-sync queue on the client that caches progress/recordings locally and pushes to server when the network is restored.

Implement a billing & donation backend—subscription plans that follow Islamic-finance rules (no riba) and a transparent donation module (e.g., Zakat eligibility).

On the frontend, create or update React components and context for:

Language selection (using react-i18next for i18n).

Notification preferences (email, SMS, in-app).

Privacy settings (data sharing, profile visibility).

Offline mode toggle (service worker registration and caching strategies).

Personalized learning settings (learning style, theme, difficulty).

Billing/subscription UI (plan selection, payment processing—for now, stub out integration with a compliant gateway).

Donation module UI (show fund pools, allow users to give Zakat, show impact reports).

Configure service workers to cache core recitation lessons, memorization flashcards, and Qur’anic text (e.g., via Workbox).

Ensure data sync from offline to online by queuing changes in IndexedDB (or similar) and uploading upon reconnection.

Use firebase or an equivalent for secure asset hosting (if needed).

Update documentation (README.md or a new docs file) describing Phase 12 setup steps, dependencies, and usage.

Follow existing coding standards; write unit/integration tests for new endpoints; test offline/online transitions and billing/donation flows.

Suggested commit message:

Add Phase 12: Offline & Global Access, Secure Billing & Donations, and Settings & Customization




Phase 12: Settings & Customization (Offline, Billing, and Custom Learning Environment)

📘 Overview

Phase 12 enhances user experience by providing offline access to core lessons, a robust billing and donation system compliant with Islamic finance principles, and a comprehensive settings & customization suite. Users can learn anywhere, donate transparently, and tailor the platform to their preferences.



🟢 1. Offline & Global Access

Core Recitation Lessons, Memorization Flashcards, Quranic Texts Available Offline:

Implement service workers to cache lesson data, flashcards, and Arabic script with minimal dependencies.

On first load (or when online), fetch and store these resources locally; fallback to cached versions when offline.

Data Sync Queue:

Store user progress (e.g., completed recitation sessions, flashcard mastery) and recorded audio in IndexedDB.

When connectivity is restored, automatically upload queued data (progress, recordings) to the server.

Show UI indicators for “Sync Pending” and “Synced” statuses.



🛡️ 2. Secure Billing & Donations

Subscription Tiers (Free Basic, Advanced Paid, Institutional Licensing):

Backend: Define a SubscriptionPlan model (e.g., MongoDB or SQL) with fields: name, price, features, complianceTags (e.g., “noRiba”).

Payments should integrate with a Shariah-compliant gateway (stub out or integrate with example test credentials).

Controllers to create/verify subscriptions, manage trial periods, and handle cancellations.

Ensure pricing logic does not involve interest; use one-time or recurring payments aligned with Islamic finance.

Zakat-Eligible Donation Module:

DonationFund model: fields: fundName, description, targetAmount, currentAmount, isZakatEligible.

Controller to accept donations, allocate to fund, and record donor details (anonymized if desired).

Impact reporting endpoints: show fund status, disbursements, and summary for transparency.

Frontend components: donation forms, fund list, progress bars, and impact reports.



⚙️ 3. Models & Backend Implementation

Models/SettingsModel.ts

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface ISettings extends Document {
  userId: string;
  language: string;
  notifications: {
    email: boolean;
    sms: boolean;
    inApp: boolean;
  };
  privacy: {
    dataSharing: boolean;
    profileVisibility: string;
  };
  offlineMode: boolean;
  personalization: {
    learningStyle: string;
    theme: string;
    difficulty: string;
  };
}

const SettingsSchema: Schema = new Schema({
  userId: { type: String, required: true, unique: true },
  language: { type: String, default: 'en' },
  notifications: {
    email: { type: Boolean, default: true },
    sms: { type: Boolean, default: false },
    inApp: { type: Boolean, default: true },
  },
  privacy: {
    dataSharing: { type: Boolean, default: true },
    profileVisibility: { type: String, default: 'public' },
  },
  offlineMode: { type: Boolean, default: false },
  personalization: {
    learningStyle: { type: String, default: 'visual' },
    theme: { type: String, default: 'light' },
    difficulty: { type: String, default: 'medium' },
  },
});

export const SettingsModel = mongoose.model<ISettings>('Settings', SettingsSchema);


Models/SubscriptionPlanModel.ts (example)

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface ISubscriptionPlan extends Document {
  name: string;
  price: number;            // in USD (or local currency); no interest
  features: string[];
  complianceTags: string[];  // e.g., ["noRiba"]
  tier: string;             // e.g., "free", "advanced", "institutional"
}

const SubscriptionPlanSchema: Schema = new Schema({
  name: { type: String, required: true },
  price: { type: Number, required: true },
  features: { type: [String], default: [] },
  complianceTags: { type: [String], default: [] },
  tier: { type: String, required: true },
});

export const SubscriptionPlan = mongoose.model<ISubscriptionPlan>(
  'SubscriptionPlan',
  SubscriptionPlanSchema
);


Models/DonationFundModel.ts

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface IDonationFund extends Document {
  fundName: string;
  description: string;
  targetAmount: number;
  currentAmount: number;
  isZakatEligible: boolean;
}

const DonationFundSchema: Schema = new Schema({
  fundName: { type: String, required: true },
  description: { type: String, required: true },
  targetAmount: { type: Number, required: true },
  currentAmount: { type: Number, default: 0 },
  isZakatEligible: { type: Boolean, default: false },
});

export const DonationFund = mongoose.model<IDonationFund>('DonationFund', DonationFundSchema);




🔧 4. Controllers

Controllers/UserSettingsController.ts

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { SettingsModel } from '../models/SettingsModel';

export const getUserSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;  // Auth middleware should set req.user
    const settings = await SettingsModel.findOne({ userId });
    if (!settings) {
      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'Settings not found' });
    }
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

export const updateUserSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const settingsData = req.body;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      settingsData,
      { new: true, upsert: true }
    );
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};


Controllers/LanguageSettingsController.ts

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { SettingsModel } from '../models/SettingsModel';
import { validateLanguage } from '../utils/validation';

export const updateLanguageSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { language } = req.body;
  if (!validateLanguage(language)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid language' });
  }

  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      { language },
      { new: true }
    );
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};


Controllers/NotificationSettingsController.ts

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { SettingsModel } from '../models/SettingsModel';

export const updateNotificationSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { email, sms, inApp } = req.body;
  if (typeof email !== 'boolean' || typeof sms !== 'boolean' || typeof inApp !== 'boolean') {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid notification preferences' });
  }

  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      { 'notifications.email': email, 'notifications.sms': sms, 'notifications.inApp': inApp },
      { new: true }
    );
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};


Controllers/PrivacySettingsController.ts

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { SettingsModel } from '../models/SettingsModel';

export const updatePrivacySettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { dataSharing, profileVisibility } = req.body;
  if (typeof dataSharing !== 'boolean' || !['public', 'private'].includes(profileVisibility)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid privacy preferences' });
  }

  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      { 'privacy.dataSharing': dataSharing, 'privacy.profileVisibility': profileVisibility },
      { new: true }
    );
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

export const updateOfflineMode = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {

  if (typeof offlineMode !== 'boolean') {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid offline mode' });
  }

  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      { offlineMode },
      { new: true }
    );
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

import { DonationFund } from '../models/DonationFundModel';

  res.status(200).json({ success: true, funds });
};

export const donate = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { fundId, amount } = req.body;
  // Process payment (compliant gateway), update fund’s currentAmount
  await DonationFund.findByIdAndUpdate(fundId, { $inc: { currentAmount: amount } });
  res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: 'Donation successful' });
};




5. Middleware & Utilities

Middleware/authenticateUser.ts

import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';

export const authenticateUser = (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
  if (!req.user) {
    return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'User not authenticated' });
  }
  next();
};


Utils/validation.ts

export const validateLanguage = (language: string) => {
  const validLanguages = ['en', 'ar', 'ur', 'fr', 'es'];
  return validLanguages.includes(language);
};

7. Server Setup (App.ts)

import express from 'express';
import mongoose from 'mongoose';
import settingsRoutes from './routes/settingsRoutes';
import billingRoutes from './routes/billingRoutes';
import donationRoutes from './routes/donationRoutes';

const app = express();
app.use(express.json());

// MongoDB connection
mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/quran_education', {
  useNewUrlParser: true,
  useUnifiedTopology: true,
}).then(() => console.log('Connected to MongoDB'))
  .catch(err => console.log('MongoDB connection error:', err));

// Register routes
app.use('/api/settings', settingsRoutes);
app.use('/api/billing', billingRoutes);
app.use('/api/donations', donationRoutes);

// Start server
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 5000;
app.listen(PORT, () => console.log(`Server is running on port ${PORT}`));




8. Frontend Implementation

services/settingsService.ts

import axios from 'axios';

const API_URL = '/api/settings';

const getUserSettings = async () => {
  const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/user-settings`);
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updateUserSettings = async (settingsData: any) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/user-settings`, settingsData);
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updateLanguageSettings = async (language: string) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/language`, { language });
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updateNotificationSettings = async (notificationSettings: any) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/notifications`, notificationSettings);
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updatePrivacySettings = async (privacySettings: any) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/privacy`, privacySettings);
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updateOfflineMode = async (offlineMode: boolean) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/offline-mode`, { offlineMode });
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updatePersonalizationSettings = async (personalizationSettings: any) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/personalization`, personalizationSettings);
  return response.data.settings;
};

export {
  getUserSettings,
  updateUserSettings,
  updateLanguageSettings,
  updateNotificationSettings,
  updatePrivacySettings,
  updateOfflineMode,
  updatePersonalizationSettings,
};


context/SettingsContext.tsx

import React, { createContext, useState, useContext, useEffect } from 'react';
import { getUserSettings } from '../services/settingsService';

interface SettingsContextType {
  settings: any;
  setSettings: React.Dispatch<React.SetStateAction<any>>;
}

const SettingsContext = createContext<SettingsContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export const SettingsProvider: React.FC = ({ children }) => {
  const [settings, setSettings] = useState<any>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchSettings = async () => {
      const data = await getUserSettings();
      setSettings(data);
    };
    fetchSettings();
  }, []);

  return (
    <SettingsContext.Provider value={{ settings, setSettings }}>
      {children}
    </SettingsContext.Provider>
  );
};

export const useSettings = () => {
  const context = useContext(SettingsContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useSettings must be used within a SettingsProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

components/Settings/LanguageSettings.tsx

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useSettings } from '../../context/SettingsContext';
import { updateLanguageSettings } from '../../services/settingsService';

const LanguageSettings: React.FC = () => {
  const { settings, setSettings } = useSettings();
  const [language, setLanguage] = useState(settings?.language || 'en');

  useEffect(() => {
    if (settings) setLanguage(settings.language);
  }, [settings]);

  const handleChange = async (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLSelectElement>) => {
    const selectedLanguage = e.target.value;
    const updated = await updateLanguageSettings(selectedLanguage);
    setSettings(updated);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Language Settings</h2>
      <select value={language} onChange={handleChange}>
        <option value="en">English</option>
        <option value="ar">Arabic</option>
        <option value="ur">Urdu</option>
        <option value="fr">French</option>
        <option value="es">Spanish</option>
      </select>
    </div>
  );
};

export default LanguageSettings;


components/Settings/NotificationSettings.tsx

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useSettings } from '../../context/SettingsContext';
import { updateNotificationSettings } from '../../services/settingsService';

const NotificationSettings: React.FC = () => {
  const { settings, setSettings } = useSettings();
  const [email, setEmail] = useState(true);
  const [sms, setSms] = useState(false);
  const [inApp, setInApp] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (settings) {
      setEmail(settings.notifications.email);
      setSms(settings.notifications.sms);
      setInApp(settings.notifications.inApp);
    }
  }, [settings]);

  const handleChange = async () => {
    const updated = await updateNotificationSettings({ email, sms, inApp });
    setSettings(updated);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Notification Settings</h2>
      <label>
        <input type="checkbox" checked={email} onChange={() => setEmail(!email)} />
        Email Notifications
      </label>
      <label>
        <input type="checkbox" checked={sms} onChange={() => setSms(!sms)} />
        SMS Notifications
      </label>
      <label>
        <input type="checkbox" checked={inApp} onChange={() => setInApp(!inApp)} />
        In-App Notifications
      </label>
      <button onClick={handleChange}>Save Settings</button>
    </div>
  );
};

export default NotificationSettings;


components/Settings/PrivacySettings.tsx

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useSettings } from '../../context/SettingsContext';
import { updatePrivacySettings } from '../../services/settingsService';

const PrivacySettings: React.FC = () => {
  const { settings, setSettings } = useSettings();
  const [dataSharing, setDataSharing] = useState(true);
  const [profileVisibility, setProfileVisibility] = useState('public');

  useEffect(() => {
    if (settings) {
      setDataSharing(settings.privacy.dataSharing);
      setProfileVisibility(settings.privacy.profileVisibility);
    }
  }, [settings]);

  const handleChange = async () => {
    const updated = await updatePrivacySettings({ dataSharing, profileVisibility });
    setSettings(updated);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Privacy Settings</h2>
      <label>
        <input type="checkbox" checked={dataSharing} onChange={() => setDataSharing(!dataSharing)} />
        Allow Data Sharing
      </label>
      <label>
        Profile Visibility
        <select value={profileVisibility} onChange={(e) => setProfileVisibility(e.target.value)}>
          <option value="public">Public</option>
          <option value="private">Private</option>
        </select>
      </label>
      <button onClick={handleChange}>Save Settings</button>
    </div>
  );
};

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useSettings } from '../../context/SettingsContext';
import { updatePersonalizationSettings } from '../../services/settingsService';

const PersonalizationSettings: React.FC = () => {
  const { settings, setSettings } = useSettings();
  const [learningStyle, setLearningStyle] = useState('visual');
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState('light');
  const [difficulty, setDifficulty] = useState('medium');

  useEffect(() => {
    if (settings) {
      setLearningStyle(settings.personalization.learningStyle);
      setTheme(settings.personalization.theme);
      setDifficulty(settings.personalization.difficulty);
    }

  const handleChange = async () => {
    const updated = await updatePersonalizationSettings({ learningStyle, theme, difficulty });
    setSettings(updated);
  };

      <h2>Personalization Settings</h2>
      <label>
        Learning Style
        <select value={learningStyle} onChange={(e) => setLearningStyle(e.target.value)}>
          <option value="visual">Visual</option>
          <option value="auditory">Auditory</option>
          <option value="kinesthetic">Kinesthetic</option>
        </select>
      </label>
      <label>
        Theme
        <select value={theme} onChange={(e) => setTheme(e.target.value)}>
          <option value="light">Light</option>
          <option value="dark">Dark</option>
        </select>
      </label>
      <label>
        Difficulty
        <select value={difficulty} onChange={(e) => setDifficulty(e.target.value)}>
          <option value="easy">Easy</option>
          <option value="medium">Medium</option>
          <option value="hard">Hard</option>
        </select>
      </label>
      <button onClick={handleChange}>Save Settings</button>
    </div>
  );
};
