components/Donations/DonationPage.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

const DonationPage: React.FC = () => {
  const [funds, setFunds] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [selectedFund, setSelectedFund] = useState<string>('');
  const [amount, setAmount] = useState<number>(0);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchFunds = async () => {
      const response = await axios.get('/api/donations/funds');
      setFunds(response.data.funds);
    };
    fetchFunds();
  }, []);

  const handleDonate = async () => {
    await axios.post('/api/donations/donate', { fundId: selectedFund, amount });
    alert('Donation successful');
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Donate</h1>
      <select value={selectedFund} onChange={(e) => setSelectedFund(e.target.value)}>
        <option value="">Select a fund</option>
        {funds.map(f => (
          <option key={f._id} value={f._id}>{f.fundName} — Raised ${f.currentAmount}/${f.targetAmount}</option>
        ))}
      </select>
      <input type="number" value={amount} onChange={(e) => setAmount(Number(e.target.value))} placeholder="Amount" />
      <button onClick={handleDonate}>Donate</button>
    </div>
  );
};

export default DonationPage;




9. Integrating Everything in App.tsx

import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import { SettingsProvider } from './context/SettingsContext';
import SettingsPage from './components/Settings/SettingsPage';
import BillingPage from './components/Billing/BillingPage';
import DonationPage from './components/Donations/DonationPage';
import HomePage from './HomePage';

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <SettingsProvider>
      <Router>
        <Switch>
          <Route path="/" exact component={HomePage} />
          <Route path="/settings" component={SettingsPage} />
          <Route path="/billing" component={BillingPage} />
          <Route path="/donate" component={DonationPage} />
        </Switch>
      </Router>
    </SettingsProvider>
  );
};

export default App;




🔍 Summary

Phase 12 delivers:

Offline & Global Access: Service workers caching core recitation lessons, flashcards, and Qur’anic text; data synchronization queue for offline progress.

Secure Billing & Donations: Subscription plans (no riba), Zakat-eligible donation module, transparent fund tracking.

Settings & Customization:

Language selection via react-i18next.

Notification preferences (email, SMS, in-app).

Privacy controls (data sharing, profile visibility).

Offline mode toggle with service worker registration.

Personalized learning (style, theme, difficulty).

Multilingual support (English, Arabic, Urdu, French, Spanish).

Accessibility features (screen reader labels, high-contrast themes, adjustable font sizes).

Please implement and test thoroughly—especially offline behavior, billing flows, and donation transparency—before merging.





Phase 12: Settings

Objective: Phase 12 enhances the user experience by offering customizable settings to personalize the learning environment. Key features include dynamic language selection with AI-powered translation, notification preferences, privacy management, offline mode, and personalized learning settings. These features are powered by robust backend APIs to ensure smooth interaction and real-time updates.

Key Features and Components:

Language Selection: Enables users to select their preferred language, including AI-powered dynamic translations and multiple language options (e.g., English, Arabic, Urdu, French, Spanish).

Notification Preferences: Allows users to select their preferred notification methods (email, SMS, in-app).

Privacy Management: Users can manage data-sharing preferences, control profile visibility, and specify AI data usage for personalized recommendations.

Offline Mode: Users can toggle offline mode for content availability without an internet connection.

Personalized Learning Settings: Lets users personalize their learning experience based on preferences (e.g., learning style, theme, difficulty).



Backend Implementation

Models/SettingsModel.ts

typescript

Copy code

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface ISettings extends Document {
  userId: string;
  language: string;
  notifications: {
    email: boolean;
    sms: boolean;
    inApp: boolean;
  };
  privacy: {
    dataSharing: boolean;
    profileVisibility: string;
  };
  offlineMode: boolean;
  personalization: {
    learningStyle: string;
    theme: string;
    difficulty: string;
  };
}

const SettingsSchema: Schema = new Schema({
  userId: { type: String, required: true, unique: true },
  language: { type: String, default: 'en' },
  notifications: {
    email: { type: Boolean, default: true },
    sms: { type: Boolean, default: false },
    inApp: { type: Boolean, default: true },
  },
  privacy: {
    dataSharing: { type: Boolean, default: true },
    profileVisibility: { type: String, default: 'public' },
  },
  offlineMode: { type: Boolean, default: false },
  personalization: {
    learningStyle: { type: String, default: 'visual' },
    theme: { type: String, default: 'light' },
    difficulty: { type: String, default: 'medium' },
  },
});

export const SettingsModel = mongoose.model<ISettings>('Settings', SettingsSchema);




Controllers/UserSettingsController.ts

typescript

Copy code

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { SettingsModel } from '../models/SettingsModel';

export const getUserSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;  // Assuming authentication middleware adds user ID to the request
    const settings = await SettingsModel.findOne({ userId });
    if (!settings) {
      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'Settings not found' });
    }
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

export const updateUserSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const settingsData = req.body;

    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate({ userId }, settingsData, { new: true, upsert: true });
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};




Controllers/LanguageSettingsController.ts

typescript

Copy code

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { SettingsModel } from '../models/SettingsModel';
import { validateLanguage } from '../utils/validation';

export const updateLanguageSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { language } = req.body;
  if (!validateLanguage(language)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid language' });
  }

  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      { language },
      { new: true }
    );
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};




Controllers/NotificationSettingsController.ts

typescript

Copy code

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { SettingsModel } from '../models/SettingsModel';

export const updateNotificationSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { email, sms, inApp } = req.body;

  if (typeof email !== 'boolean' || typeof sms !== 'boolean' || typeof inApp !== 'boolean') {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid notification preferences' });
  }

  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      { 'notifications.email': email, 'notifications.sms': sms, 'notifications.inApp': inApp },
      { new: true }
    );
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};

export const updatePrivacySettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {

  }

  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      { 'privacy.dataSharing': dataSharing, 'privacy.profileVisibility': profileVisibility },
      { new: true }
    );

  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });

Controllers/OfflineModeController.ts

Copy code

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { SettingsModel } from '../models/SettingsModel';

export const updateOfflineMode = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { offlineMode } = req.body;

  if (typeof offlineMode !== 'boolean') {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid offline mode' });
  }

  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      { offlineMode },
      { new: true }
    );
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};




Controllers/PersonalizationController.ts

typescript

Copy code

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { SettingsModel } from '../models/SettingsModel';

export const updatePersonalizationSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { learningStyle, theme, difficulty } = req.body;

  try {
    const userId = req.user.id;
    const updatedSettings = await SettingsModel.findOneAndUpdate(
      { userId },
      { 'personalization.learningStyle': learningStyle, 'personalization.theme': theme, 'personalization.difficulty': difficulty },
      { new: true }
    );
    res.status(200).json({ success: true, settings: updatedSettings });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: error.message });
  }
};




Middleware/authenticateUser.ts

typescript

Copy code

import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';

export const authenticateUser = (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
  if (!req.user) {
    return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'User not authenticated' });
  }
  next();
};

Copy code

export const validateLanguage = (language: string) => {
  const validLanguages = ['en', 'ar', 'ur', 'fr', 'es'];  // Add more languages as needed
  return validLanguages.includes(language);
};




Routes/settingsRoutes.ts

typescript

Copy code

import express from 'express';
import { authenticateUser } from '../middleware/authenticateUser';
import { updateUserSettings, getUserSettings } from '../controllers/UserSettingsController';
import { updateLanguageSettings } from '../controllers/LanguageSettingsController';
import { updateNotificationSettings } from '../controllers/NotificationSettingsController';
import { updatePrivacySettings } from '../controllers/PrivacySettingsController';
import { updateOfflineMode } from '../controllers/OfflineModeController';
import { updatePersonalizationSettings } from '../controllers/PersonalizationController';

const router = express.Router();

// Middleware to ensure user is authenticated
router.use(authenticateUser);

// User settings routes
router.get('/user-settings', getUserSettings);
router.put('/user-settings', updateUserSettings);

// Language settings
router.put('/language', updateLanguageSettings);

// Notification settings
router.put('/notifications', updateNotificationSettings);

// Privacy settings
router.put('/privacy', updatePrivacySettings);

// Offline mode settings
router.put('/offline-mode', updateOfflineMode);

// Personalization settings
router.put('/personalization', updatePersonalizationSettings);

export default router;




Server Setup (App.ts)

typescript

import express from 'express';
import mongoose from 'mongoose';
import settingsRoutes from './routes/settingsRoutes';

const app = express();

// Middleware to parse JSON request bodies
app.use(express.json());

// Connect to MongoDB
mongoose.connect('mongodb://localhost:27017/quran_education', { useNewUrlParser: true, useUnifiedTopology: true })
  .then(() => console.log('Connected to MongoDB'))
  .catch(err => console.log('MongoDB connection error:', err));

// Register settings routes
app.use('/api/settings', settingsRoutes);

// Start the server
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 5000;
app.listen(PORT, () => console.log(`Server is running on port ${PORT}`));

services/settingsService.ts

This file contains functions to interact with the backend API for updating settings.

typescript

Copy code

import axios from 'axios';

const API_URL = '/api/settings';

const getUserSettings = async () => {
  const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/user-settings`);
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updateUserSettings = async (settingsData: any) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/user-settings`, settingsData);
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updateLanguageSettings = async (language: string) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/language`, { language });
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updateNotificationSettings = async (notificationSettings: any) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/notifications`, notificationSettings);
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updatePrivacySettings = async (privacySettings: any) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/privacy`, privacySettings);
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updateOfflineMode = async (offlineMode: boolean) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/offline-mode`, { offlineMode });
  return response.data.settings;
};

const updatePersonalizationSettings = async (personalizationSettings: any) => {
  const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/personalization`, personalizationSettings);
  return response.data.settings;
};

export {
  getUserSettings,
  updateUserSettings,
  updateLanguageSettings,
  updateNotificationSettings,
  updatePrivacySettings,
  updateOfflineMode,
  updatePersonalizationSettings,
};




context/SettingsContext.tsx

This context manages the global settings state, which will be accessed by various components.

typescript

Copy code

import React, { createContext, useState, useContext, useEffect } from 'react';
import { getUserSettings } from '../services/settingsService';

interface SettingsContextType {
  settings: any;
  setSettings: React.Dispatch<React.SetStateAction<any>>;
}

const SettingsContext = createContext<SettingsContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export const SettingsProvider: React.FC = ({ children }) => {
  const [settings, setSettings] = useState<any>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchSettings = async () => {
      const data = await getUserSettings();
      setSettings(data);
    };
    fetchSettings();
  }, []);

  return (
    <SettingsContext.Provider value={{ settings, setSettings }}>
      {children}
    </SettingsContext.Provider>
  );
};

export const useSettings = () => {
  const context = useContext(SettingsContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useSettings must be used within a SettingsProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

components/Settings/LanguageSettings.tsx

This component allows the user to update their language settings.

typescript

Copy code

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useSettings } from '../../context/SettingsContext';
import { updateLanguageSettings } from '../../services/settingsService';

const LanguageSettings: React.FC = () => {
  const { settings, setSettings } = useSettings();
  const [language, setLanguage] = useState(settings?.language || 'en');

  const handleChange = async (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLSelectElement>) => {
    const selectedLanguage = e.target.value;
    const updatedSettings = await updateLanguageSettings(selectedLanguage);
    setSettings(updatedSettings);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Language Settings</h2>
      <select value={language} onChange={handleChange}>
        <option value="en">English</option>
        <option value="ar">Arabic</option>
        <option value="ur">Urdu</option>
        <option value="fr">French</option>
        <option value="es">Spanish</option>
      </select>
    </div>
  );
};

export default LanguageSettings;




components/Settings/NotificationSettings.tsx

This component handles the user’s notification preferences.

typescript

Copy code

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useSettings } from '../../context/SettingsContext';
import { updateNotificationSettings } from '../../services/settingsService';

const NotificationSettings: React.FC = () => {
  const { settings, setSettings } = useSettings();
  const [email, setEmail] = useState(settings?.notifications?.email || true);
  const [sms, setSms] = useState(settings?.notifications?.sms || false);
  const [inApp, setInApp] = useState(settings?.notifications?.inApp || true);

  const handleChange = async () => {
    const updatedSettings = await updateNotificationSettings({ email, sms, inApp });
    setSettings(updatedSettings);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Notification Settings</h2>
      <label>
        <input type="checkbox" checked={email} onChange={() => setEmail(!email)} />
        Email Notifications
      </label>
      <label>
        <input type="checkbox" checked={sms} onChange={() => setSms(!sms)} />
        SMS Notifications
      </label>
      <label>
        <input type="checkbox" checked={inApp} onChange={() => setInApp(!inApp)} />
        In-App Notifications
      </label>
      <button onClick={handleChange}>Save Settings</button>
    </div>
  );
};

export default NotificationSettings;




components/Settings/PrivacySettings.tsx

This component allows the user to manage their privacy settings.

typescript

Copy code

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useSettings } from '../../context/SettingsContext';
import { updatePrivacySettings } from '../../services/settingsService';

const PrivacySettings: React.FC = () => {
  const { settings, setSettings } = useSettings();
  const [dataSharing, setDataSharing] = useState(settings?.privacy?.dataSharing || true);
  const [profileVisibility, setProfileVisibility] = useState(settings?.privacy?.profileVisibility || 'public');

  const handleChange = async () => {
    const updatedSettings = await updatePrivacySettings({ dataSharing, profileVisibility });
    setSettings(updatedSettings);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Privacy Settings</h2>
      <label>
        <input type="checkbox" checked={dataSharing} onChange={() => setDataSharing(!dataSharing)} />
        Allow Data Sharing
      </label>
      <label>
        <select value={profileVisibility} onChange={(e) => setProfileVisibility(e.target.value)}>
          <option value="public">Public</option>
          <option value="private">Private</option>
        </select>
        Profile Visibility
      </label>
      <button onClick={handleChange}>Save Settings</button>
    </div>
  );
};

export default PrivacySettings;

3. Integrating Everything

To integrate all these components into your App.tsx:

typescript

Copy code

import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Route, Switch } from 'react-router-dom';
import { SettingsProvider } from './context/SettingsContext';
import SettingsPage from './components/Settings/SettingsPage';

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <SettingsProvider>
      <Router>
        <Switch>
          <Route path="/settings" component={SettingsPage} />
        </Switch>
      </Router>
    </SettingsProvider>
  );
};

export default App;

The platform supports language selection with AI-driven dynamic translation (including Urdu), customizable notification preferences, privacy settings, offline mode, and personalized learning features. The backend is designed to persist these settings in a database and ensure real-time updates. This phase ensures that users have a highly customizable, dynamic, and responsive experience.

Phase 13: Admin & Security, Sharia & Ethics Compliance, Privacy & Security, and Admin Dashboard & AI Analytics



1. Admin & Security

Centralized Admin Console

 • User management (view, edit, delete, assign roles)

 • Role assignment (e.g., “user”, “admin”, “moderator”)

 • Content moderation (approve/reject user-generated content)

Threat Detection

 • Integrate Cloud IAP (Identity-Aware Proxy) for per-endpoint access control

 • Audit logs in Cloud Logging (track every admin action)

GDPR & Sharia Compliance

 • Data-retention policies (e.g., purge user logs after 90 days; archive Sharia audit logs)

 • “Right to be forgotten” workflow: securely delete all personal data on user’s request

2. Sharia & Ethics Compliance

Scholar-Led Governance Board

 • Periodic Sharia audits of content, payments, AI recommendations

GDPR-Aligned Data Practices

 • Transparent data collection, consent records, audit trail

Transparent AI-Ethics Guidelines

 • Document how AI models handle user data, ensure no bias, fully auditable

Islamic Finance in Payment/Donation Flows

 • No Riba (interest) in subscription billing

 • Real-time Zakat audit logs for donation module

3. Privacy & Security

End-to-End Encryption (AES-256)

 • Encrypt all personal and recitation data at rest (MongoDB) using field-level AES-256

 • Enforce HTTPS/TLS for data in transit

Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) & Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA)

 • Only “admin” role can access admin routes

 • Require MFA for any role elevation or sensitive operations

GDPR & Sharia Data Ethics Compliance

 • User data remains private; any analytics data is fully anonymized

 • Consent stored in a separate collection; data deletion upon request



4. Admin Dashboard & AI Analytics

Objective:

 Create a comprehensive Admin Dashboard and AI Analytics interface where administrators can:

View AI-driven insights (user engagement, content performance, learning progress)

Manage users (view details, assign roles, delete accounts)

Moderate content (approve/reject pending submissions)

Configure platform settings (notifications, filtering thresholds)

Observe AI usage metrics (total API calls, active sessions, model performance)

Enforce RBAC so only Admins can access the dashboard

4.1 Backend Files

src/models/User.ts

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface IUser extends Document {
  name: string;
  email: string;
  role: string;
}

const userSchema = new Schema<IUser>({
  name: { type: String, required: true },
  email: { type: String, required: true, unique: true },
  role: { type: String, required: true, default: 'user' },
});

const User = mongoose.model<IUser>('User', userSchema);
export { User };


src/models/Content.ts

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface IContent extends Document {
  title: string;
  body: string;
  status: string; // e.g., 'pending', 'approved', 'rejected'
}

const contentSchema = new Schema<IContent>({
  title: { type: String, required: true },
  body: { type: String, required: true },
  status: { type: String, required: true, default: 'pending' },
});

const Content = mongoose.model<IContent>('Content', contentSchema);
export { Content };


src/models/PlatformSettings.ts

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface IPlatformSettings extends Document {
  notificationEnabled: boolean;
  contentFiltering: string; // e.g., 'low', 'medium', 'high'
}

const platformSettingsSchema = new Schema<IPlatformSettings>({
  notificationEnabled: { type: Boolean, required: true, default: true },
  contentFiltering: { type: String, required: true, default: 'medium' },
});

const PlatformSettings = mongoose.model<IPlatformSettings>(
  'PlatformSettings',
  platformSettingsSchema
);
export { PlatformSettings };


src/models/AIUsageStats.ts

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface IAIUsageStats extends Document {
  totalUsage: number;
  activeSessions: number;
}

const aiUsageStatsSchema = new Schema<IAIUsageStats>({
  totalUsage: { type: Number, required: true },
  activeSessions: { type: Number, required: true },
});

const AIUsageStats = mongoose.model<IAIUsageStats>(
  'AIUsageStats',
  aiUsageStatsSchema
);
export { AIUsageStats };


src/controllers/adminController.ts

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { User } from '../models/User';
import { Content } from '../models/Content';
import { PlatformSettings } from '../models/PlatformSettings';
import { AIUsageStats } from '../models/AIUsageStats';

// Get AI Insights
export const getAIInsights = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    // Example static insights; replace with real analytics logic
    const insights = {
      userEngagement: 2500,
      popularContent: 'Quranic Studies 101',
      learningCompletion: 78,
    };
    res.json(insights);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch AI insights' });
  }
};

// Get Users
export const getUsers = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const users = await User.find();
    res.json(users);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch users' });
  }
};

// Update User Role
export const updateUserRole = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { userId } = req.params;
  const { role } = req.body;
  try {
    const user = await User.findById(userId);
    if (!user) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'User not found' });
    }
    user.role = role;
    await user.save();
    res.status(200).json(user);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to update user role' });
  }
};

// Get Pending Content
export const getContent = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const content = await Content.find({ status: 'pending' });
    res.json(content);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch pending content' });
  }
};

// Approve Content
export const approveContent = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { contentId } = req.params;
  try {
    const content = await Content.findById(contentId);
    if (!content) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Content not found' });
    }
    content.status = 'approved';
    await content.save();
    res.status(200).json(content);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to approve content' });
  }
};

// Get AI Usage Stats
export const getAIUsageStats = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const stats = await AIUsageStats.findOne();
    if (!stats) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'AI usage stats not found' });
    }
    res.json(stats);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch AI usage stats' });
  }
};

// Update Platform Settings
export const updatePlatformSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { notificationEnabled, contentFiltering } = req.body;
  try {
    const settings = await PlatformSettings.findOne();
    if (!settings) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Settings not found' });
    }
    settings.notificationEnabled = notificationEnabled;
    settings.contentFiltering = contentFiltering;
    await settings.save();
    res.status(200).json(settings);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to update platform settings' });
  }
};


src/routes/adminRoutes.ts

import { Router } from 'express';
import {
  getAIInsights,
  getUsers,
  updateUserRole,
  getContent,
  approveContent,
  getAIUsageStats,
  updatePlatformSettings,
} from '../controllers/adminController';
import { authenticateAdmin } from '../middleware/authorizeRole'; // RBAC middleware

const router = Router();

// Admin API Routes (protected by RBAC)
router.get('/ai-analytics', authenticateAdmin, getAIInsights);
router.get('/users', authenticateAdmin, getUsers);
router.put('/users/:userId/role', authenticateAdmin, updateUserRole);
router.get('/content', authenticateAdmin, getContent);
router.post('/content/:contentId/approve', authenticateAdmin, approveContent);
router.get('/ai-usage', authenticateAdmin, getAIUsageStats);
router.post('/settings', authenticateAdmin, updatePlatformSettings);

export default router;


src/services/adminService.ts

import axios from 'axios';

const API_URL = process.env.API_URL || 'http://localhost:5000/admin';

// Fetch AI Insights
export const fetchAIInsights = async () => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/ai-analytics`);
    return response.data;
  } catch {
    throw new Error('Error fetching AI insights');
  }
};

// Fetch Users
export const fetchUsers = async () => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/users`);
    return response.data;
  } catch {
    throw new Error('Error fetching users');
  }
};

// Update User Role
export const updateUserRole = async (userId: string, role: string) => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.put(`${API_URL}/users/${userId}/role`, { role });
    return response.data;
  } catch {
    throw new Error('Error updating user role');
  }
};

// Fetch Pending Content
export const fetchPendingContent = async () => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/content`);
    return response.data;
  } catch {
    throw new Error('Error fetching content');
  }
};

// Approve Content
export const approveContent = async (contentId: string) => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/content/${contentId}/approve`);
    return response.data;
  } catch {
    throw new Error('Error approving content');
  }
};

// Fetch AI Usage Stats
export const fetchAIUsageStats = async () => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/ai-usage`);
    return response.data;
  } catch {
    throw new Error('Error fetching AI usage stats');
  }
};

// Update Platform Settings
export const updatePlatformSettings = async (settings: {
  notificationEnabled: boolean;
  contentFiltering: string;
}) => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/settings`, settings);
    return response.data;
  } catch {
    throw new Error('Error updating platform settings');
  }
};


src/middleware/authorizeRole.ts (RBAC & MFA)

import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';

export const authenticateAdmin = (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
  try {
    const token = req.headers.authorization?.split(' ')[1];
    if (!token) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'No token provided' });
    const payload = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET as string) as any;
    if (payload.role !== 'admin') {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: Admins only' });
    }
    // Optionally, check MFA flag in payload
    next();
  } catch {
    res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid token' });
  }
};

src/pages/AdminDashboard.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { fetchAIInsights, fetchUsers, fetchPendingContent, fetchAIUsageStats } from '../services/adminService';
import UserManagement from '../components/UserManagement';
import ContentApproval from '../components/ContentApproval';
import PlatformSettings from '../components/PlatformSettings';
import AIUsageInsights from '../components/AIUsageInsights';

const AdminDashboard: React.FC = () => {
  const [aiInsights, setAIInsights] = useState<any>(null);
  const [users, setUsers] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [content, setContent] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [aiUsageStats, setAIUsageStats] = useState<any>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const loadData = async () => {
      try {
        const [insights, usersData, pendingContent, usageStats] = await Promise.all([
          fetchAIInsights(),
          fetchUsers(),
          fetchPendingContent(),
          fetchAIUsageStats(),
        ]);
        setAIInsights(insights);
        setUsers(usersData);
        setContent(pendingContent);
        setAIUsageStats(usageStats);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading admin data:', error);
      }
    };
    loadData();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="admin-dashboard">
      <h1>Admin Dashboard</h1>

      <section>
        <h2>AI Insights</h2>
        {aiInsights && <AIUsageInsights data={aiInsights} />}
      </section>

      <section>
        <h2>User Management</h2>
        <UserManagement users={users} />
      </section>

      <section>
        <h2>Content Approval</h2>
        <ContentApproval content={content} />
      </section>

      <section>
        <h2>Platform Settings</h2>
        <PlatformSettings />
      </section>

      <section>
        <h2>AI Usage Stats</h2>
        {aiUsageStats && <AIUsageInsights data={aiUsageStats} />}
      </section>
    </div>
  );
};

export default AdminDashboard;

const UserManagement: React.FC<{ users: any[] }> = ({ users }) => {

    try {
      await updateUserRole(userId, role);
      // Ideally refresh user list or update local state
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error updating user role:', error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <table>
        <thead>

            <th>Name</th><th>Email</th><th>Role</th><th>Actions</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>

              <td>{user.name}</td>
              <td>{user.email}</td>
              <td>{user.role}</td>

                <select
                  value={user.role}
                  onChange={(e) => handleRoleChange(user._id, e.target.value)}
                >
                  <option value="user">User</option>
                  <option value="admin">Admin</option>
                  <option value="moderator">Moderator</option>
                </select>
              </td>
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  );
};

Phase 13: Admin Dashboard and AI Analytics

Objective:

Phase 13 focuses on the creation of a comprehensive Admin Dashboard and AI Analytics. This dashboard will include multiple management features like AI insights, user management, content approval, platform settings, and AI usage stats. The goal is to provide the admin with full control and visibility over the platform’s operations, user activity, and content, along with AI-driven insights to optimize user engagement.

Key Features:

AI Analytics Dashboard: Provides insights into user engagement, content performance, and AI-driven learning progress.

User Management: Allows the admin to manage users, view details, and assign roles.

Content Approval: Enables the admin to approve or reject content before it becomes publicly available.

Platform Settings: Allows the admin to configure platform-wide settings such as notifications and content filtering.

AI Usage Insights: Provides data on the AI models' performance and usage metrics.

Admin Dashboard: Central hub for accessing all of the above features.

Role-Based Access Control (RBAC): For controlling user access to different admin functionalities.



Backend Files:

Let's consolidate all of the backend files, including necessary models, controllers, routes, and services, ensuring full functionality of all features.

src/models/User.ts

typescript

Copy code

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface IUser extends Document {
  name: string;
  email: string;
  role: string;
}

const userSchema = new Schema<IUser>({
  name: { type: String, required: true },
  email: { type: String, required: true, unique: true },
  role: { type: String, required: true, default: 'user' },
});

const User = mongoose.model<IUser>('User', userSchema);

export { User };


src/models/Content.ts

typescript

Copy code

import mongoose, { Schema, Document } from 'mongoose';

interface IContent extends Document {
  title: string;
  body: string;
  status: string;
}

const contentSchema = new Schema<IContent>({
  title: { type: String, required: true },
  body: { type: String, required: true },
  status: { type: String, required: true, default: 'pending' },
});

const Content = mongoose.model<IContent>('Content', contentSchema);

export { Content };

interface IPlatformSettings extends Document {
  notificationEnabled: boolean;
  contentFiltering: string;
}

const platformSettingsSchema = new Schema<IPlatformSettings>({
  notificationEnabled: { type: Boolean, required: true, default: true },
  contentFiltering: { type: String, required: true, default: 'medium' },
});

const PlatformSettings = mongoose.model<IPlatformSettings>('PlatformSettings', platformSettingsSchema);

export { PlatformSettings };

src/controllers/adminController.ts

typescript

Copy code

import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { User } from '../models/User';
import { Content } from '../models/Content';
import { PlatformSettings } from '../models/PlatformSettings';
import { AIUsageStats } from '../models/AIUsageStats';

// Get AI Insights
export const getAIInsights = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const insights = {
      userEngagement: 2500,
      popularContent: 'Quranic Studies 101',
      learningCompletion: 78,
    };
    res.json(insights);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch AI insights' });
  }
};

// Get Users
export const getUsers = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const users = await User.find();
    res.json(users);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch users' });
  }
};

// Update User Role
export const updateUserRole = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { userId } = req.params;
  const { role } = req.body;
  try {
    const user = await User.findById(userId);
    if (!user) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'User not found' });
    }
    user.role = role;
    await user.save();
    res.status(200).json(user);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to update user role' });
  }
};

// Get Pending Content
export const getContent = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const content = await Content.find({ status: 'pending' });
    res.json(content);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch pending content' });
  }
};

// Approve Content
export const approveContent = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { contentId } = req.params;
  try {
    const content = await Content.findById(contentId);
    if (!content) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Content not found' });
    }
    content.status = 'approved';
    await content.save();
    res.status(200).json(content);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to approve content' });
  }
};

// Get AI Usage Stats
export const getAIUsageStats = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const stats = await AIUsageStats.findOne();
    if (!stats) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'AI usage stats not found' });
    }
    res.json(stats);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch AI usage stats' });
  }
};

// Update Platform Settings
export const updatePlatformSettings = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  const { notificationEnabled, contentFiltering } = req.body;
  try {
    const settings = await PlatformSettings.findOne();
    if (!settings) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Settings not found' });
    }
    settings.notificationEnabled = notificationEnabled;
    settings.contentFiltering = contentFiltering;
    await settings.save();
    res.status(200).json(settings);
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to update platform settings' });
  }
};


src/routes/adminRoutes.ts

typescript

Copy code

import { Router } from 'express';
import { getAIInsights, getUsers, updateUserRole, getContent, approveContent, getAIUsageStats, updatePlatformSettings } from '../controllers/adminController';

const router = Router();

// Admin API Routes
router.get('/ai-analytics', getAIInsights);
router.get('/users', getUsers);
router.put('/users/:userId/role', updateUserRole);
router.get('/content', getContent);
router.post('/content/:contentId/approve', approveContent);
router.get('/ai-usage', getAIUsageStats);
router.post('/settings', updatePlatformSettings);

export default router;

Phase 13: Admin Dashboard and AI Analytics (Frontend)

Now that the backend is covered, let's focus on the frontend files and components needed to create the Admin Dashboard with all of the requested features. This will include the components to manage AI Analytics, Content Approval, User Management, Platform Settings, and AI Usage Insights.

1. src/pages/AdminDashboard.tsx

This will be the main admin dashboard page that renders all of the admin components.

tsx

Copy code

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { fetchAIInsights, fetchUsers, fetchPendingContent, fetchAIUsageStats } from '../services/adminService';
import UserManagement from '../components/UserManagement';
import ContentApproval from '../components/ContentApproval';
import PlatformSettings from '../components/PlatformSettings';
import AIUsageInsights from '../components/AIUsageInsights';

const AdminDashboard: React.FC = () => {
  const [aiInsights, setAIInsights] = useState<any>(null);
  const [users, setUsers] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [content, setContent] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [aiUsageStats, setAIUsageStats] = useState<any>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Fetch the data
    const loadData = async () => {
      try {
        const aiInsightsData = await fetchAIInsights();
        const usersData = await fetchUsers();
        const pendingContentData = await fetchPendingContent();
        const aiUsageStatsData = await fetchAIUsageStats();

        setAIInsights(aiInsightsData);
        setUsers(usersData);
        setContent(pendingContentData);
        setAIUsageStats(aiUsageStatsData);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error loading data:', error);
      }
    };

    loadData();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="admin-dashboard">
      <h1>Admin Dashboard</h1>
      <section>
        <h2>AI Insights</h2>
        {aiInsights && <AIUsageInsights data={aiInsights} />}
      </section>

      <section>
        <h2>User Management</h2>
        <UserManagement users={users} />
      </section>

      <section>
        <h2>Content Approval</h2>
        <ContentApproval content={content} />
      </section>

      <section>
        <h2>Platform Settings</h2>
        <PlatformSettings />
      </section>

      <section>
        <h2>AI Usage Stats</h2>
        {aiUsageStats && <AIUsageInsights data={aiUsageStats} />}
      </section>
    </div>
  );
};

export default AdminDashboard;

✅ BACKEND IMPLEMENTATION

1. Services (src/services)

aiAgentService.ts

Coordinates multi-agent system logic

Fetches/stores AgentModel and uses swarm data to generate learning suggestions

guidanceAssistantService.ts

Processes text or voice input via STT (Speech-to-Text)

Runs message through GPT-4 or sentiment-analysis pipeline

Returns text + TTS audio (Howler.js/Web Speech API)

swarmIntelligenceService.ts

Analyzes collective user behavior

Uses advanced algorithms (e.g., Ant Colony, Particle Swarm) to generate insights

Updates SwarmModel in MongoDB and caches results in Redis

userProfileService.ts

CRUD operations on UserProfileModel

Manages preferences (theme, accessibility, avatar settings)

Fetches / updates learning progress, engagement, mood

aiCore.service.ts

Central AI orchestration pipeline

Loads TensorFlow.js/PyTorch models for feedback, reinforcement learning

Routes incoming telemetry to ML models and returns personalized adjustments

feedback.service.ts

Receives feedback from UI (quizzes, recitations, avatar interactions)

Sanitizes + logs into FeedbackModel

Pushes events to Kafka feedback stream

export const getUserProfile = async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
  try {
    const profile = await getUserProfile(req.body.userId);
    return res.json(profile);
  } catch (err) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
  }
};

    const { progress } = req.body;

  } catch (err) {

  }
};

3. Middleware (src/middleware/authMiddleware.ts)

import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';

export const authMiddleware = (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
  const token = req.headers.authorization?.split(' ')[1];
  if (!token) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Access token missing' });
  }
  try {
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET as string) as any;
    req.body.userId = decoded.sub; // Attach userId for downstream services
    next();
  } catch (err) {
    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Invalid token' });
  }
};

5. App Initialization (src/app.ts)

import express from 'express';
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import bodyParser from 'body-parser';
import userRoutes from './routes/userRoutes';
import swarmRoutes from './routes/swarmRoutes';
import feedbackRoutes from './routes/feedbackRoutes';
import agentRoutes from './routes/agentRoutes';
import assistantRoutes from './routes/assistantRoutes';

dotenv.config();

const app = express();
app.use(bodyParser.json());
app.use('/api/users', userRoutes);
app.use('/api/swarm', swarmRoutes);
app.use('/api/feedback', feedbackRoutes);
app.use('/api/agent', agentRoutes);
app.use('/api/assistant', assistantRoutes);

// Health check
app.get('/health', (req, res) => res.send('OK'));

export default app;




6. Server Entry (src/server.ts)

import mongoose from 'mongoose';
import Redis from 'ioredis';
import { Kafka } from 'kafkajs';
import app from './app';

const PORT = process.env.PORT || 5000;

// Initialize Redis
export const redisClient = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL!);

// Initialize Kafka
export const kafka = new Kafka({ clientId: 'quran-platform', brokers: [process.env.KAFKA_BROKER!] });

// Connect to MongoDB
mongoose.connect(process.env.MONGODB_URI!, { useNewUrlParser: true, useUnifiedTopology: true })
  .then(() => console.log('MongoDB connected'))
  .catch(err => console.error('MongoDB connection error:', err));

// Start server only after Redis & Kafka are ready
Promise.all([
  redisClient.ping(),
  kafka.admin().connect()
]).then(() => {
  app.listen(PORT, () => {
    console.log(`Server listening on port ${PORT}`);
  });
}).catch(err => {
  console.error('Failed to initialize Kafka/Redis:', err);
  process.exit(1);
});

2. Context: src/context/UserProfileContext.tsx

import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect, ReactNode } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

// Define the shape of UserProfile
interface UserProfile {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  age: number;
  gender: 'male' | 'female';
  learningLevel: 'beginner' | 'intermediate' | 'advanced';
  themePreference: 'light' | 'dark' | 'islamic';
}

interface UserProfileContextType {
  userProfile: UserProfile | null;
  loading: boolean;
  error: Error | null;
}

const UserProfileContext = createContext<UserProfileContextType>({
  userProfile: null,
  loading: true,
  error: null,
});

export const UserProfileProvider: React.FC<{ children: ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  const [userProfile, setUserProfile] = useState<UserProfile | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<Error | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchProfile = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await axios.get('/api/users/profile');
        setUserProfile(response.data);
        setLoading(false);
      } catch (err) {
        setError(err as Error);
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };
    fetchProfile();
  }, []);

  return (
    <UserProfileContext.Provider value={{ userProfile, loading, error }}>
      {children}
    </UserProfileContext.Provider>
  );
};

export const useUserProfile = () => useContext(UserProfileContext);

4. Frontend Components

src/components/GuidanceAvatar.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';
import { Howl } from 'howler';

interface GuidanceAvatarProps {
  user: {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    gender: 'male' | 'female';
    learningLevel: 'beginner' | 'intermediate' | 'advanced';
  };
}

const GuidanceAvatar: React.FC<GuidanceAvatarProps> = ({ user }) => {
  const [mood, setMood] = useState<string>('neutral');
  const [responseText, setResponseText] = useState<string>('');

  useEffect(() => {
    // Initial greeting from Avatar (optional)
    const greeting = `Hello ${user.name}, I'm here to guide you!`;
    setResponseText(greeting);
    playText(greeting);
  }, [user]);

  const playText = (text: string) => {
    // Simple TTS using Web Speech API
    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
    window.speechSynthesis.speak(utterance);
  };

  const sendTextQuery = async (message: string) => {
    try {
      const { data } = await axios.post('/api/assistant/interact', {
        userId: user.id,
        message,
      });
      setResponseText(data.text);
      playText(data.text);
      if (data.mood) setMood(data.mood);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Avatar error:', err);
    }
  };

  const handleSpeechInput = () => {
    // Start STT recognition
    const recognition = new (window.SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition)();
    recognition.lang = 'en-US';
    recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {
      const spoken = event.results[0][0].transcript;
      sendTextQuery(spoken);
    };
    recognition.start();
  };

  const avatarImage = () => {
    // Dynamically pick avatar image based on user gender & mood
    if (user.gender === 'female') {
      return mood === 'positive' ? '/avatars/female_happy.png' : '/avatars/female_neutral.png';
    }
    return mood === 'positive' ? '/avatars/male_happy.png' : '/avatars/male_neutral.png';
  };

  return (
    <div className="text-center space-y-4">
      <img
        src={avatarImage()}
        alt={`${user.name} Avatar`}
        className="w-32 h-32 rounded-full border-4"
        style={{ borderColor: 'var(--avatar-border)' }}
      />
      <div className="space-y-2">
        <button
          onClick={handleSpeechInput}
          className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-600"
        >
          🎤 Speak to Avatar
        </button>
      </div>
      <p className="italic">{responseText}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

export default GuidanceAvatar;




src/components/UserDashboard.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface UserDashboardProps {
  userId: string;
}

interface Activity {
  id: number;
  action: string;
  timestamp: string;
}

const UserDashboard: React.FC<UserDashboardProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [progress, setProgress] = useState<number>(0);
  const [recentActivity, setRecentActivity] = useState<Activity[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchData = async () => {
      try {
        const { data: profile } = await axios.get('/api/users/profile');
        setProgress(profile.progress);
        const { data: path } = await axios.get('/api/users/learning-path');
        // path would be used to render steps if needed
        // Simulate recent activity:
        setRecentActivity([
          { id: 1, action: 'Completed Surah Al-Fatiha recitation', timestamp: '2 hours ago' },
          { id: 2, action: 'Joined Quran competition', timestamp: '1 day ago' },
          { id: 3, action: 'Memorized 5 new verses', timestamp: '3 days ago' },
        ]);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Failed to fetch dashboard data:', err);
      }
    };
    fetchData();
  }, [userId]);

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="mb-6">
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Learning Progress</h3>
        <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-4">
          <div
            className="h-4 rounded-full"
            style={{
              width: `${progress}%`,
              backgroundColor: 'var(--accent-color)',
            }}
          ></div>
        </div>
        <p className="mt-1 text-right">{progress}% completed</p>
      </div>

      <div>
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Recent Activity</h3>
        <ul className="space-y-2">
          {recentActivity.map((activity) => (
            <li key={activity.id} className="flex justify-between border-b pb-2">
              <span>{activity.action}</span>
              <span className="text-gray-500">{activity.timestamp}</span>
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default UserDashboard;




src/components/SwarmInsights.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface SwarmInsightsProps {
  userId: string;
}

interface Insight {
  userId: string;
  collectiveInsights: number;
}

const SwarmInsights: React.FC<SwarmInsightsProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [insights, setInsights] = useState<Insight[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchInsights = async () => {
      try {
        const { data } = await axios.get('/api/swarm/insights');
        setInsights(data);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Failed to fetch swarm insights:', err);
      }
    };
    fetchInsights();
  }, [userId]);

  return (
    <div>
      <ul className="space-y-2">
        {insights.map((insight, idx) => (
          <li key={idx} className="flex justify-between">
            <span>User {insight.userId}</span>
            <span className="text-blue-600">{insight.collectiveInsights.toFixed(2)}</span>
          </li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
};

export default SwarmInsights;




src/components/VoiceCommand.tsx

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface VoiceCommandProps {
  userId: string;
}

export const VoiceCommand: React.FC<VoiceCommandProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [command, setCommand] = useState<string>('');
  const [response, setResponse] = useState<string>('');

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    try {
      const { data } = await axios.post('/api/assistant/interact', {
        userId,
        message: command,
      });
      setResponse(data.text);
      speechSynthesis.speak(new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(data.text));
      setCommand('');
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Failed to send voice command:', err);
    }
  };

  const startSpeechRecognition = () => {
    const recognition = new (window.SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition)();
    recognition.lang = 'en-US';
    recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {
      const spoken = event.results[0][0].transcript;
      setCommand(spoken);
    };
    recognition.start();
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="flex space-x-2">
        <input
          type="text"
          value={command}
          onChange={(e) => setCommand(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Type or speak a command..."
          className="flex-1 border rounded-lg px-4 py-2"
        />
        <button
          type="submit"
          className="px-4 py-2 bg-green-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-green-600"
        >
          Send
        </button>
      </form>
      <button
        onClick={startSpeechRecognition}
        className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-600"
      >
        🎤 Speak
      </button>
      {response && (
        <div className="mt-2 p-4 bg-gray-100 rounded-lg">
          <p className="italic">Avatar: {response}</p>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

1. Services (src/services)

aiAgentService.ts

Coordinates AI agent logic

Fetches/stores AgentModel

Leverages swarm data to generate real-time suggestions

guidanceAssistantService.ts

Accepts text queries or voice transcripts

Sends to GPT-4 for guidance; returns text + optional TTS audio

NEW: Integrates Hugging Face “Open Computer” Agent for UI navigation commands

Exposes processUICommand(userId, command: string) which:

Calls HF “Open Computer” endpoint to interpret UI-intent

Returns a structured action (e.g., { action: 'navigate', target: '/settings' })

Frontend consumes that to adjust routing / UI

swarmIntelligenceService.ts

Analyzes collective user behavior

Uses Ant Colony or Particle Swarm to generate group insights

Updates SwarmModel in MongoDB; caches in Redis

userProfileService.ts

CRUD operations on UserProfileModel

Manages preferences: theme, accessibility, avatar settings, HF agent preferences

Generates personalized learning path

aiCore.service.ts

Central AI pipeline orchestrator

Loads TensorFlow.js/PyTorch models for feedback, RL, clustering

Routes telemetry (recitations, quizzes, emotion) into ML models; returns adjustments

feedback.service.ts

Receives feedback events (session quizzes, recitations)

Logs into FeedbackModel

Emits to Kafka feedback topic for downstream AI processing

huggingFaceService.ts (new)

import axios from 'axios';

const HF_API_URL = 'https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/openai-computer-agent';
const HF_API_TOKEN = process.env.HF_API_TOKEN!;

export const interpretUICommand = async (command: string) => {
  const response = await axios.post(
    HF_API_URL,
    { inputs: command },
    { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${HF_API_TOKEN}` } }
  );
  // Assume HF returns something like: { action: 'navigate', target: '/settings' }
  return response.data;
};

3. Middleware (src/middleware/authMiddleware.ts)

import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';

export const authMiddleware = (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {
  const token = req.headers.authorization?.split(' ')[1];
  if (!token) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Access token missing' });
  }
  try {
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET as string) as any;
    req.body.userId = decoded.sub; // Attach userId for downstream usage
    next();
  } catch (err) {
    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Invalid token' });
  }
};

import express from 'express';
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import bodyParser from 'body-parser';
import userRoutes from './routes/userRoutes';
import swarmRoutes from './routes/swarmRoutes';
import feedbackRoutes from './routes/feedbackRoutes';
import agentRoutes from './routes/agentRoutes';
import assistantRoutes from './routes/assistantRoutes';

dotenv.config();

const app = express();
app.use(bodyParser.json());

app.use('/api/users', userRoutes);
app.use('/api/swarm', swarmRoutes);
app.use('/api/feedback', feedbackRoutes);

// Health check
app.get('/health', (req, res) => res.send('OK'));

export default app;




6. Server Entry (src/server.ts)

import mongoose from 'mongoose';
import Redis from 'ioredis';
import { Kafka } from 'kafkajs';
import app from './app';

const PORT = process.env.PORT || 5000;

// Initialize Redis
export const redisClient = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL!);

// Initialize Kafka
export const kafka = new Kafka({ clientId: 'quran-platform', brokers: [process.env.KAFKA_BROKER!] });

// Connect to MongoDB
mongoose
  .connect(process.env.MONGODB_URI!, { useNewUrlParser: true, useUnifiedTopology: true })
  .then(() => console.log('MongoDB connected'))
  .catch((err) => console.error('MongoDB connection error:', err));

// Start server only after Redis & Kafka are ready
Promise.all([
  redisClient.ping(),
  kafka.admin().connect()
])
  .then(() => {
    app.listen(PORT, () => {
      console.log(`Server listening on port ${PORT}`);
    });
  })
  .catch((err) => {
    console.error('Failed to initialize Kafka/Redis:', err);
    process.exit(1);
  });

2. Context: src/context/UserProfileContext.tsx

import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect, ReactNode } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface UserProfile {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  age: number;
  gender: 'male' | 'female';
  learningLevel: 'beginner' | 'intermediate' | 'advanced';
  themePreference: 'light' | 'dark' | 'islamic';
}

interface UserProfileContextType {
  userProfile: UserProfile | null;
  loading: boolean;
  error: Error | null;
}

const UserProfileContext = createContext<UserProfileContextType>({
  userProfile: null,
  loading: true,
  error: null,
});

export const UserProfileProvider: React.FC<{ children: ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  const [userProfile, setUserProfile] = useState<UserProfile | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<Error | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchProfile = async () => {
      try {
        const { data } = await axios.get('/api/users/profile');
        setUserProfile(data);
        setLoading(false);
      } catch (err) {
        setError(err as Error);
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };
    fetchProfile();
  }, []);

  return (
    <UserProfileContext.Provider value={{ userProfile, loading, error }}>
      {children}
    </UserProfileContext.Provider>
  );
};

export const useUserProfile = () => useContext(UserProfileContext);

4. Frontend Components

4.1 src/components/GuidanceAvatar.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface GuidanceAvatarProps {
  user: {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    gender: 'male' | 'female';
    learningLevel: 'beginner' | 'intermediate' | 'advanced';
  };
}

const GuidanceAvatar: React.FC<GuidanceAvatarProps> = ({ user }) => {
  const [mood, setMood] = useState<string>('neutral');
  const [responseText, setResponseText] = useState<string>('');

  useEffect(() => {
    // Initial greeting
    const greeting = `Assalamu Alaikum ${user.name}, I'm ready to assist you hands-free.`;
    setResponseText(greeting);
    playText(greeting);
  }, [user]);

  const playText = (text: string) => {
    const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
    window.speechSynthesis.speak(utterance);
  };

  const sendTextQuery = async (message: string) => {
    try {
      // First check if it’s a UI command (e.g., “go to settings”)
      const uiAction = await axios.post('/api/assistant/ui-command', { command: message, userId: user.id });
      if (uiAction.data.action === 'navigate') {
        window.location.href = uiAction.data.target; // e.g., '/settings'
        return;
      }

      // Otherwise, treat as normal guidance query
      const { data } = await axios.post('/api/assistant/interact', {
        userId: user.id,
        message,
      });
      setResponseText(data.text);
      playText(data.text);
      if (data.mood) setMood(data.mood);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Guidance Avatar error:', err);
    }
  };

  const handleSpeechInput = () => {
    const recognition = new (window.SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition)();
    recognition.lang = 'en-US';
    recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {
      const spoken = event.results[0][0].transcript;
      sendTextQuery(spoken);
    };
    recognition.start();
  };

  const avatarImage = () => {
    if (user.gender === 'female') {
      return mood === 'positive' ? '/avatars/female_happy.png' : '/avatars/female_neutral.png';
    }
    return mood === 'positive' ? '/avatars/male_happy.png' : '/avatars/male_neutral.png';
  };

  return (
    <div className="text-center space-y-4">
      <img
        src={avatarImage()}
        alt={`${user.name} Avatar`}
        className="w-32 h-32 rounded-full border-4"
        style={{ borderColor: 'var(--avatar-border)' }}
      />
      <button
        onClick={handleSpeechInput}
        className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-600"
      >
        🎤 Speak
      </button>
      <p className="italic">{responseText}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

export default GuidanceAvatar;




4.2 src/components/UserDashboard.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface UserDashboardProps {
  userId: string;
}

interface Activity {
  id: number;
  action: string;
  timestamp: string;
}

const UserDashboard: React.FC<UserDashboardProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [progress, setProgress] = useState<number>(0);
  const [recentActivity, setRecentActivity] = useState<Activity[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchData = async () => {
      try {
        const { data: profile } = await axios.get('/api/users/profile');
        setProgress(profile.progress);
        const { data: path } = await axios.get('/api/users/learning-path');
        // Use `path` if needed for detailed UI; here we simulate recent activity
        setRecentActivity([
          { id: 1, action: 'Completed Surah Al-Fatiha recitation', timestamp: '2 hours ago' },
          { id: 2, action: 'Joined Quran competition', timestamp: '1 day ago' },
          { id: 3, action: 'Memorized 5 new verses', timestamp: '3 days ago' },
        ]);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Failed to fetch dashboard data:', err);
      }
    };
    fetchData();
  }, [userId]);

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="mb-6">
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Learning Progress</h3>
        <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-4">
          <div
            className="h-4 rounded-full"
            style={{
              width: `${progress}%`,
              backgroundColor: 'var(--accent-color)',
            }}
          ></div>
        </div>
        <p className="mt-1 text-right">{progress}% completed</p>
      </div>

      <div>
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-2">Recent Activity</h3>
        <ul className="space-y-2">
          {recentActivity.map((activity) => (
            <li key={activity.id} className="flex justify-between border-b pb-2">
              <span>{activity.action}</span>
              <span className="text-gray-500">{activity.timestamp}</span>
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default UserDashboard;

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface SwarmInsightsProps {
  userId: string;
}

interface Insight {
  userId: string;
  collectiveInsights: number;
}

const SwarmInsights: React.FC<SwarmInsightsProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [insights, setInsights] = useState<Insight[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchInsights = async () => {
      try {
        const { data } = await axios.get('/api/swarm/insights');
        setInsights(data);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Failed to fetch swarm insights:', err);
      }
    };
    fetchInsights();
  }, [userId]);

  return (
    <div>
      <ul className="space-y-2">
        {insights.map((insight, idx) => (
          <li key={idx} className="flex justify-between">
            <span>User {insight.userId}</span>
            <span className="text-blue-600">{insight.collectiveInsights.toFixed(2)}</span>
          </li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
};

4.4 src/components/VoiceCommand.tsx

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import axios from 'axios';

interface VoiceCommandProps {
  userId: string;
}

export const VoiceCommand: React.FC<VoiceCommandProps> = ({ userId }) => {
  const [command, setCommand] = useState<string>('');
  const [response, setResponse] = useState<string>('');

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    try {
      const { data } = await axios.post('/api/assistant/interact', {
        userId,
        message: command,
      });
      setResponse(data.text);
      speechSynthesis.speak(new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(data.text));
      setCommand('');
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Failed to send voice command:', err);
    }
  };

  const startSpeechRecognition = () => {
    const recognition = new (window.SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition)();
    recognition.lang = 'en-US';
    recognition.onresult = (event: any) => {
      const spoken = event.results[0][0].transcript;
      setCommand(spoken);
    };
    recognition.start();
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="flex space-x-2">
        <input
          type="text"
          value={command}
          onChange={(e) => setCommand(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="Command or question..."
          className="flex-1 border rounded-lg px-4 py-2"
        />
        <button
          type="submit"
          className="px-4 py-2 bg-green-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-green-600"
        >
          Send
        </button>
      </form>
      <button
        onClick={startSpeechRecognition}
        className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-600"
      >
        🎤 Speak
      </button>
      {response && (
        <div className="mt-2 p-4 bg-gray-100 rounded-lg">
          <p className="italic">Avatar: {response}</p>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

✅ Phase 14 complete. Jules — please merge to main, deploy to dev, and verify everything end-to-end. Phase 14: AI Agents, Guidance Assistant, and Swarm Intelligence Hub

Title:

Phase 14: Core AI Intelligence Hub

Objective:

The objective of Phase 14 is to develop a comprehensive, centralized AI-driven system capable of integrating AI/ML models, AI agents, guidance assistants, and swarm intelligence for personalized learning experiences. This phase will facilitate deep user interaction, guide personalized learning paths, provide real-time feedback, and enhance the overall platform by utilizing data across all phases, incorporating reinforcement learning, real-time AI analysis, and advanced voice and avatar-based interaction.

Key Features:

AI-Driven Agents: AI agents monitor user behavior, performance, and preferences, making personalized learning suggestions in real-time.

Guidance Assistant with Voice & Avatar: An intelligent assistant that communicates with users using voice recognition and visual avatars. It helps with navigation, user guidance, and managing platform preferences.

Swarm Intelligence: A system that uses collective data from all users to predict behavior and improve learning outcomes, offering highly accurate personalized feedback.

Personalized User Dashboards: Dashboards will dynamically change based on user profiles, learning progress, and AI-driven suggestions.

Real-Time Feedback: Users will receive real-time insights and recommendations based on ongoing analysis of their learning progress, behavior patterns, and engagement.

Cross-Phase Data Integration: Data from all platform phases (Recitation, Competitions, Memorization, Learning, Teaching, Video Conferencing, VR/AR) will be integrated to refine and personalize the learning experience.

const agentSchema = new Schema({ userId: { type: String, required: true }, behaviorHistory: { type: [Schema.Types.Mixed], default: [] }, preferences: { type: Object, default: {} }, lastInteraction: { type: Date, default: Date.now }, learningSuggestions: { type: [String], default: [] }, });

services/aiAgentService.ts

typescript

Copy code

import { AgentModel } from '../models/agentModel'; import { UserProfileModel } from '../models/userProfileModel'; import { SwarmModel } from '../models/swarmModel';

class AIAgentService { // Process agent-based logic for user learning guidance static async processUserBehavior(userId: string) { const agent = await AgentModel.findOne({ userId }); const userProfile = await UserProfileModel.findOne({ userId }); const swarmInsights = await SwarmModel.findOne({ userId });

if (!agent || !userProfile || !swarmInsights) {
  throw new Error('User data not found for AI processing.');
}

// Analyze user behavior using swarm intelligence data
const behaviorAnalysis = this.analyzeBehavior(agent, userProfile, swarmInsights);
const learningSuggestions = this.generateLearningSuggestions(behaviorAnalysis);

// Update agent profile with the new suggestions
agent.learningSuggestions = learningSuggestions;
await agent.save();

return { behaviorAnalysis, learningSuggestions };


}

// Analyze behavior based on various factors (historical data, engagement, etc.) static analyzeBehavior(agent, userProfile, swarmInsights) { // Complex logic for behavior analysis return { behaviorScore: agent.behaviorHistory.length, progressScore: userProfile.progress, swarmScore: swarmInsights.collectiveInsights, }; }

// Generate learning suggestions based on analysis static generateLearningSuggestions(analysis) { const suggestions = []; if (analysis.behaviorScore < 5) { suggestions.push('Practice recitation more frequently.'); } if (analysis.progressScore < 0.7) { suggestions.push('Consider enrolling in more interactive sessions.'); } if (analysis.swarmScore > 0.8) { suggestions.push('You are progressing well! Keep up the great work.'); } return suggestions; } }

export { AIAgentService };

services/guidanceAssistantService.ts

import { GuidanceAssistant } from '../models/guidanceAssistantModel'; // Assuming the model exists import { SpeechRecognition } from 'speech-to-text-api'; // External library for voice input

class GuidanceAssistantService { // Process user interaction with the guidance assistant static async processInteraction(userId: string, message: string) { const assistant = await GuidanceAssistant.findOne({ userId });

if (!assistant) {
  throw new Error('No guidance assistant found for user.');
}

// Process the message (may include NLP or AI-driven responses)
const response = await this.analyzeMessage(message);

return response;


}

// Analyze the user's message (could be expanded with NLP or intent recognition) static analyzeMessage(message: string) { if (message.includes('help')) { return { text: 'How can I assist you today?', voice: 'help-response.mp3' }; } return { text: 'Sorry, I did not understand that. Could you please clarify?', voice: 'error-response.mp3' }; }

// Additional method to handle voice commands using speech recognition static async handleVoiceCommand(userId: string, voiceInput: string) { const textInput = await SpeechRecognition.convertSpeechToText(voiceInput); return this.processInteraction(userId, textInput); } }

export { GuidanceAssistantService };

services/swarmIntelligenceService.ts

typescript

Copy code

import { SwarmModel } from '../models/swarmModel'; import { UserProfileModel } from '../models/userProfileModel';

class SwarmIntelligenceService { // Get collective intelligence data to influence personalized learning static async getInsights() { const swarmData = await SwarmModel.find(); const insights = swarmData.map(data => this.calculateInsights(data));

return insights;


}

// Analyze and calculate insights based on swarm data static calculateInsights(swarmData) { // Complex algorithm based on the swarm's behavior and insights return { insight: 'Recommendation based on collective data.', prediction: this.predictOutcome(swarmData), }; }

// Predict learning outcomes based on swarm collective intelligence static predictOutcome(swarmData) { const collectivePattern = swarmData.behaviorData.map(item => item.score); const averageScore = collectivePattern.reduce((acc, score) => acc + score, 0) / collectivePattern.length; return averageScore > 0.75 ? 'Positive' : 'Needs improvement'; } }

export { SwarmIntelligenceService };

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

interface AvatarProps { userId: string; }

const Avatar: React.FC = ({ userId }) => { const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(true);

// Logic to handle visibility and interactions for the avatar const toggleVisibility = () => { setIsVisible(!isVisible); };

useEffect(() => { // Keep the avatar visible as long as the user is navigating const handleVisibility = () => { setIsVisible(true); };

// Listen for navigation or page change
window.addEventListener('popstate', handleVisibility);

return () => {
  window.removeEventListener('popstate', handleVisibility);
};


}, []);

return ( isVisible && ( <div style={{ position: 'fixed', bottom: '20px', right: '20px' }}> <div onClick={toggleVisibility} style={{ cursor: 'pointer' }}>

Hi, how can I assist you?

) ); };

export default Avatar;
